*Calvin's Commentaries, Vol. 12: Psalms, Part V*, tr. by John King,
\[1847-50\], at Intangible Textual Heritage

<span id="xxxv"></span>

<span id="xxxv-p1"></span>A NEW TRANSLATION OF

<span id="xxxv-p2"></span>THE BOOK OF PSALMS.

<span id="xxxv.i"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i-p2"></span>PSALMS 1—35

<span id="xxxv.i-p3"></span>PART FIRST.  <span
id="fr_311"></span>[312](#fn_311)

<span id="xxxv.i.i"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i.i-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i.i-p2"></span>PSALM 1

<span id="xxxv.i.i-p3"></span>**1** Blessed *is* the man who walketh not
in the counsel of the ungodly; And in the way of sinners doth not stand;
And in the seat of scoffers doth not sit:

<span id="xxxv.i.i-p4"></span>**2** But in the law of the Lord *is* his
delight; And in his law doth he meditate day and night.

<span id="xxxv.i.i-p5"></span>**3** He shall be like a tree planted near
rivers of waters, Which shall yield its fruit in its season, And whose
leaf shall not fade; And all that he doeth shall prosper.

<span id="xxxv.i.i-p6"></span>**4** Not so the ungodly: But they are
like the chaff, which scatter doth the wind.

<span id="xxxv.i.i-p7"></span>**5** Therefore shall not stand the
ungodly in the judgment, Nor sinners in the assembly of the righteous.

<span id="xxxv.i.i-p8"></span>**6** For know doth Jehovah the way of the
righteous; But the way of the ungodly shall perish.

<span id="xxxv.i.ii"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i.ii-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i.ii-p2"></span>PSALM 2

<span id="xxxv.i.ii-p3"></span>**1** Why tumultuously rise do the
Gentiles, And the peoples murmur in vain?

<span id="xxxv.i.ii-p4"></span>**2** Confederated have the kings of the
earth, And the princes have assembled together, Against Jehovah and
against his Christ.

<span id="xxxv.i.ii-p5"></span>**3** “Let us break asunder their bonds,
“And cast away from us their yoke.”

<span id="xxxv.i.ii-p6"></span>**4** He who dwelleth in heaven shall
laugh; The Lord shall deride them.

<span id="xxxv.i.ii-p7"></span>**5** Then shall he speak to them in his
wrath, And in his hot displeasure he shall vex them.

<span id="xxxv.i.ii-p8"></span>**6** “I have anointed my king, “Upon
Zion, the mountain of my holiness.”

<span id="xxxv.i.ii-p9"></span>**7** I will declare the decree: Jehovah
hath said to me, “My Son art thou; I, this day, have begotten thee.

<span id="xxxv.i.ii-p10"></span>**8** “Ask of me, and I will give thee
the Gentiles for thy inheritance, “And for thy possession the uttermost
parts of the earth.

<span id="xxxv.i.ii-p11"></span>**9** “Thou shalt break them with a rod
of iron;” As the vessel of a potter thou shalt dash them in pieces.”

<span id="xxxv.i.ii-p12"></span>**10** And now, O ye kings! understand;
Be instructed, O ye judges of the earth!

<span id="xxxv.i.ii-p13"></span>**11** Serve Jehovah with fear, Rejoice
with trembling.

<span id="xxxv.i.ii-p14"></span>**12** Kiss the Son, lest he be angry,
And ye perish from the way, When shall be kindled in a short time his
wrath. Blessed are all who trust in him.

<span id="xxxv.i.iii"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i.iii-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i.iii-p2"></span>PSALM 3

<span id="xxxv.i.iii-p3"></span>A Psalm of David, when he fled from the
face of Absalom his son

<span id="xxxv.i.iii-p4"></span>**1** O Lord! how are my oppressors
multiplied! Many rise up against me,

<span id="xxxv.i.iii-p5"></span>**2** Many say to my soul, “There is no
help for him in God.” Selah.

<span id="xxxv.i.iii-p6"></span>**3** And thou, O Jehovah! art a shield
for me; My glory, and he that exalteth my head.

<span id="xxxv.i.iii-p7"></span>**4** With my voice to the Lord have I
cried, And he heard me from the mountain of his holiness. Selah.

<span id="xxxv.i.iii-p8"></span>**5** I lay down and slept; I awaked,
because the Lord sustains me.

<span id="xxxv.i.iii-p9"></span>**6** I will not be afraid of ten
thousands of people, Who on all sides have set their camps against me.

<span id="xxxv.i.iii-p10"></span>**7** Arise, O Lord l Save me, O my
God! For thou hast smitten all my enemies upon the cheekbone; The teeth
of the ungodly thou hast broken.

<span id="xxxv.i.iii-p11"></span>**8** To the Lord belongeth salvation;
Upon thy people *is* thy blessing. Selah.

<span id="xxxv.i.iv"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i.iv-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i.iv-p2"></span>PSALM 4

<span id="xxxv.i.iv-p3"></span>To the Chief Musician on Neginoth. A
Psalm of David

<span id="xxxv.i.iv-p4"></span>**1** When I cry, answer me, O God of my
righteousness! In distress thou hast enlarged me; Have pity upon me, and
hear my prayer.

<span id="xxxv.i.iv-p5"></span>**2** O ye sons of men! how long my glory
will ye try to put to shame? Will ye love vanity, will ye seek after
lying? Selah.

<span id="xxxv.i.iv-p6"></span>**3** But know that chosen hath Jehovah
the merciful man for himself: Jehovah will hear when I cry unto him.

<span id="xxxv.i.iv-p7"></span>**4** Tremble and ye shall not sin;
Discourse in your heart upon your bed, and be silent. Selah.

<span id="xxxv.i.iv-p8"></span>**5** Sacrifice the sacrifices of
righteousness, And trust in the Lord.

<span id="xxxv.i.iv-p9"></span>**6** Many say, “Who will show us good?”
Lift thou up on us the light of thy countenance, O Jehovah!

<span id="xxxv.i.iv-p10"></span>**7** Thou hast given joy to my heart
More than *theirs* in the time that their corn and their wine are
increased.

<span id="xxxv.i.iv-p11"></span>**8** In peace \[*as if*\] with a
multitude I will sleep and take rest,  <span
id="fr_312"></span>[313](#fn_312) For thou, O Jehovah! in safety hast
placed me, \[*though*\] alone.

<span id="xxxv.i.v"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i.v-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i.v-p2"></span>PSALM 5

<span id="xxxv.i.v-p3"></span>To the Chief. Musician upon Nehiloth. A
Psalm of David

<span id="xxxv.i.v-p4"></span>**1** My words do thou give ear to, O
Jehovah! Attend to my speech.

<span id="xxxv.i.v-p5"></span>**2** Hearken to the voice of my cry, my
King and my God! For to thee will I pray.

<span id="xxxv.i.v-p6"></span>**3** O Jehovah! in the morning do thou
hear my voice; In the morning will I direct to thee and will watch.

<span id="xxxv.i.v-p7"></span>**4** For not a God taking pleasure in
wickedness art thou; There shall not dwell with thee evil.

<span id="xxxv.i.v-p8"></span>**5** There shall not stand the foolish
before thine eyes; Thou hatest all that commit iniquity.

<span id="xxxv.i.v-p9"></span>**6** Thou shalt destroy them that speak
falsehood: The man of bloods and the deceitful man abominate shall
Jehovah.

<span id="xxxv.i.v-p10"></span>**7** And I, in the multitude of thy
mercy, will enter into thy house; I will worship in thy holy temple in
thy fear.

<span id="xxxv.i.v-p11"></span>**8** O Jehovah! lead me in thy
righteousness, because of my adversaries; Make straight before my face
thy way.

<span id="xxxv.i.v-p12"></span>**9** For there is not in their mouth
uprightness; Their inward part is deep depravity; A sepulcher that is
open is their throat; With their tongues they deal deceitfully.

<span id="xxxv.i.v-p13"></span>**10** Cause them to err, O God! Let them
fall from their counsels; In the multitude of their transgressions
destroy them; For they have rebelled against thee.

<span id="xxxv.i.v-p14"></span>**11** And rejoice let all those who
trust in thee, For ever let them exult; and cover thou them, And let
those delight in thee that love thy name.

<span id="xxxv.i.v-p15"></span>**12** For thou shalt bless the
righteous, O Jehovah! With thy good will as with a shield thou shalt
encompass them.

<span id="xxxv.i.vi"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i.vi-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i.vi-p2"></span>PSALM 6

<span id="xxxv.i.vi-p3"></span>To the Chief Musician on Neginoth, upon
the Eighth. A Psalm of David

<span id="xxxv.i.vi-p4"></span>**1** O Jehovah! do not in thy anger
rebuke me, And do not in thy wrath chastise me.

<span id="xxxv.i.vi-p5"></span>**2** Have mercy upon me, O Jehovah! for
I am weak; Heal me, O Jehovah! for affrighted are my bones.

<span id="xxxv.i.vi-p6"></span>**3** And my soul is exceedingly afraid:
And thou, O Jehovah! — how long? —

<span id="xxxv.i.vi-p7"></span>**4** Return, O Lord! deliver my soul;
Save me for the sake of thy mercy.

<span id="xxxv.i.vi-p8"></span>**5** For there is not in death any
remembrance of thee; In the grave who shall acknowledge thee?

<span id="xxxv.i.vi-p9"></span>**6** I have become wearied with my
groaning; I make to swim every night my bed; With my tears my couch I
water.

<span id="xxxv.i.vi-p10"></span>**7** Waxed dim for vexation hath mine
eye; It hath become old among all my persecutors.

<span id="xxxv.i.vi-p11"></span>**8** Depart from me, all ye workers of
iniquity; For heard hath the Lord the voice of my weeping.

<span id="xxxv.i.vi-p12"></span>**9** Heard hath the Lord my
supplication; The Lord my prayer will receive.

<span id="xxxv.i.vi-p13"></span>**10** Put to shame and confounded
greatly be all my enemies; Let them turn back, and be ashamed suddenly.

<span id="xxxv.i.vii"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i.vii-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i.vii-p2"></span>PSALM 7

<span id="xxxv.i.vii-p3"></span>Shiggaion of David, which he sung to
Jehovah, upon the words  
of Cush the Benjamite

<span id="xxxv.i.vii-p4"></span>**1** O Jehovah, my God! in thee do I
trust: Save me from all them that persecute me, and deliver me:

<span id="xxxv.i.vii-p5"></span>**2** Lest He seize, as a lion, upon my
soul, And tear it in pieces while there is none to deliver it.

<span id="xxxv.i.vii-p6"></span>**3** O Jehovah, my God! if I have done
this, If there be iniquity in my hands,

<span id="xxxv.i.vii-p7"></span>**4** If I have rewarded to him that was
at peace with me evil, And have not delivered him that afflicted me
without cause;

<span id="xxxv.i.vii-p8"></span>**5** Pursue let the enemy my soul and
take it, And let him cast down to the earth my life, And my glory in the
dust let him hold down. Selah

<span id="xxxv.i.vii-p9"></span>**6** Arise, O Jehovah! in thy anger;
Lift up thyself against the fury of my enemies; And awake thou for me to
the judgment which thou hast ordained.

<span id="xxxv.i.vii-p10"></span>**7** And the congregation of peoples
shall be round about thee: And on account of this, do thou on high
return.

<span id="xxxv.i.vii-p11"></span>**8** Jehovah shall judge the peoples:
Judge me, O Jehovah! according to my righteousness, And according to the
integrity which is in me.

<span id="xxxv.i.vii-p12"></span>**9** Let come to an end, I pray, the
malice of the wicked; And direct thou the righteous man: For he proves
the hearts and the reins, the righteous God.

<span id="xxxv.i.vii-p13"></span>**10** My shield is in God, Who saves
the upright in heart.

<span id="xxxv.i.vii-p14"></span>**11** God judgeth the righteous man,
And him who despiseth God, daily.

<span id="xxxv.i.vii-p15"></span>**12** If he turn not, his sword he
will whet; His bow he hath bent, he hath made it ready.

<span id="xxxv.i.vii-p16"></span>**13** And for it he hath prepared the
instruments of death; He shall make fit his arrows for the persecutors.

<span id="xxxv.i.vii-p17"></span>**14** Behold! he shall travail to
bring forth iniquity, And he hath conceived wickedness, And he shall
bring forth falsehood.

<span id="xxxv.i.vii-p18"></span>**15** A pit he hath digged, and
hollowed it out; And he hath fallen into the ditch which he hath made.

<span id="xxxv.i.vii-p19"></span>**16** Return shall his wickedness upon
his own head, And upon his own crown his violence shall descend.

<span id="xxxv.i.vii-p20"></span>**17** I will praise Jehovah, according
to his righteousness; And I will sing to the name of Jehovah, Most High.

<span id="xxxv.i.viii"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i.viii-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i.viii-p2"></span>PSALM 8

<span id="xxxv.i.viii-p3"></span>To the chief Musician upon Hagittith. A
Psalm of David

<span id="xxxv.i.viii-p4"></span>**1** O Jehovah, our Lord! How
wonderful is thy name in all the earth, To set thy glory above the
heavens!

<span id="xxxv.i.viii-p5"></span>**2** Out of the mouths of babes and
sucklings Thou hast founded *thy* strength, because of thy adversaries,
To put to flight the enemy and the avenger.

<span id="xxxv.i.viii-p6"></span>**3** When! see thy heavens, the works
of thy fingers; The moon and the stars which thou hast arranged:

<span id="xxxv.i.viii-p7"></span>**4** What is man that thou art mindful
of him? And the son of man, that thou visitest him?

<span id="xxxv.i.viii-p8"></span>**5** For thou hast made him lower a
little than God, And with glory and honor thou hast crowned him.

<span id="xxxv.i.viii-p9"></span>**6** Thou hast set him over the works
of thy hands: All things thou hast put under his feet.

<span id="xxxv.i.viii-p10"></span>**7** Sheep and oxen, all of them, And
also the beasts of the fields;

<span id="xxxv.i.viii-p11"></span>**8** The fowl of the heavens, and the
fish of the sea, And whatsoever passeth through the paths of the seas.

<span id="xxxv.i.viii-p12"></span>**9** O Jehovah, our Lord! How
wonderful is thy name in all the earth!

<span id="xxxv.i.ix"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i.ix-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i.ix-p2"></span>PSALM 9

<span id="xxxv.i.ix-p3"></span>To the chief Musician upon Hagittith.
Almuth Laben. A Psalm of David

<span id="xxxv.i.ix-p4"></span>**1** I will praise Jehovah with my whole
heart; will recount all thy marvelous works.

<span id="xxxv.i.ix-p5"></span>**2** I will rejoice and exult in thee; I
will celebrate in Psalms thy name, O thou Most high!

<span id="xxxv.i.ix-p6"></span>**3** When turned are my enemies
backward, They fall and are put to flight at thy presence.

<span id="xxxv.i.ix-p7"></span>**4** For thou hast maintained my
judgment and my cause; Thou hast sat upon the throne a righteous judge.

<span id="xxxv.i.ix-p8"></span>**5** Thou hast rebuked the heathen; Thou
hast destroyed the ungodly; Their name thou hast blotted out for ever
and ever.

<span id="xxxv.i.ix-p9"></span>**6** O thou enemy! come to an end are
desolations for ever; And cities thou hast destroyed; Perished has their
memory with them.

<span id="xxxv.i.ix-p10"></span>**7** And Jehovah for ever sitteth: His
throne for judgment lie hath prepared.

<span id="xxxv.i.ix-p11"></span>**8** And he shall judge the world in
righteousness; He shall judge the peoples in rectitude.

<span id="xxxv.i.ix-p12"></span>**9** And Jehovah will be a place of
defense to the poor, And a protection in seasonable times in trouble.

<span id="xxxv.i.ix-p13"></span>**10** And trust in thee shall those who
know thy name: For thou forsakest not those who seek thee, O Jehovah!

<span id="xxxv.i.ix-p14"></span>**11** Sing psalms to Jehovah, who
dwelleth in Zion, Proclaim among the peoples his doings;

<span id="xxxv.i.ix-p15"></span>**12** For in requiring blood, it lie
hath remembered: He hath not forgotten the cry of the poor.

<span id="xxxv.i.ix-p16"></span>**13** Have mercy upon me, O Jehovah!
See my affliction from those who persecute me, O thou that liftest me up
from the gates of death;

<span id="xxxv.i.ix-p17"></span>**14** That I may recount all thy
praises in the gates of the daughter of Zion; That I may exult in thy
salvation.

<span id="xxxv.i.ix-p18"></span>**15** Sunk are the heathen into the pit
which they have made; In the net which they have hid taken are their own
feet.

<span id="xxxv.i.ix-p19"></span>**16** Known is Jehovah by executing
judgment: In the work of his own hands the wicked is snared. Higgaion
Selah.

<span id="xxxv.i.ix-p20"></span>**17** Turned shall be the wicked into
hell: All the nations that forget God.

<span id="xxxv.i.ix-p21"></span>**18** For not for ever shall be
forgotten the poor; The hope of the humble shall not perish for ever.

<span id="xxxv.i.ix-p22"></span>**19** Arise, O Jehovah! let not man
prevail: Let the heathen be judged in thy sight.

<span id="xxxv.i.ix-p23"></span>**20** Put, O Jehovah! fear in them,
That the heathen may know that mortal men they are. Selah.

<span id="xxxv.i.x"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i.x-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i.x-p2"></span>PSALM 10

<span id="xxxv.i.x-p3"></span>**1** Why, O Jehovah! standest thou afar
off? And winkest at seasonable times in trouble?

<span id="xxxv.i.x-p4"></span>**2** In his pride the ungodly doth
persecute the poor; Let them be caught in the devices which they
imagine.

<span id="xxxv.i.x-p5"></span>**3** For praise himself doth the ungodly
on account of the desire of his own soul; And the violent man blesseth
himself: He despiseth Jehovah.

<span id="xxxv.i.x-p6"></span>**4** The ungodly, in the pride of his
countenance doth not inquire; All his devices say, “There is not a God.”

<span id="xxxv.i.x-p7"></span>**5** Prosperous are his ways at all
times; High are thy judgments before him; At all his enemies he puffeth.

<span id="xxxv.i.x-p8"></span>**6** He saith in his heart, “I shall not
be moved from generation to generation,” Because he is not in adversity,

<span id="xxxv.i.x-p9"></span>**7** Of cursing his mouth is full, and of
deceit, and of malice: Under his tongue are mischief and iniquity.

<span id="xxxv.i.x-p10"></span>**8** He will sit in the ensnaring places
of the villages; In his lurking places will he murder the innocent: His
eyes against the poor will take their aim.

<span id="xxxv.i.x-p11"></span>**9** He will lie in wait in secret, as a
lion in his den; He will lie in wait to catch the poor; He will catch
the poor by drawing him into his net.

<span id="xxxv.i.x-p12"></span>**10** He will crouch low, he will cast
himself down; Then shall fall by his strengths an army of the afflicted.

<span id="xxxv.i.x-p13"></span>**11** He hath said in his heart,
“Forgotten it hath God; “He hideth his face, that he may not see it for
ever.”

<span id="xxxv.i.x-p14"></span>**12** Arise, O Jehovah, God! lift up thy
hand: Do not forget the poor.

<span id="xxxv.i.x-p15"></span>**13** Why do the wicked despise God? He
saith in his heart, “Thou wilt not require it.”

<span id="xxxv.i.x-p16"></span>**14** Thou hast seen *it*; For mischief
and oppression thou considerest, That thou mayest take them into thy own
hand: Upon thee shall the poor leave; To the orphan thou wilt be an
helper.

<span id="xxxv.i.x-p17"></span>**15** Break thou the arm of the wicked
and the evil man; Thou shalt seek his wickedness, and shalt not find it.

<span id="xxxv.i.x-p18"></span>**16** Jehovah is King for ever and ever;
Perished are the heathen out of his land.

<span id="xxxv.i.x-p19"></span>**17** The desire of the needy thou hast
heard, O Jehovah! Thou wilt direct their heart; Hear shall thine car:

<span id="xxxv.i.x-p20"></span>**18** That thou mayest judge the
fatherless and the poor, That the man *who* is of earth may terrify no
more.

<span id="xxxv.i.xi"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i.xi-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i.xi-p2"></span>PSALM 11

<span id="xxxv.i.xi-p3"></span>To the chief Musician. A Psalm of David

<span id="xxxv.i.xi-p4"></span>**1** In Jehovah do I put my trust: How
then say ye to my soul, “Flee ye into your mountain as a bird?”

<span id="xxxv.i.xi-p5"></span>**2** Surely behold! the ungodly shall
bend the bow, They have made ready their arrows upon the string, shoot
in secret at the upright in heart.

<span id="xxxv.i.xi-p6"></span>**3** Truly, the foundations are
destroyed: The righteous, what hath he done?

<span id="xxxv.i.xi-p7"></span>**4** Jehovah is in the palace of his
holiness; Jehovah in heaven *hath* his throne; His eyes behold, his
eyelids consider the children of men.

<span id="xxxv.i.xi-p8"></span>**5** Jehovah will approve the righteous
man; But the ungodly and him who loveth iniquity, hate doth his soul.

<span id="xxxv.i.xi-p9"></span>**6** He will rain upon the ungodly
snares, Fire and brimstone, and a storm of whirlwinds: This is the
portion of their cup.

<span id="xxxv.i.xi-p10"></span>**7** For the righteous Jehovah loveth
righteousness; His countenance approveth the upright.

<span id="xxxv.i.xii"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i.xii-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i.xii-p2"></span>PSALM 12

<span id="xxxv.i.xii-p3"></span>To the Chief Musician upon the Eighth. A
Psalm of David

<span id="xxxv.i.xii-p4"></span>**1** Save me, O Jehovah! for failed
hath the merciful man, For wasted away are the faithful from among the
children of men.

<span id="xxxv.i.xii-p5"></span>**2** Deceit doth every one speak with
his neighbor; With lips of flatteries, with a double heart do they
speak.

<span id="xxxv.i.xii-p6"></span>**3** Let Jehovah cut off all lips of
flatteries, The tongue that great things doth speak:

<span id="xxxv.i.xii-p7"></span>**4** Those who have said, “By our
tongues we will be strengthened; “Our lips are our own; who is lord over
us?”

<span id="xxxv.i.xii-p8"></span>**5** “Because of the spoiling of the
needy, “Because of the groaning of the poor, “Now will I arise,” say
will Jehovah, “I will set in safety him for whom *the wicked man* layeth
snares.”

<span id="xxxv.i.xii-p9"></span>**6** The words of Jehovah are pure
words; Silver melted in an excellent crucible of earth, purified seven
times.

<span id="xxxv.i.xii-p10"></span>**7** Thou, O Jehovah! wilt keep them;
Thou wilt preserve him from this generation for ever.

<span id="xxxv.i.xii-p11"></span>**8** On every side the ungodly walk;
When they are exalted, reproach is to the children of men.

<span id="xxxv.i.xiii"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i.xiii-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i.xiii-p2"></span>PSALM 13

<span id="xxxv.i.xiii-p3"></span>To the chief Musician. A Psalm of David

<span id="xxxv.i.xiii-p4"></span>**1** How long, O Jehovah! wilt thou
forget me for ever? How long wilt thou hide thy face from me?

<span id="xxxv.i.xiii-p5"></span>**2** How long shall I take counsel in
my soul? And have sorrow in my heart daily? How long exalted shall be my
enemy over me?

<span id="xxxv.i.xiii-p6"></span>**3** Look upon me, answer me, O
Jehovah, my God! Enlighten my eyes, lest I sleep in death;

<span id="xxxv.i.xiii-p7"></span>**4** Lest my enemy say, “I have
prevailed against him;” And those who afflict me rejoice if I should
fall.

<span id="xxxv.i.xiii-p8"></span>**5** But as for me, in thy goodness I
trust; Exult shall my heart in thy salvation. I will sing to the Lord
because he hath dealt bountifully with me.

<span id="xxxv.i.xiv"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i.xiv-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i.xiv-p2"></span>PSALM 14

<span id="xxxv.i.xiv-p3"></span>To the Chief Musician. A Psalm Of David

<span id="xxxv.i.xiv-p4"></span>**1** The fool hath said in his heart,
“There is no God;” They have corrupted \[*all good order*,\] they have
done abominable work. There is none that doeth good.

<span id="xxxv.i.xiv-p5"></span>**2** Jehovah from heaven looked down
Upon the children of men, To see whether there were any that did
understand, And seek after God.

<span id="xxxv.i.xiv-p6"></span>**3** Every one of them hath gone aside,
Together putrid have they become: There is none that doeth good, not
even one.

<span id="xxxv.i.xiv-p7"></span>**4** Have they no knowledge all these
workers of iniquity? Who eat up my people as they eat bread. Upon the
Lord they do not call.

<span id="xxxv.i.xiv-p8"></span>**5** There did they tremble with fear,
For God is in the generation of the righteous.

<span id="xxxv.i.xiv-p9"></span>**6** The counsel of the poor ye deride,
Because Jehovah is his hope.

<span id="xxxv.i.xiv-p10"></span>**7** Who shall give from Zion
salvation to Israel? When turn back shall Jehovah the captivity of his
people, Rejoice shall Jacob, and exult shall Israel.

<span id="xxxv.i.xv"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i.xv-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i.xv-p2"></span>PSALM 15

<span id="xxxv.i.xv-p3"></span>A Psalm of David

<span id="xxxv.i.xv-p4"></span>**1** O Jehovah! who shall dwell in thy
tabernacle? Who shall rest in the mountain of thy holiness?

<span id="xxxv.i.xv-p5"></span>**2** He who walketh in integrity and
doeth righteousness, And who speaketh truth in his heart,

<span id="xxxv.i.xv-p6"></span>**3** He who detracteth not with his
tongue, Who doeth not to his companion evil, And a calumnious report
doth not raise up against his neighbor.

<span id="xxxv.i.xv-p7"></span>**4** Despised in his eyes is the off
cast; But those who fear the Lord he honoreth; When he hath sworn to his
own hurt he doth not change.

<span id="xxxv.i.xv-p8"></span>**5** His money he doth not put out to
usury; And a present upon the innocent he doth not accept: He who doeth
these things shall not be moved for ever.

<span id="xxxv.i.xvi"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i.xvi-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i.xvi-p2"></span>PSALM 16

<span id="xxxv.i.xvi-p3"></span>Michtam. A Psalm Of David

<span id="xxxv.i.xvi-p4"></span>**1** Keep me, O God! *For* in thee do I
trust.

<span id="xxxv.i.xvi-p5"></span>**2** Thou shalt say to Jehovah, “My
Lord thou art; “My well doing *extendeth* not to thee.”

<span id="xxxv.i.xvi-p6"></span>**3** To the saints who are on the
earth, And to the excellent; all my delight is in them.

<span id="xxxv.i.xvi-p7"></span>**4** Multiplied shall be their sorrows
who offer to a stranger; I will not taste their libations of blood, Nor
will I take their names in my lips.

<span id="xxxv.i.xvi-p8"></span>**5** Jehovah is the portion of my
inheritance, and of my cup; Thou maintainest my lot.

<span id="xxxv.i.xvi-p9"></span>**6** The lines have fallen to me in
pleasant *places*; Yea, an inheritance that is goodly hath fallen to me.

<span id="xxxv.i.xvi-p10"></span>**7** I will magnify Jehovah, who
giveth me counsel; Even in the nights instruct me do my reins.

<span id="xxxv.i.xvi-p11"></span>**8** I have set Jehovah before me
continually; Since he is at my right hand, I shall not be moved.

<span id="xxxv.i.xvi-p12"></span>**9** Therefore glad is my heart,
rejoice doth my tongue; Also my flesh dwelleth in confidence.

<span id="xxxv.i.xvi-p13"></span>**10** For thou wilt not leave my soul
in the grave; Nor wilt thou make thy Holy One to see the pit.

<span id="xxxv.i.xvi-p14"></span>**11** Thou wilt make known to me the
way of life; Fullness of joy *is* in thy countenance; Pleasures *are* at
thy right hand for evermore.

<span id="xxxv.i.xvii"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i.xvii-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i.xvii-p2"></span>PSALM 17

<span id="xxxv.i.xvii-p3"></span>A Prayer of David

<span id="xxxv.i.xvii-p4"></span>**1** Hear, O Jehovah! my
righteousness; Attend to my cry; Hearken to my prayer, which is not in
lips of deceit.

<span id="xxxv.i.xvii-p5"></span>**2** From the presence of thy
countenance let my judgment go forth Let thine eyes behold uprightness.

<span id="xxxv.i.xvii-p6"></span>**3** Thou hast proved my heart; Thou
hast visited *it* by night; Thou hast examined *it*, thou shalt not find
*any thing in it*; My thought shall not pass beyond my mouth.

<span id="xxxv.i.xvii-p7"></span>**4** As for the works of men, by the
word of thy lips I have taken heed of the ways of the destroyer.

<span id="xxxv.i.xvii-p8"></span>**5** Uphold my steps in thy paths,
That my footsteps may not slide.

<span id="xxxv.i.xvii-p9"></span>**6** I have called upon thee, surely
thou wilt hear me, O God! Incline thy ear to me, and hear my speech.

<span id="xxxv.i.xvii-p10"></span>**7** Make marvelous thy mercies, O
thou Preserver of those who trust \[*in thee*,\] From those that exalt
themselves against thy right hand.

<span id="xxxv.i.xvii-p11"></span>**8** Keep me as the apple, the
daughter of the eye; In the shadow of thy wings hide me,

<span id="xxxv.i.xvii-p12"></span>**9** From the face of the ungodly who
endeavor to destroy me — Of my enemies who in my soul besiege me.

<span id="xxxv.i.xvii-p13"></span>**10** In their own fat they have
enclosed themselves; With their mouth they have spoken haughtily.

<span id="xxxv.i.xvii-p14"></span>**11** In our steps they have now
encompassed me; eyes they have set to east down to the ground.

<span id="xxxv.i.xvii-p15"></span>**12** He is like a lion, he desireth
to seize his prey, And like a lion’s whelp which lurketh in secret
places.

<span id="xxxv.i.xvii-p16"></span>**13** Arise, O Jehovah! confront him,
lay him prostrate; Deliver my soul from the ungodly man by thy sword

<span id="xxxv.i.xvii-p17"></span>**14** From men by thy hand, O
Jehovah! — From men who are of long duration, Whose portion is in life,
Whose belly thou fillets with thy secret, goods: Filled to the full are
their children with them, And their residue they leave to their babes.

<span id="xxxv.i.xvii-p18"></span>**15** As for me in righteousness I
shall behold thy face; I shall be satisfied when I shall awake with thy
likeness.

<span id="xxxv.i.xviii"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i.xviii-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i.xviii-p2"></span>PSALM 18

<span id="xxxv.i.xviii-p3"></span>To the Chief Musician. Of the servant
of Jehovah, David, who spake to Jehovah the words of this song, in the
day that Jehovah delivered him from the hand of all his enemies, and
from the hand of Saul. And he said,

<span id="xxxv.i.xviii-p4"></span>**1** I will love thee, O Jehovah! my
strength;

<span id="xxxv.i.xviii-p5"></span>**2** Jehovah my rock, my fortress,
and my deliverer; My God, my rock, I will hope in him: My shield and the
horn of my salvation, my refuge.

<span id="xxxv.i.xviii-p6"></span>**3** Upon the praised Jehovah will I
call; And from my enemies I shall be saved.

<span id="xxxv.i.xviii-p7"></span>**4** Encompassed me had the cords of
death. The torrents of ungodliness had affrighted me.

<span id="xxxv.i.xviii-p8"></span>**5** The cords of the grave had
encompassed me; Prevented me had the snares of death.

<span id="xxxv.i.xviii-p9"></span>**6** In my distress I called upon
Jehovah, And to my God I cried: And he heard from his temple my voice,
And my cry before him came, \[*even*\] into his ears.

<span id="xxxv.i.xviii-p10"></span>**7** Then shake and tremble did the
earth; And the foundations of the mountains were troubled and shaken,
Because he was wroth.

<span id="xxxv.i.xviii-p11"></span>**8** There ascended smoke out of his
nostrils, And fire *proceeding* from his mouth consumed; Coals were
kindled by it.

<span id="xxxv.i.xviii-p12"></span>**9** And he bowed the heavens and
descended; And thick darkness *was* under his feet.

<span id="xxxv.i.xviii-p13"></span>**10** And he rode upon a cherub and
flew; And was carried upon the wings of the wind.

<span id="xxxv.i.xviii-p14"></span>**11** He made darkness his hiding
place; Round about him his pavilion was dark waters, And the clouds of
the skies.

<span id="xxxv.i.xviii-p15"></span>**12** At the brightness *which was*
before him his clouds passed away, \[*There were*\] hail-storm, and
coals of fire.

<span id="xxxv.i.xviii-p16"></span>**13** And thunder in the heavens did
Jehovah, And the Most High sent forth his voice; \[*There were*\]
hailstorm and coals of fire.

<span id="xxxv.i.xviii-p17"></span>**14** And he sent out his army and
scattered them; And lightnings he multiplied, and put them into
confusion.

<span id="xxxv.i.xviii-p18"></span>**15** And seen were the abysses of
the waters, And disclosed were the foundations of the world, At thy
rebuke, O Jehovah! At the blast of the breath of thy nostrils.

<span id="xxxv.i.xviii-p19"></span>**16** He sent from on high, he took
me; He drew me from waters great.

<span id="xxxv.i.xviii-p20"></span>**17** He delivered me from my enemy
\[*that was*\] strong, And from my adversary; Because they were stronger
than I.

<span id="xxxv.i.xviii-p21"></span>**18** They had prevented me in the
day of my calamity; And Jehovah was a support for me.

<span id="xxxv.i.xviii-p22"></span>**19** And he brought me forth into a
wide place; He rescued me because he wished well to me.

<span id="xxxv.i.xviii-p23"></span>**20** Rewarded me hath Jehovah
according to my righteousness; According to the purity of my hands he
hath repaid me;

<span id="xxxv.i.xviii-p24"></span>**21** Because I have kept the ways
of Jehovah, And have not impiously departed from my God;

<span id="xxxv.i.xviii-p25"></span>**22** Because all his judgments *I
have had* before me, And his statutes I have not removed from me.

<span id="xxxv.i.xviii-p26"></span>**23** And I have been upright with
him, And have kept me from my iniquity.

<span id="xxxv.i.xviii-p27"></span>**24** And repaid me hath Jehovah
according to my righteousness According to the purity of my hands before
his eyes.

<span id="xxxv.i.xviii-p28"></span>**25** With the merciful thou wilt
deal mercifully, With a man of uprightness thou wilt show thyself
upright.

<span id="xxxv.i.xviii-p29"></span>**26** With the pure thou wilt be
pure, And with the perverse thou wilt deal perversely.

<span id="xxxv.i.xviii-p30"></span>**27** For thou the afflicted people
wilt save, And the haughty eyes thou wilt east down.

<span id="xxxv.i.xviii-p31"></span>**28** For thou shalt light my lamp,
O Jehovah! My God shall enlighten my darkness.

<span id="xxxv.i.xviii-p32"></span>**29** For by thee I shall break
through the wedge of a troop, And by my God I shall leap over a wall.

<span id="xxxv.i.xviii-p33"></span>**30** As for God perfect is his way;
The word of Jehovah \[*is*\] refined; A shield is He to all who confide
in him.

<span id="xxxv.i.xviii-p34"></span>**31** For who is God besides
Jehovah? And who is strong except our God?

<span id="xxxv.i.xviii-p35"></span>**32** It is God who hath girded me
with strength, And hath made perfect my way.

<span id="xxxv.i.xviii-p36"></span>**33** He maketh my feet like *those*
of hinds, And upon my high places he hath set me.

<span id="xxxv.i.xviii-p37"></span>**34** He traineth my hands to the
battle, And broken will be a bow of steel by my arms.

<span id="xxxv.i.xviii-p38"></span>**35** And thou hast given me the
shield of thy salvation, And thy right hand hath sustained me, And thy
clemency hath increased me.

<span id="xxxv.i.xviii-p39"></span>**36** Thou hast enlarged my steps
under me, And my ankles shall not totter.

<span id="xxxv.i.xviii-p40"></span>**37** I will pursue my enemies and
will seize them; Nor will I return until I have consumed them.

<span id="xxxv.i.xviii-p41"></span>**38** I have afflicted them, and
they were not able to rise; They have fallen under my feet.

<span id="xxxv.i.xviii-p42"></span>**39** Thou hast girded me with might
for the battle; Thou hast bowed down my enemies under me.

<span id="xxxv.i.xviii-p43"></span>**40** And of my enemies thou hast
given me the neck, And \[*as for*\] my haters I will destroy them.

<span id="xxxv.i.xviii-p44"></span>**41** They shall cry aloud, and
*there shall* *be* no Savior *for them*; To Jehovah, but he shall not
answer them.

<span id="xxxv.i.xviii-p45"></span>**42** And I will bruise them to
powder as dust before the wind; As the mire of the streets I will tread
upon them.

<span id="xxxv.i.xviii-p46"></span>**43** Thou shalt deliver me from the
contentions of the people; Thou shalt make me head of the nations; A
people whom I have not known shall serve me.

<span id="xxxv.i.xviii-p47"></span>**44** At the hearing of the ear they
shall obey me; The children of strangers shall lie to me;

<span id="xxxv.i.xviii-p48"></span>**45** The children of strangers
shall lose courage, And tremble from within their places of concealment.

<span id="xxxv.i.xviii-p49"></span>**46** Let Jehovah live and blessed
*be* my strength, And let the God of my salvation be exalted:

<span id="xxxv.i.xviii-p50"></span>**47** The God who giveth vengeance
for me, And subdueth peoples under me.

<span id="xxxv.i.xviii-p51"></span>**48** My deliverer from my enemies:
Yea, from those who had risen up against me thou hast lifted me up: From
the man of violence thou hast rescued me.

<span id="xxxv.i.xviii-p52"></span>**49** Therefore will I praise thee,
O Jehovah! among the Gentiles, And to thy name will I sing.

<span id="xxxv.i.xviii-p53"></span>**50** Who worketh great deliverances
for his king, And showeth mercy to his anointed, \[even to\] David, And
to his seed for ever.

<span id="xxxv.i.xix"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i.xix-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i.xix-p2"></span>PSALM 19

<span id="xxxv.i.xix-p3"></span>To the Chief Musician. A Psalm of David

<span id="xxxv.i.xix-p4"></span>**1** The heavens recount the glory of
God; And the works of his hands proclaim doth the expanse.

<span id="xxxv.i.xix-p5"></span>**2** Day unto day poureth forth speech;
And night unto night publisheth knowledge.

<span id="xxxv.i.xix-p6"></span>**3** There is no speech and no
language, Where is not heard their voice.

<span id="xxxv.i.xix-p7"></span>**4** Through all the earth hath gone
forth their writing, And to the extremity of the world their words: For
the sun he hath set a tabernacle in them,

<span id="xxxv.i.xix-p8"></span>**5** And he as a bridegroom goeth forth
from his chamber; He exulteth as a strong man to run *his* course.

<span id="xxxv.i.xix-p9"></span>**6** From *one* extremity of the
heavens *is* his going forth, And his circuit to the utmost limits
thereof, And no *person* is hidden from his heat.

<span id="xxxv.i.xix-p10"></span>**7** The law of the Lord is perfect,
restoring the soul; The testimony of Jehovah is faithful, instructing in
wisdom the babes;

<span id="xxxv.i.xix-p11"></span>**8** The statutes of Jehovah *are*
right, rejoicing the heart; The commandment of the Lord *is* pure,
enlightening the eyes;

<span id="xxxv.i.xix-p12"></span>**9** The fear of Jehovah is clean,
enduring for ever; The judgments of Jehovah are truth, they are
justified together.

<span id="xxxv.i.xix-p13"></span>**10** More desirable \[*are they*\]
than gold, and much fine gold; And sweeter than honey, and the dropping
of honeycombs.

<span id="xxxv.i.xix-p14"></span>**11** Moreover, thy servant is made
circumspect by them; And in their observance the reward *is* great.

<span id="xxxv.i.xix-p15"></span>**12** His errors who can understand?
From my hidden *sins* cleanse thou me.

<span id="xxxv.i.xix-p16"></span>**13** Likewise from presumptuous sins
restrain thou thy servant, That they may not have dominion over me; Then
upright shall I be and clean from much wickedness.

<span id="xxxv.i.xix-p17"></span>**14** Let the words of my mouth, and
the meditation of my heart be acceptable Before thee, O Jehovah! my
strength and my Redeemer.

<span id="xxxv.i.xx"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i.xx-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i.xx-p2"></span>PSALM 20

<span id="xxxv.i.xx-p3"></span>To the Chief Musician. A Psalm Of David

<span id="xxxv.i.xx-p4"></span>**1** May Jehovah hear thee in the day of
trouble!

<span id="xxxv.i.xx-p5"></span>**2** May he send help to thee from the
sanctuary! And out of Zion sustain thee!

<span id="xxxv.i.xx-p6"></span>**3** May he be mindful of all thy
offerings! And thy holocaust may he make flit! Selah.

<span id="xxxv.i.xx-p7"></span>**4** May he give to thee according to
thy heart! And all thy counsel may he fulfill!

<span id="xxxv.i.xx-p8"></span>**5** That we may exult in thy salvation,
And in the name of our God erect a banner, When Jehovah shall fulfill
all thy petitions.

<span id="xxxv.i.xx-p9"></span>**6** Now I have known that Jehovah hath
saved his anointed; He will hear him from the heavens of his sanctuary,
In the mightiness of the salvation of his right hand.

<span id="xxxv.i.xx-p10"></span>**7** Some *trust* in chariots, and some
in horses; But the name of Jehovah our God we will remember.

<span id="xxxv.i.xx-p11"></span>**8** They are bowed down and fallen;
But we are risen up and stand erect.

<span id="xxxv.i.xx-p12"></span>**9** O Jehovah! do thou save; Let the
King hear us in the day that we call upon him.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxi"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i.xxi-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i.xxi-p2"></span>PSALM 21

<span id="xxxv.i.xxi-p3"></span>To the Chief Musician. A Psalm Of David

<span id="xxxv.i.xxi-p4"></span>**1** O Jehovah! in thy strength rejoice
shall the king, And in thy salvation how greatly shall he exult!

<span id="xxxv.i.xxi-p5"></span>**2** The desire of his heart thou hast
given him, And what he uttered with his lips, thou hast not denied
*him*. Selah.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxi-p6"></span>**3** For thou shalt prevent him with
blessings of good; Thou shalt place upon his head a crown of gold.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxi-p7"></span>**4** Life he asked from thee; Thou hast
given him length of days for ever and ever.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxi-p8"></span>**5** Great *is* his glory in thy
salvation: Splendor and beauty thou hast put upon him.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxi-p9"></span>**6** For thou hast set him \[*to be*\]
blessings for ever: Thou hast gladdened him with joy before thy
countenance.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxi-p10"></span>**7** For the king trusteth in Jehovah;
And through the goodness of the Most High, he shall not be moved

<span id="xxxv.i.xxi-p11"></span>**8** Find out shall thy hand all thy
enemies; Thy right hand shall find out thy haters.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxi-p12"></span>**9** Thou shalt put them as in a
furnace of fire in the time of thy wrath, O Jehova! In his wrath he
shall overwhelm them, And consume them shall the fire.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxi-p13"></span>**10** Their fruit from the earth thou
wilt destroy, And their seed from among the sons of men.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxi-p14"></span>**11** For they have spread out against
thee evil; They have devised against thee a stratagem which they could
not accomplish.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxi-p15"></span>**12** For thou wilt set them as a
butt; On thy strings thou shalt make ready *thy arrows* against their
faces.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxi-p16"></span>**13** Be thou exalted, O Jehovah! in
thy strength, *Then* we will sing and celebrate in psalms thy power.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxii"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i.xxii-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i.xxii-p2"></span>PSALM 22

<span id="xxxv.i.xxii-p3"></span>To the Chief Musician. Upon the hind of
the morning. A Psalm Of David

<span id="xxxv.i.xxii-p4"></span>**1** My God! my God! why hast thou
forsaken me? \[*Why art thou*\] far from my help, from the words of my
roaring?

<span id="xxxv.i.xxii-p5"></span>**2** O my God! I cry by day, and thou
dost not hear: And in the night, and am not silent.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxii-p6"></span>**3** Yet thou art holy, Inhabiting the
praises of Israel.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxii-p7"></span>**4** In thee trust did our fathers:
They trusted, and thou didst deliver them.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxii-p8"></span>**5** To thee they cried, and were
saved: In thee they trusted, and were not put to shame.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxii-p9"></span>**6** But I *am* a worm, and not a man;
The reproach of men, and despised of the people.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxii-p10"></span>**7** All who see me scoff at me: They
thrust out the lip, they shake the head.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxii-p11"></span>**8** “He hath devolved,” *say they*,
“upon Jehovah, *his* cause, let him rescue him, “Let him deliver him,
since he hath a favor for him.”

<span id="xxxv.i.xxii-p12"></span>**9** Surely it is thou who didst take
me out of the womb, Causing me to confide upon the breasts of my mother.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxii-p13"></span>**10** Upon thee I was cast from the
womb: From the belly of my mother my God art thou.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxii-p14"></span>**11** Depart not far from me, for
trouble is near, For there is no helper.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxii-p15"></span>**12** Encompassed me have bulls
\[*that are*\] strong, The bulls of Bashan have beset me.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxii-p16"></span>**13** They have opened upon me their
mouth, As a lion ravening and roaring.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxii-p17"></span>**14** Like water I have flowed,
 <span id="fr_313"></span>[314](#fn_313) And disjointed have been  <span
id="fr_314"></span>[315](#fn_314) all my bones: My heart hath been
 <span id="fr_315"></span>[316](#fn_315) like wax, It hath been  <span
id="fr_316"></span>[317](#fn_316) melted in the midst of my bowels.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxii-p22"></span>**15** Dried up as a potsherd hath
been  <span id="fr_317"></span>[318](#fn_317) my strength, And my tongue
cleaveth to my jaws; And to the dust of death thou hast brought me.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxii-p24"></span>**16** For encompassed me have dogs;
The assembly of the wicked have surrounded me: They have pierced my
hands and my feet.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxii-p25"></span>**17** I will count all my bones; As
for them they look and gaze upon me.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxii-p26"></span>**18** They divide my garments among
them; Upon my vesture they cast the lot.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxii-p27"></span>**19** And thou, O Jehovah! be not far
from me; *Thou who art* my strength, to my aid hasten.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxii-p28"></span>**20** Rescue from the sword my soul;
From the hand of the dog my only one.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxii-p29"></span>**21** Save me from the mouth of the
lion, And from the horns of unicorns do thou hear me.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxii-p30"></span>**22** I will declare thy name to my
brethren; In the midst of the assembly will I praise thee.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxii-p31"></span>**23** *Saying*, “Ye who fear Jehovah
praise him: “All ye the seed of Jacob glorify him: “And stand in awe of
him, all ye the seed of Israel.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxii-p32"></span>**24** “For he hath not despised nor
disdained the poor; “Nor hath he hidden his face from him; “And when he
cried to him, he heard him.”

<span id="xxxv.i.xxii-p33"></span>**25** From thee shall proceed my
praise in the congregation great; My vows will I pay before them that
fear him.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxii-p34"></span>**26** Eat shall the poor, and be
satisfied; They shall praise Jehovah who seek him; Your heart shall live
for ever.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxii-p35"></span>**27** Remember and turn to Jehovah
shall all the ends of the earth; And prostrate themselves before his
face shall all the tribes of the Gentiles.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxii-p36"></span>**28** For Jehovah’s is the kingdom,
That he may have dominion among the Gentiles.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxii-p37"></span>**29** Eat and worship shall all the
fat ones of the earth: Before his face shall bow all who are going down
to the dust; And he who his own soul doth not quicken.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxii-p38"></span>**30** *Their* seed shall serve him,
It shall be registered to the Lord for a generation.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxii-p39"></span>**31** They shall come and shall
declare his righteousness, To a people that shall be born, because he
hath done \[*this*.\],

<span id="xxxv.i.xxiii"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i.xxiii-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i.xxiii-p2"></span>PSALM 23

<span id="xxxv.i.xxiii-p3"></span>A Psalm of David

<span id="xxxv.i.xxiii-p4"></span>**1** Jehovah is my shepherd,
therefore I shall not want any thing.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxiii-p5"></span>**2** In pastures of grass he maketh
me to lie down; To waters gently flowing he leadeth me.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxiii-p6"></span>**3** My soul he restoreth: He leadeth
me by the paths of righteousness for his name’s sake.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxiii-p7"></span>**4** Though I should walk in the
valley of the shadow of death, I will not fear evil, because thou art
with me; Thy staff and thy crook they comfort me.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxiii-p8"></span>**5** Thou wilt prepare before me a
table in the presence of my persecutors; Thou wilt anoint with oil my
head; My cup overfloweth.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxiii-p9"></span>**6** Surely goodness and mercy shall
follow me all the days of my life, And I shall dwell in the house of
Jehovah for a length of days.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxiv"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i.xxiv-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i.xxiv-p2"></span>PSALM 24

<span id="xxxv.i.xxiv-p3"></span>A Psalm of David

<span id="xxxv.i.xxiv-p4"></span>**1** Jehovah’s is the earth, and the
fullness thereof; The world, and those who dwell therein.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxiv-p5"></span>**2** For he upon the seas hath founded
it, And upon the floods he hath arranged it.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxiv-p6"></span>**3** Who shall ascend into the
mountain of Jehovah? Who shall stand in the place of his holiness?

<span id="xxxv.i.xxiv-p7"></span>**4** He who is clean in hands and pure
in heart, Who hath not lifted up to vanity his soul, And hath not sworn
deceitfully.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxiv-p8"></span>**5** He shall receive blessing from
Jehovah, And righteousness from the God of his salvation.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxiv-p9"></span>**6** This is the generation of those
who seek him, Of those who seek thy face, O Jacob! Selah.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxiv-p10"></span>**7** Lift up, O ye gates! your heads,
And be ye lifted up, ye doors everlasting! And enter shall the King of
Glory.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxiv-p11"></span>**8** Who is this King of Glory?
Jehovah strong and mighty, Jehovah mighty in power.  <span
id="fr_318"></span>[319](#fn_318)

<span id="xxxv.i.xxiv-p13"></span>**9** Lift up, O ye gates! your heads,
Lift up, I say, ye doors everlasting! *And* enter shall the King of
Glory.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxiv-p14"></span>**10** Who is this King of Glory?
Jehovah of armies — He is the King of Glory. Selah.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxv"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i.xxv-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i.xxv-p2"></span>PSALM 25

<span id="xxxv.i.xxv-p3"></span>Of David

<span id="xxxv.i.xxv-p4"></span>**1** To thee, O Jehovah! my soul have I
lifted up.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxv-p5"></span>**2** O my God! in thee have I hoped:
Let me not be put to shame, Let not my enemies rejoice over me.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxv-p6"></span>**3** Yea none who wait on thee shall be
put to shame: They shall be ashamed who deal perfidiously without cause.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxv-p7"></span>**4** Thy ways, O Jehovah! make me to
know, Thy paths teach thou me.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxv-p8"></span>**5** Direct me in thy truth, and teach
me; For thou art the God of my salvation; For thee I have waited all the
day.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxv-p9"></span>**6** Remember thy compassions, O
Jehovah! And thy loving-kindnesses; for they have been from everlasting.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxv-p10"></span>**7** The transgressions of my youth,
and my iniquities do not thou remember According to thy clemency
remember thou me, For the sake of thy goodness, O Jehovah!

<span id="xxxv.i.xxv-p11"></span>**8** Good and upright *is* Jehovah,
Therefore he will teach sinners in the way.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxv-p12"></span>**9** He will guide the poor in
judgment, And will teach the poor his way.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxv-p13"></span>**10** All the ways of Jehovah are
mercy and truth, To those who keep his covenant and his testimony.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxv-p14"></span>**11** For the sake of thy name, O
Jehovah! Be merciful to my iniquity, for great is it.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxv-p15"></span>**12** Who is the man that feareth
Jehovah? He will teach him in the way which he should choose.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxv-p16"></span>**13** His soul in good shall dwell,
And his seed shall inherit the land.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxv-p17"></span>**14** The counsel of Jehovah is to
those who fear him, That he may make known to them his covenant.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxv-p18"></span>**15** My eyes are continually towards
Jehovah, For he will bring out of the net my feet.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxv-p19"></span>**16** Have respect to me, take pity
upon me, For solitary and poor am I.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxv-p20"></span>**17** The afflictions of my heart are
enlarged; Out of my distresses do thou bring me.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxv-p21"></span>**18** Behold my affliction and my
travail, And take away all my sins.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxv-p22"></span>**19** Behold my enemies, for they are
multiplied; And with a violent hatred they hate me.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxv-p23"></span>**20** Guard my soul, and rescue me,
That I may not be ashamed; For I have trusted in thee.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxv-p24"></span>**21** Let integrity and rectitude
preserve me; Because I have waited for thee.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxv-p25"></span>**22** Redeem O God! Israel from all
his troubles.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxvi"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i.xxvi-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i.xxvi-p2"></span>PSALM 26

<span id="xxxv.i.xxvi-p3"></span>Of David

<span id="xxxv.i.xxvi-p4"></span>**1** Judge me, O Jehovah: Because in
my integrity I have walked, And in Jehovah have trusted, I shall not
stumble.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxvi-p5"></span>**2** Prove me, O Jehovah! and try me,
Examine my reins and my heart.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxvi-p6"></span>**3** For thy goodness *is* before my
eyes; Therefore I have walked in thy truth.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxvi-p7"></span>**4** I have not sat with men of
vanity, And with crafty men I will not go in.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxvi-p8"></span>**5** I hate the assembly of
transgressors, And with the wicked I will not sit.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxvi-p9"></span>**6** I will wash in purity my hands,
And will encompass thy altar, O Jehovah!

<span id="xxxv.i.xxvi-p10"></span>**7** To cause to be heard the voice
of praise, And to tell of all thy marvelous deeds.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxvi-p11"></span>**8** O Jehovah! I have loved the
habitation of thy house, And the place of the dwelling of thy glory.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxvi-p12"></span>**9** Gather not with ungodly men, my
soul, Nor with men of bloods my life.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxvi-p13"></span>**10** For in their hands *is*
maliciousness, And their right hand is full of bribes.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxvi-p14"></span>**11** But as for me in my integrity I
will walk: Redeem me, and have mercy upon me.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxvi-p15"></span>**12** My foot hath stood in
uprightness: In the congregations will I bless thee, O Jehovah!

<span id="xxxv.i.xxvii"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i.xxvii-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i.xxvii-p2"></span>PSALM 27

<span id="xxxv.i.xxvii-p3"></span>Of David

<span id="xxxv.i.xxvii-p4"></span>**1** Jehovah is my light and my
salvation, Whom shall I fear? Jehovah *is* the strength of my life, Of
whom shall I be afraid?

<span id="xxxv.i.xxvii-p5"></span>**2** When approach against me did the
wicked, To devour my flesh — My oppressors and my enemies against me —
They stumbled and fell.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxvii-p6"></span>**3** If there should encamp against
me a camp, My heart shall not fear: If there should rise against me war,
In this shall I have confidence.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxvii-p7"></span>**4** One thing have I requested from
Jehovah — This will I follow after — That I may dwell in the house of
Jehovah all the days of my life, To behold the beauty of Jehovah, To
survey his temple.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxvii-p8"></span>**5** For he shall hide me in his
pavilion in the day of evil; He shall conceal me in the secret
\[*recess*\] of his tent, Upon a rock he will set me.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxvii-p9"></span>**6** And now he shall exalt my head
Above my enemies who surround me: And I will sacrifice in his tabernacle
sacrifices of triumph; I will sing and will celebrate in psalms Jehovah.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxvii-p10"></span>**7** Hear, O Jehovah! my voice with
which I cry; Have mercy upon me and answer me.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxvii-p11"></span>**8** To thee my heart hath said,
“Seek ye my face;” Therefore thy face, O Jehovah! will I seek.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxvii-p12"></span>**9** Hide not thy face from me; Cast
not away in wrath thy servant: My strength thou hast been, do not desert
me, And do not forsake me, O God of my salvation!

<span id="xxxv.i.xxvii-p13"></span>**10** When my father and my mother
shall forsake me, Jehovah shall receive me.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxvii-p14"></span>**11** Teach me, O Jehovah! thy way,
And lead me in the path of rectitude because of my enemies.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxvii-p15"></span>**12** Do not deliver me to the
desire of my oppressors, For risen up against me have false witnesses,
And he who uttereth violence.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxvii-p16"></span>**13** Unless I had believed to see
the goodness of Jehovah, in the land of the living —.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxvii-p17"></span>**14** Wait thou on Jehovah; Be
strong, and he will comfort thy heart, And wait thou on Jehovah.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxviii"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i.xxviii-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i.xxviii-p2"></span>PSALM 28

<span id="xxxv.i.xxviii-p3"></span>Of David

<span id="xxxv.i.xxviii-p4"></span>**1** Unto thee, O Jehovah! will I
cry; O my strength! hold not thy peace from me Lest if thou shouldst be
silent to me, I then become like those who descend into the grave.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxviii-p5"></span>**2** Hear the voice of my prayers
when I cry to thee, When I lift up my hands to the sanctuary of thy
holiness.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxviii-p6"></span>**3** Draw me not away with ungodly
men, And with the workers of iniquity, Who speak peace  <span
id="fr_319"></span>[320](#fn_319) with their neighbors, When in their
hearts is malice.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxviii-p8"></span>**4** Give them according to their
works, And according to the wickedness of their doings: According to the
work of their hands give them, Render their reward to them.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxviii-p9"></span>**5** Because they do not consider
the doing of Jehovah, Nor the work of his hands, Let him destroy them
and not build them up.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxviii-p10"></span>**6** Blessed *be* Jehovah! For he
hath heard the voice of my supplications.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxviii-p11"></span>**7** Jehovah *is* my strength and
my shield; In him trusted hath my heart, and I have been helped:
Therefore exult shall my heart, And with my song will I celebrate him.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxviii-p12"></span>**8** Jehovah *is* strength to them,
And the strength of the salvations of his Anointed *is* He.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxviii-p13"></span>**9** Save thy people, and bless thy
inheritance; Feed them and exalt them for ever.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxix"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i.xxix-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i.xxix-p2"></span>PSALM 29

<span id="xxxv.i.xxix-p3"></span>A Psalm of David

<span id="xxxv.i.xxix-p4"></span>**1** Ascribe to Jehovah: ye sons of
the mighty — Ascribe to Jehovah glory and strength.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxix-p5"></span>**2** Ascribe to Jehovah the glory of
his name; Worship before Jehovah in the brightness of his sanctuary.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxix-p6"></span>**3** The voice of Jehovah is upon the
waters; The God of glory thundereth; Jehovah is upon the waters great.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxix-p7"></span>**4** The voice of Jehovah is in
strength, The voice of Jehovah is in majesty.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxix-p8"></span>**5** The voice of Jehovah breaketh the
cedars; Break, I say, doth Jehovah the cedars of Lebanon.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxix-p9"></span>**6** And he maketh Lebanon to leap
like a calf, And Sirion like the son of the unicorns.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxix-p10"></span>**7** The voice of Jehovah striketh
out flames of fire.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxix-p11"></span>**8** The voice of Jehovah maketh the
desert to tremble. Jehovah maketh to tremble the desert of Kadesh.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxix-p12"></span>**9** The voice of Jehovah maketh the
hinds to bring forth, And discovereth the forests, And all *meanwhile*
in his temple speak his praise.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxix-p13"></span>**10** Jehovah over the flood
presideth, Preside, I say, doth Jehovah \[*as*\] King for ever.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxix-p14"></span>**11** Jehovah strength to his people
will give; Jehovah will bless his people with peace.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxx"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i.xxx-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i.xxx-p2"></span>PSALM 30

<span id="xxxv.i.xxx-p3"></span>A Psalm of a Song at the dedication of
the house of David

<span id="xxxv.i.xxx-p4"></span>**1** I will exalt thee, O Jehovah! for
thou hast raised me up, And hast not made glad my enemies over me.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxx-p5"></span>**2** O Jehovah, my God! I have cried to
thee, And thou hast healed me.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxx-p6"></span>**3** O Jehovah! thou hast brought up
from the grove my soul; Thou hast quickened me from among those who
descend into the pit.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxx-p7"></span>**4** Sing to Jehovah, O ye his meek
ones! And acknowledge the memorial of his holiness.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxx-p8"></span>**5** For *there is only* a moment in
his anger, *But* life in his favor: In the evening will lodge weeping,
And in the morning shall come exultation.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxx-p9"></span>**6** But as for me I had said in my
tranquillity, “I shall not be moved for ever.”

<span id="xxxv.i.xxx-p10"></span>**7** O Jehovah! in thy good pleasure
Thou hast established strength to my mountain; Thou didst hide thy face,
I was confounded.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxx-p11"></span>**8** O Jehovah! to thee I cried, And
to my Lord I made supplication.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxx-p12"></span>**9** What profit shall there be in my
blood, When I descend into the pit? Celebrate thee shall the dust? Shall
it proclaim thy truth?

<span id="xxxv.i.xxx-p13"></span>**10** Hear, O Jehovah! and have mercy
upon me; O Jehovah! be thou a helper to me.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxx-p14"></span>**11** Thou hast turned my mourning
into dancing for me; Thou hast loosed my sackcloth, And girded me with
gladness.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxx-p15"></span>**12** That celebrate thee in psalms
may my glory, and not be silent: O Jehovah, my God! for ever will I
celebrate thee.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxi"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxi-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxi-p2"></span>PSALM 31

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxi-p3"></span>To the Chief Musician,. A Psalm of
David

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxi-p4"></span>**1** In thee, O Jehovah! have I
trusted, Let me not be put to shame for ever: In thy righteousness
deliver me.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxi-p5"></span>**2** Incline to me thy ear, Speedily
do thou rescue me; Be to me for a rock of strength, For a house of
defense to save me.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxi-p6"></span>**3** For my rock, and my fortress
*art* thou: And for the sake of thy name thou wilt direct and guide me.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxi-p7"></span>**4** Extricate me from the net, which
they have hidden for me, For thou art my strength.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxi-p8"></span>**5** Into thy hand I will commend my
spirit; For thou hast redeemed me, O Jehovah! God of truth.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxi-p9"></span>**6** I hate all those who regard lying
vanities; But as for me in Jehovah I have trusted.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxi-p10"></span>**7** I will exult and rejoice in thy
goodness; Because thou hast looked upon my affliction: Thou hast known
in distresses my soul:

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxi-p11"></span>**8** And thou hast not shut me up in
the hand of the enemy: *But* thou hast set at large my feet.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxi-p12"></span>**9** Have pity upon me, O Jehovah!
for trouble is to me: My eye hath consumed away for vexation; my soul
and my belly.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxi-p13"></span>**10** My life hath riffled through
grid; And my years with groaning: My strength hath sunk through my
sorrow, And my bones have moldered away.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxi-p14"></span>**11** On account of all my enemies I
was a reproach, Yea to my neighbors exceedingly, And a terror to my
acquaintances; And those who saw me abroad fled from me.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxi-p15"></span>**12** I was forgotten as a dead man
from the heart; I became like a vessel \[*that is*\] broken.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxi-p16"></span>**13** For I have heard the slander of
many: Fear *hath seized* me on every side, While they consult together
against me, And to take away my life do devise.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxi-p17"></span>**14** But as for me, in thee have I
trusted, O Jehovah! I have said, “My God art thou.”

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxi-p18"></span>**15** In thy hand are my times;
Rescue me from the hand of my enemies, And from those who persecute me.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxi-p19"></span>**16** Cause to shine upon thy servant
thy face, Save me in thy goodness.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxi-p20"></span>**17** O Jehovah! let me not be put to
shame, For I have called upon thee: Let the wicked be put to shame, Let
Gem be silent in the grave.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxi-p21"></span>**18** Let the lips of lying be put to
shame, Which speak against the righteous a hard thing in pride and
scorn.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxi-p22"></span>**19** How great is thy goodness,
Which thou hast hidden for those who fear thee! Which thou hast
performed for those who confide in thee, Before the sons of men!

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxi-p23"></span>**20** Thou shalt hide them in the
hidden place of thy presence, From the prides of man; Thou shalt conceal
them *as* in a tent, From the strife of tongues.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxi-p24"></span>**21** Blessed be Jehovah! For he hath
made wonderful his goodness towards me, As in a city fortified.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxi-p25"></span>**22** But as for me, I had said in my
fear, “I am cast away from before thy eyes:” Yet truly thou hast heard
the voice of my supplications, When I cried unto thee.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxi-p26"></span>**23** Love Jehovah, all ye meek ones
of his! The faithful preserve doth Jehovah, And he repayeth plentifully
him who behaveth proudly.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxi-p27"></span>**24** Be of good courage, and he
shall strengthen your heart, All ye who hope in Jehovah.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxii"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxii-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxii-p2"></span>PSALM 32

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxii-p3"></span>Of David. Giving instruction

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxii-p4"></span>**1** Blessed are those to whom is
remitted iniquity, And whose transgression is covered.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxii-p5"></span>**2** Blessed is the man to whom
Jehovah doth not impute iniquity, And in whose spirit there is not
guile.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxii-p6"></span>**3** When I kept silence, waste away
did my bones, And when I wailed all the day.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxii-p7"></span>**4** For by day and night heavy upon
me was thy hand; Turned into the drought of summer was my greenness.
Selah.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxii-p8"></span>**5** My sin I have acknowledged to
thee, And my iniquity I have not hid. I said, “I will confess against
myself my wickedness to Jehovah;” And thou didst remit the guilt of my
sin. Selah.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxii-p9"></span>**6** On this account, pray to thee
shall every *man*, that is meek, In the time of finding thee: So that in
a flood of many waters, To him they shall not come near.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxii-p10"></span>**7** Thou art a hiding-place to me;
From trouble thou shalt preserve me; With songs of deliverance thou
shalt encompass me. Selah.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxii-p11"></span>**8** I will instruct thee, And teach
thee the way wherein thou shouldest walk: I will counsel thee with mine
eye.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxii-p12"></span>**9** Be ye not like a horse, *or*
like a mule, Which have not understanding: With bit and bridle his jaws
thou shalt bind, Lest they kick against thee.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxii-p13"></span>**10** Many sorrows *shall* *be* to
the wicked: But the man who hopeth in Jehovah goodness shall encompass.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxii-p14"></span>**11** Rejoice in Jehovah, and exult,
ye righteous! Sing all ye *who are* upright in heart.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxiii"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxiii-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxiii-p2"></span>PSALM 33

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxiii-p3"></span>**1** Exult, ye righteous! in
Jehovah: For to the upright comely is praise.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxiii-p4"></span>**2** Celebrate Jehovah upon the
harp; Upon the nablure,  <span id="fr_320"></span>[321](#fn_320) and
instrument of ten strings, sing psalms to him

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxiii-p6"></span>**3** Sing to him a song that is new;
Ardently sing with shouting.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxiii-p7"></span>**4** For right *is* the word of
Jehovah, And all his works are in faithfulness.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxiii-p8"></span>**5** He loveth righteousness and
judgment: Of the goodness of Jehovah fill is the earth.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxiii-p9"></span>**6** By the word of Jehovah the
heavens were established, And by the breath of his mouth all their host.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxiii-p10"></span>**7** He gathered together as an
heap the waters of the sea; He laid up as in treasure houses the deeps.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxiii-p11"></span>**8** Let all the earth fear
Jehovah; Of him let all the inhabitants of the world stand in awe.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxiii-p12"></span>**9** For he spake, and it was; He
commanded, and it stood.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxiii-p13"></span>**10** Jehovah scattereth the
counsel of the Gentiles, He rendereth fruitless the imaginations of the
peoples.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxiii-p14"></span>**11** The counsel of Jehovah for
ever shall stand, The thoughts of his heart from age to age.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxiii-p15"></span>**12** Blessed is the people to whom
Jehovah is their God, The people whom he hath chosen for: in inheritance
to himself.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxiii-p16"></span>**13** From heavens looked down hath
Jehovah, He hath beheld all the sons of Adam.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxiii-p17"></span>**14** From the dwelling place of
His throne, He hath looked on all the inhabitants of the earth.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxiii-p18"></span>**15** He who hath fashioned
together their hearts, Who understandeth all their works.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxiii-p19"></span>**16** There is not a king saved by
the multitude of an host, Nor a giant rescued by greatness of strength.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxiii-p20"></span>**17** Fallacious is a horse for
safety, And by the greatness of his strength he will not deliver.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxiii-p21"></span>**18** Behold! the eye of Jehovah is
upon those who fear him, \[*Upon those*\] who hope in his mercy;

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxiii-p22"></span>**19** To rescue from death their
souls, To keep them alive in famine.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxiii-p23"></span>**20** Our soul waiteth for Jehovah:
Our help and our shield is he.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxiii-p24"></span>**21** Surely in him rejoice shall
our heart, Because in his holy name we will trust.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxiii-p25"></span>**22** Let thy mercy be upon us, O
Jehovah! According as we have trusted in thee.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxiv"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxiv-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxiv-p2"></span>PSALM 34

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxiv-p3"></span>Of David when he changed his
countenance before Abimelech, who expelled him, and he departed

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxiv-p4"></span>**1** I will bless Jehovah at all
times: Continually his praise *shall be* in my mouth.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxiv-p5"></span>**2** In Jehovah make her boast shall
my soul: Hear shall the humble and be glad.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxiv-p6"></span>**3** Magnify? Jehovah with me, And
let us exalt his name together.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxiv-p7"></span>**4** I sought. Jehovah, and he
answered me, And from all my fears he delivered me.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxiv-p8"></span>**5** They shall look to him, and
shall flow to him, And their faces shall not he ashamed.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxiv-p9"></span>**6** This poor man cried,: and
Jehovah heard him, And from all his distresses saved him.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxiv-p10"></span>**7** Encamp doth the angel of
Jehovah about those who fear him, And will deliver them.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxiv-p11"></span>**8** Taste ye and see that good is
Jehovah: Blessed is the man who trusteth in him.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxiv-p12"></span>**9** Fear Jehovah, ye saints of his;
For nothing is lacking to those who fear him.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxiv-p13"></span>**10** The young lions suffer want
and are famished: But those who fear Jehovah shall not want any good
thing.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxiv-p14"></span>**11** Come ye children, hearken to
me, The fear of Jehovah I will teach you.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxiv-p15"></span>**12** Who is the man that desireth
life, Loving days in which he may see good?

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxiv-p16"></span>**13** Keep thy tongue from evil, And
thy lips from speaking deceit.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxiv-p17"></span>**14** Depart from evil, and do good;
Seek peace, and pursue it.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxiv-p18"></span>**15** The eyes of Jehovah *are* upon
the righteous, And his ears \[*are open*\] to their cry.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxiv-p19"></span>**16** The face of Jehovah is upon
those who do evil, To blot out from the earth their remembrance.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxiv-p20"></span>**17** They cried, and Jehovah heard
*them*, And from all their distresses he delivered them.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxiv-p21"></span>**18** Near is Jehovah to the broken
in heart; The contrite in spirit he will save.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxiv-p22"></span>**19** Many *are* the afflictions of
the righteous; But from them all deliver him will Jehovah.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxiv-p23"></span>**20** He keepeth all his bones: One
of them is not broken.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxiv-p24"></span>**21** That malice shall slay the
wicked, And those who hate the righteous shall be destroyed.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxiv-p25"></span>**22** Redeem doth, Jehovah the soul
of his servants, And they shall not perish who confide in him.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxv"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxv-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxv-p2"></span>PSALM 35

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxv-p3"></span>Of David

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxv-p4"></span>**1** Plead, O Jehovah! with those who
plead with me, Fight against those who fight against me.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxv-p5"></span>**2** Lay hold on shield and buckler,
And rise up to my aid.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxv-p6"></span>**3** Draw out the spear, and stop my
ears against my persecutors: Say to my soul, “Thy salvation am I.”

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxv-p7"></span>**4** Let those be confounded and put
to shame Who seek my soul, Let those be turned back and be abashed Who
devise my hurt.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxv-p8"></span>**5** Let them be as chaff before the
wind? And let the angel of Jehovah drive them.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxv-p9"></span>**6** Let their way be darkness and
slipperiness; And let the angel of Jehovah pursue them:

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxv-p10"></span>**7** For without a cause they have
hid for me the pitfall of their net,  <span
id="fr_321"></span>[322](#fn_321) Without a cause they have digged a pit
for my soul.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxv-p12"></span>**8** Let there come upon him
confusion of which he is not aware; And let the net which he hath hidden
catch him; With confusion let him fall into it.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxv-p13"></span>**9** And my soul hath exulted in
Jehovah, It shall rejoice in his salvation.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxv-p14"></span>**10** All my bones shall say, “O
Jehovah! who is like to thee, “Rescuing the poor from him who is too
strong for him, “The poor and wretched from his spoiler?”

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxv-p15"></span>**11** Rise up do witnesses \[*that
are*\] violent; Things which I have not known they ask me.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxv-p16"></span>**12** They repay me evil for good, To
the bereaving of my soul.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxv-p17"></span>**13** But as for me, in their
sickness my clothing was sackcloth: I afflicted by fasting my soul; And
my prayer upon my own bosom was turned.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxv-p18"></span>**14** As if he had been a friend, as
if a brother to me, I behaved myself *towards him*: As he who mourneth
heavily for his mother I humbled myself.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxv-p19"></span>**15** But they at my halting
rejoiced, they were assembled together: Assembled together, I say,
against me, were the abjects whom I had not known: They have torn with
their lips and have not been silent.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxv-p20"></span>**16** Among perfidious jesters at
feasts, They gnash upon me with their teeth.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxv-p21"></span>**17** O Lord! how long wilt thou
behold it? Rescue my soul from their violence, From the lions my only
one.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxv-p22"></span>**18** I will celebrate thee in the
congregation great: Among people many I will praise thee.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxv-p23"></span>**19** Let not those rejoice over me,
who unjustly are my enemies; Nor let those who hate me without a cause
wink with the eye.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxv-p24"></span>**20** For peace they speak not;

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxv-p25"></span>**21** They have opened against me
their mouth; They have said, “Aha! aha! seen *it* hath our eye.”

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxv-p26"></span>**22** Thou hast seen *it* *also*, O
Jehovah: Be not silent, O Lord! be not far from me.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxv-p27"></span>**23** Arouse thyself, and awake for
my judgment, My God! and my Lord! to my cause.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxv-p28"></span>**24** Judge me according to thy
righteousness, O Jehovah, my God! And let them not rejoice over me.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxv-p29"></span>**25** Let them not say in their
heart, “Aha! our soul!” Let them not say “We have destroyed him.”

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxv-p30"></span>**26** Let those be ashamed and
confounded together, Who rejoice at my calamity; Let those be clothed
with shame and ignominy, Who magnify themselves against me.

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxv-p31"></span>**27** *But* let those shout and
rejoice, who favor my righteousness: And let them say continually,
“Magnified be Jehovah! “Who loveth the peace of his servant.”

<span id="xxxv.i.xxxv-p32"></span>**28** And my tongue shall speak of
thy righteousness; All the day of thy praise.

<span id="xxxv.ii"></span>

<span id="xxxv.ii-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.ii-p2"></span>PSALMS 36—66

<span id="xxxv.ii.i"></span>

<span id="xxxv.ii.i-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.ii.i-p2"></span>PSALM 36

<span id="xxxv.ii.i-p3"></span>To the Chief Musician. Of the servant of
Jehovah, \[even\] of David

<span id="xxxv.ii.i-p4"></span>**1** Ungodliness saith to the wicked man
in the midst of my heart, There is no fear of God before his eyes.

<span id="xxxv.ii.i-p5"></span>**2** For he flattereth himself in his
own eyes, Until his iniquity be found to be hateful.

<span id="xxxv.ii.i-p6"></span>**3** The words of his mouth are iniquity
and deceit, He teaseth to understand that he may do good.

<span id="xxxv.ii.i-p7"></span>**4** Iniquity he meditates upon his bed;
He setteth himself in a way not good; Evil he doth not abhor.

<span id="xxxv.ii.i-p8"></span>**5** O Jehovah! unto the heavens is thy
mercy, Thy truth even unto the clouds.

<span id="xxxv.ii.i-p9"></span>**6** Thy justice is like the great
mountains, Thy judgments are a great deep. Man and beast, thou
preservest, O Jehovah!

<span id="xxxv.ii.i-p10"></span>**7** How precious is thy
loving-kindness, O God! Therefore the sons of men in the shadow of thy
wings shall trust.

<span id="xxxv.ii.i-p11"></span>**8** They shall be fully satisfied with
the fatness of thy house; And of the river of thy pleasures thou shalt
cause them to drink.

<span id="xxxv.ii.i-p12"></span>**9** For with thee is the fountain of
life, And in thy light shall we see light.

<span id="xxxv.ii.i-p13"></span>**10** Extend thy mercy to those who
know thee, And thy righteousness to the upright in heart.

<span id="xxxv.ii.i-p14"></span>**11** Let not the foot of pride come
upon me; And the hand of the ungodly let it not remove me.

<span id="xxxv.ii.i-p15"></span>**12** There fallen are the workers of
iniquity; They are thrust down and shall not be able to stand.  <span
id="fr_322"></span>[323](#fn_322)

<span id="xxxv.ii.ii"></span>

<span id="xxxv.ii.ii-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.ii.ii-p2"></span>PSALM 37

<span id="xxxv.ii.ii-p3"></span>Of David

<span id="xxxv.ii.ii-p4"></span>**1** Vex not thyself because of the
wicked, Nor be envious on account of the workers of iniquity.

<span id="xxxv.ii.ii-p5"></span>**2** For like the grass quickly shall
they be cut down; And as the green herb they shall wither.

<span id="xxxv.ii.ii-p6"></span>**3** Trust thou in Jehovah, and do
good; Dwell in the land, and be fed in truth.

<span id="xxxv.ii.ii-p7"></span>**4** And delight in Jehovah, And he
will grant thee the request of thy heart.

<span id="xxxv.ii.ii-p8"></span>**5** Devolve upon Jehovah thy ways, And
trust in him, and he will bring it to pass.

<span id="xxxv.ii.ii-p9"></span>**6** And he will bring forth as the
light thy righteousness, And thy judgments as the noonday.

<span id="xxxv.ii.ii-p10"></span>**7** Be silent to Jehovah, and wait
