for him; Vex not thyself at him who prospereth in his way, At the man
who committeth wickedness.

<span id="xxxv.ii.ii-p11"></span>**8** Cease from anger, forsake wrath,
Vex not thyself so as to commit sin.

<span id="xxxv.ii.ii-p12"></span>**9** For the wicked shall be cut off;
But those who wait for Jehovah shall inherit the earth.

<span id="xxxv.ii.ii-p13"></span>**10** Yet a little while, and the
ungodly shall not be; And thou shalt give attention to his place, and
shalt not find *him*

<span id="xxxv.ii.ii-p14"></span>**11** But the meek ones shall inherit
the earth, And shall be delighted in the abundance of peace.

<span id="xxxv.ii.ii-p15"></span>**12** Plot doth the ungodly against
the righteous, And gnasheth against him with his teeth.

<span id="xxxv.ii.ii-p16"></span>**13** The Lord shall laugh at him, For
he seeth that coming is his day.

<span id="xxxv.ii.ii-p17"></span>**14** *Their* sword draw do the
ungodly, And their bow they bend, To lay prostrate the poor and needy,
To slay those who are upright in the way.

<span id="xxxv.ii.ii-p18"></span>**15** *But* their sword shall enter
into their own heart, And their bow shall be broken.

<span id="xxxv.ii.ii-p19"></span>**16** Better is a little to the
righteous man, Than the wealth of the ungodly who are great.

<span id="xxxv.ii.ii-p20"></span>**17** For the arms of the ungodly
shall be broken; But Jehovah sustaineth the righteous.

<span id="xxxv.ii.ii-p21"></span>**18** Know doth Jehovah the days of
the upright, And their inheritance for ever shall be.

<span id="xxxv.ii.ii-p22"></span>**19** They shall not be put to shame
in the time of adversity; And in the days of famine they shall be
satisfied.

<span id="xxxv.ii.ii-p23"></span>**20** For the ungodly shall perish,
And the enemies of Jehovah like the fattest of lambs shall be consumed;
Into smoke they shall be consumed.;

<span id="xxxv.ii.ii-p24"></span>**21** Borrow doth the ungodly man, and
doth not repay; But the righteous man is compassionate and giveth.

<span id="xxxv.ii.ii-p25"></span>**22** For those who are blessed of him
shall inherit the earth, And those who are cursed of him shall be cut
off.

<span id="xxxv.ii.ii-p26"></span>**23** By Jehovah the steps of a man
are directed, And his way he will love.

<span id="xxxv.ii.ii-p27"></span>**24** When he shall fall he shall not
be bruised, For Jehovah putteth under \[*him*\] his hand.

<span id="xxxv.ii.ii-p28"></span>**25** Young I have been, I have also
grown old; And yet I have not seen the righteous man forsaken, Nor his
seed begging for bread.

<span id="xxxv.ii.ii-p29"></span>**26** Daily he is compassionate and
lendeth, And his seed is for blessing.

<span id="xxxv.ii.ii-p30"></span>**27** Depart from evil and do good,
And dwell for ever.

<span id="xxxv.ii.ii-p31"></span>**28** For Jehovah loveth judgment, And
doth not forsake his meek ones; For ever shall they be preserved: And
the seed of the ungodly shall be cut off.

<span id="xxxv.ii.ii-p32"></span>**29** The righteous shall inherit the
earth, And shall dwell for ever upon it.

<span id="xxxv.ii.ii-p33"></span>**30** The mouth of the righteous shall
speak wisdom;

<span id="xxxv.ii.ii-p34"></span>**31** The law of his God is in his
heart; Slide not shall his steps.

<span id="xxxv.ii.ii-p35"></span>**32** Watch doth the ungodly the
righteous man, And seeketh to put him to death.

<span id="xxxv.ii.ii-p36"></span>**33** Jehovah will not leave him in
his hand, Nor condemn him when he is judged.

<span id="xxxv.ii.ii-p37"></span>**34** Wait for Jehovah, and keep his
way, And he shall exalt thee to inherit the earth: When the ungodly
shall be cut off thou shalt see it.

<span id="xxxv.ii.ii-p38"></span>**35** I have seen the ungodly man
robust,  <span id="fr_323"></span>[324](#fn_323) And spreading himself
like a green bay tree;

<span id="xxxv.ii.ii-p40"></span>**36** And he passed away, and to I he
was not; And I sought for his place, and he was not found.

<span id="xxxv.ii.ii-p41"></span>**37** Mark the perfect man, and
consider the upright; For the end of such a man is peace.

<span id="xxxv.ii.ii-p42"></span>**38** But transgressors shall be
destroyed together: The end of the ungodly shall be cut off.

<span id="xxxv.ii.ii-p43"></span>**39** But the salvation of the
righteous is from Jehovah: *He will* be their strength in the time of
trouble.

<span id="xxxv.ii.ii-p44"></span>**40** And help them shall Jehovah, and
deliver them: He shall deliver them from the wicked: He shall save them,
because they trust in him.

<span id="xxxv.ii.iii"></span>

<span id="xxxv.ii.iii-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.ii.iii-p2"></span>PSALM 38

<span id="xxxv.ii.iii-p3"></span>A Psalm of David: to bring to
remembrance

<span id="xxxv.ii.iii-p4"></span>**1** O Jehovah! do not in thy fury
rebuke me, And in thy wrath do not chasten me.

<span id="xxxv.ii.iii-p5"></span>**2** For thy arrows go down in me, And
descend upon me doth thy hand.

<span id="xxxv.ii.iii-p6"></span>**3** There is no soundness in my
flesh, because of thy wrath, Nor peace in my bones because of my sin.

<span id="xxxv.ii.iii-p7"></span>**4** For my iniquities have passed
over my head, Like a burden that is weighty, they are too heavy for me.

<span id="xxxv.ii.iii-p8"></span>**5** Putrid \[*and*\] corrupt have my
wounds become, Because of my foolishness.

<span id="xxxv.ii.iii-p9"></span>**6** I am bowed down, I am brought low
exceedingly; Day by day a mourner I do walk:

<span id="xxxv.ii.iii-p10"></span>**7** For my reins are filled with a
burning heat; Nor is there soundness in my flesh.

<span id="xxxv.ii.iii-p11"></span>**8** I am enfeebled and broken
exceedingly: I have roared through the disquietude of my heart.

<span id="xxxv.ii.iii-p12"></span>**9** O Lord! before thee is all my
desire, And my groaning from thee is not hidden,

<span id="xxxv.ii.iii-p13"></span>**10** My heart hath throbbed,
forsaken me hath my strength; And the light of my eyes, it also is gone
from me.

<span id="xxxv.ii.iii-p14"></span>**11** My friends and my companions
aloof from my stroke have stood, And my kinsmen afar off have stood.

<span id="xxxv.ii.iii-p15"></span>**12** And they have laid snares who
sought for my soul; Arid those who sought my hurt have threatened
mischiefs; And deceits daily do they meditate.

<span id="xxxv.ii.iii-p16"></span>**13** But as for me, like a deaf man
I hear not; And *I am* like a dumb man who openeth not his mouth.

<span id="xxxv.ii.iii-p17"></span>**14** And I was as a man who doth not
hear, And in whose mouth there are no reproofs.

<span id="xxxv.ii.iii-p18"></span>**15** For on thee, O Jehovah! do I
wait: Thou wilt answer *me*, O Lord, my God!

<span id="xxxv.ii.iii-p19"></span>**16** For I said, “Lest they should
rejoice over me:” At the slipping of my foot against me they magnified
themselves,

<span id="xxxv.ii.iii-p20"></span>**17** Surely as for me I am ready to
halt; And my sorrow is before me continually.

<span id="xxxv.ii.iii-p21"></span>**18** Surely my iniquity I declare; I
am in consternation because of my sin.

<span id="xxxv.ii.iii-p22"></span>**19** But my enemies are living;
 <span id="fr_324"></span>[325](#fn_324) they are strong; And those are
become mighty who hate me wrongfully.

<span id="xxxv.ii.iii-p24"></span>**20** And they who requite me evil
for good are against me, Because I follow \[*what is*\] good.

<span id="xxxv.ii.iii-p25"></span>**21** Forsake me not, O Jehovah, my
God! Be not far from me.

<span id="xxxv.ii.iii-p26"></span>**22** Hasten to my help, O Lord, my
salvation!

<span id="xxxv.ii.iv"></span>

<span id="xxxv.ii.iv-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.ii.iv-p2"></span>PSALM 39

<span id="xxxv.ii.iv-p3"></span>To the Chief Musician, Jeduthun. A Psalm
of David

<span id="xxxv.ii.iv-p4"></span>**1** I said “I will take heed to my
ways, “That I sin not with my tongue: “I will keep my mouth with a
muzzle, “While the ungodly man standeth before me.”

<span id="xxxv.ii.iv-p5"></span>**2** I was dumb not uttering a word; I
held my peace \[*even*\] from good; And my sorrow was stirred.

<span id="xxxv.ii.iv-p6"></span>**3** My heart became hot within me; In
my musing a fire did burn; I spake with my tongue.

<span id="xxxv.ii.iv-p7"></span>**4** Cause me to know, O Jehovah! my
end, And the number of my days, That I may know of what duration I am.

<span id="xxxv.ii.iv-p8"></span>**5** Behold! as an handbreadth thou
hast made my days, And my duration is as nothing before thee: Surely
altogether vanity is every mart while he standeth.

<span id="xxxv.ii.iv-p9"></span>**6** Surely in a shadow man walketh;
\[Selah. Surely in vain is he disquieted: They heap together, and know
not who shall gather.

<span id="xxxv.ii.iv-p10"></span>**7** And now what do I wait for, O
Lord? My hope is towards thee.

<span id="xxxv.ii.iv-p11"></span>**8** From all my sins deliver thou me:
The reproach of the foolish make me not.

<span id="xxxv.ii.iv-p12"></span>**9** I was dumb; I will not open my
mouth, Because thou hast done it.

<span id="xxxv.ii.iv-p13"></span>**10** Remove from me thy stroke: By
the blow of thy hand I have failed.

<span id="xxxv.ii.iv-p14"></span>**11** With rebukes for iniquity thou
chastisest man; And causest to waste away as a moth his beauty: Surely
vanity *is* every man. Selah.

<span id="xxxv.ii.iv-p15"></span>**12** Hear my prayer, O Jehovah! And
to my cry give ear; At my tears be not silent; For a stranger am I
before thee, A sojourner like all my fathers.

<span id="xxxv.ii.iv-p16"></span>**13** Let me alone, that I may recover
strength, Before I depart and be no more.

<span id="xxxv.ii.v"></span>

<span id="xxxv.ii.v-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.ii.v-p2"></span>PSALM 40

<span id="xxxv.ii.v-p3"></span>To the Chief Musician. A Psalm of David

<span id="xxxv.ii.v-p4"></span>**1** I have patiently waited for
Jehovah, And he inclined to me, and heard my cry.

<span id="xxxv.ii.v-p5"></span>**2** And he drew me out of the roaring
pit, Out of the mire of clay, And set upon a rock my feet; He hath
established my steps.

<span id="xxxv.ii.v-p6"></span>**3** And he hath put in my mouth a song
\[that is\] new, *Even* praise to our God: See shall many and shall
fear, And shall trust in Jehovah.

<span id="xxxv.ii.v-p7"></span>**4** Blessed is the man who maketh
Jehovah his confidence, And hath not respected the proud, Nor those who
turn aside to lying.

<span id="xxxv.ii.v-p8"></span>**5** Many, O Jehovah, my God! are thy
wonderful works which thou hast done; And thy thoughts towards us it is
impossible to reckon up in order to thee: I will declare and speak \[*of
them;*\] \[But\] they are more than can be told.

<span id="xxxv.ii.v-p9"></span>**6** Sacrifice and oblation thou hast
not taken pleasure in: *But* my ears hast thou made fit:  <span
id="fr_325"></span>[326](#fn_325) Burnt-offering and sin-offering thou
hast not required.

<span id="xxxv.ii.v-p11"></span>**7** Then I said, “Behold! I come; “In
the volume of the book it is written of me,

<span id="xxxv.ii.v-p12"></span>**8** “That I may do thy pleasure, O my
God! “I have desired *to do it*, “And thy law is in the midst of my
bowels.”

<span id="xxxv.ii.v-p13"></span>**9** I have proclaimed thy
righteousness in the assembly great: Behold my lips I will not restrain;
O Jehovah! thou knowest it.

<span id="xxxv.ii.v-p14"></span>**10** Thy righteousness I have not
hidden within my heart; Thy truth and thy salvation I have declared: I
have not concealed thy goodness and thy truth in the assembly great.

<span id="xxxv.ii.v-p15"></span>**11** O thou, Jehovah! withhold not thy
compassions from me; Let thy goodness and thy truth continually preserve
me.

<span id="xxxv.ii.v-p16"></span>**12** For encompassed me have evils
innumerable; Laid hold upon me have my iniquities, *yea in so great
number* that I cannot see them: They are more in number than the hairs
of my head; *And* my heart hath failed me.

<span id="xxxv.ii.v-p17"></span>**13** Let it please thee, O Jehovah! to
deliver me; O Jehovah! to my aid make haste.

<span id="xxxv.ii.v-p18"></span>**14** Let them be put to shame and
confounded together Who seek after my soul to destroy it; Let them be
turned backward and put to shame Who seek after my hurt.

<span id="xxxv.ii.v-p19"></span>**15** Let them be destroyed for a
reward of their shame, Who have said to me, “Aha! aha!”

<span id="xxxv.ii.v-p20"></span>**16** Let all those exult and rejoice
in thee who seek thee; And let those say continually, “May Jehovah be
magnified” — “Those who love thy salvation.

<span id="xxxv.ii.v-p21"></span>**17** But as for me *I am* poor and
needy. Jehovah hath regarded me; My help and my deliverer *art thou*: O
thou, my God! delay not.

<span id="xxxv.ii.vi"></span>

<span id="xxxv.ii.vi-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.ii.vi-p2"></span>PSALM 41

<span id="xxxv.ii.vi-p3"></span>To the Chief Musician. A Psalm of David

<span id="xxxv.ii.vi-p4"></span>**1** Blessed is he who judgeth wisely
of the poor: In the day of evil Jehovah will deliver him.

<span id="xxxv.ii.vi-p5"></span>**2** Jehovah will keep him, and
preserve him alive: He shall be blessed upon the earth: And thou will
not give him up to the desire of his enemies.

<span id="xxxv.ii.vi-p6"></span>**3** Jehovah will support him upon the
bed of sorrow: All his bed thou hast turned in his sickness.

<span id="xxxv.ii.vi-p7"></span>**4** I have said, “O Jehovah! have
mercy upon me; ” “Heal my soul, for I have sinned against thee.”

<span id="xxxv.ii.vi-p8"></span>**5** My enemies have spoken evil of me,
“When will he die, and perish shall his name?“

<span id="xxxv.ii.vi-p9"></span>**6** And if he come to see me falsely
doth he speak; His heart gathereth iniquity to itself’: When he goeth
abroad he speaketh \[*it*.\]

<span id="xxxv.ii.vi-p10"></span>**7** Together against me do all my
haters whisper; Against me do they devise evil for me, \[*saying*,\]

<span id="xxxv.ii.vi-p11"></span>**8** “An evil deed of Belial cleaveth
fast to him; “And he who lieth shall not rise again.”

<span id="xxxv.ii.vi-p12"></span>**9** Even the man of my peace in whom
I trusted, Who eateth of my bread, hath lifted up against me the heel.

<span id="xxxv.ii.vi-p13"></span>**10** Do thou *then*, O Jehovah! have
mercy upon me; Raise me up, and I will recompense them.

<span id="xxxv.ii.vi-p14"></span>**11** By this I have known that I have
been acceptable to thee, Because my enemy shall not triumph over me.

<span id="xxxv.ii.vi-p15"></span>**12** And as for me, in my integrity
thou wilt uphold me, And wilt establish me before thy face for ever.

<span id="xxxv.ii.vi-p16"></span>**13** Blessed *be* Jehovah, the God of
Israel, For ever and ever. Amen and Amen.

<span id="xxxv.ii.vii"></span>

<span id="xxxv.ii.vii-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.ii.vii-p2"></span>PART SECOND.  <span
id="fr_326"></span>[327](#fn_326)

<span id="xxxv.ii.vii-p4"></span>PSALM 42

<span id="xxxv.ii.vii-p5"></span>To the Chief Musician. A lesson of
instruction to the Sons of Korah

<span id="xxxv.ii.vii-p6"></span>**1** As the hart crieth for the
fountains of waters, So my soul crieth for thee, O God!

<span id="xxxv.ii.vii-p7"></span>**2** Thirsted hath my soul for God,
for the living God: When shall I come to appear before the face of God?

<span id="xxxv.ii.vii-p8"></span>**3** To me have my tears been *for*
bread, by day and night, While it is said to me daily, “Where is thy
God?“

<span id="xxxv.ii.vii-p9"></span>**4** When these things I remember, I
pour out within me my soul, Because I had gone with the procession,
Leading them even to the house of God, With the voice of exultation and
praise, — The multitude dancing for joy.

<span id="xxxv.ii.vii-p10"></span>**5** ‘Why art thou cast down, O my
soul! And why art thou disquieted within me? Wait thou for God; for I
shall yet give him thanks, \[*For*\] the salvations of his countenance.

<span id="xxxv.ii.vii-p11"></span>**6** O my God! my soul within me is
cast down, When I remember thee from the land of Jordan and of Hermonim,
From the mountain Mizar.

<span id="xxxv.ii.vii-p12"></span>**7** Deep unto deep calleth at the
noise of thy waterspouts: All thy waves and all thy billows over me have
gone.

<span id="xxxv.ii.vii-p13"></span>**8** By day command will Jehovah his
loving-kindness, And by night his song *shall be* with me, And prayer to
the God of my life.

<span id="xxxv.ii.vii-p14"></span>**9** I will say to God, my Rock, “Why
hast thou forgotten me? “Why mourning do I go because of the oppression
of *my* enemy?”

<span id="xxxv.ii.vii-p15"></span>**10** \[*It is as*\] a wound in my
bones when my enemies reproach me, Saying to me daily, “Where is thy
God?“

<span id="xxxv.ii.vii-p16"></span>**11** Why art thou cast down, O my
soul? And why art thou disquieted within me? Hope in God; for I shall
yet give thanks to him, The salvations of my countenance, and my God.

<span id="xxxv.ii.viii"></span>

<span id="xxxv.ii.viii-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.ii.viii-p2"></span>PSALM 43

<span id="xxxv.ii.viii-p3"></span>**1** Judge me, O God! and plead my
cause: From a people without mercy, from a man deceitful and wicked
deliver me.

<span id="xxxv.ii.viii-p4"></span>**2** For thou *art* the God of my
strength; Why art thou estranged from me? Why mourning do I go because
of the oppression of the enemy?

<span id="xxxv.ii.viii-p5"></span>**3** Send forth thy light and thy
truth; Let them direct me, let them conduct me, To the mountain of thy
holiness, and to thy tabernacles.

<span id="xxxv.ii.viii-p6"></span>**4** And I will go to the altar of
God, To the God of the joy of my rejoicing; And I will celebrate thee
upon the harp, O God, my God!

<span id="xxxv.ii.viii-p7"></span>**5** Why art thou cast down, O my
soul! And why art thou disquieted within me? Hope in God, for I shall
yet celebrate him, *Who is* the salvation of my countenance and my God.

<span id="xxxv.ii.ix"></span>

<span id="xxxv.ii.ix-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.ii.ix-p2"></span>PSALM 44

<span id="xxxv.ii.ix-p3"></span>To the Chief Musician. Of the sons of
Korah. Giving instruction

<span id="xxxv.ii.ix-p4"></span>**1** O God! with our ears we have
heard, Our fathers have told us, The work which thou hast done in their
days, In the days of old.

<span id="xxxv.ii.ix-p5"></span>**2** Thou with thy hand hast expelled
the heathen, and planted them: Thou hast wasted the peoples and
multiplied them:

<span id="xxxv.ii.ix-p6"></span>**3** For not by their own sword
acquired they the land, And their own arm did not save them; But thy
right hand and thy arm, and the light of thy countenance, Because thou
wast favorable to them.

<span id="xxxv.ii.ix-p7"></span>**4** Thou, even thou, *art* my King; O
God! command salvations for Jacob.

<span id="xxxv.ii.ix-p8"></span>**5** Through thee our adversaries with
the horn we have pushed; In thy name we have trampled under foot those
who rise up against us.

<span id="xxxv.ii.ix-p9"></span>**6** For not in my bow will I trust,
And my sword will not save me.

<span id="xxxv.ii.ix-p10"></span>**7** Surely thou hast saved us from
our enemies, And our haters thou hast put to shame.

<span id="xxxv.ii.ix-p11"></span>**8** In God we will boast all the day,
And thy name for ever shall we praise. Selah.

<span id="xxxv.ii.ix-p12"></span>**9** Nevertheless thou hast abhorred
us and put us to shame, And thou goest not forth *any more* with our
armies.

<span id="xxxv.ii.ix-p13"></span>**10** Thou hast made us to turn back
from him that afflicteth us, And our haters have spoiled *us* for
themselves.

<span id="xxxv.ii.ix-p14"></span>**11** Thou hast given us as sheep for
food; And among the heathen thou hast scattered us.

<span id="xxxv.ii.ix-p15"></span>**12** Thou hast sold thy people, and
not become rich, And thou hast not increased the price of them.

<span id="xxxv.ii.ix-p16"></span>**13** Thou hast made us a reproach to
our neighbors, A scorn and derision to those who are round about us.

<span id="xxxv.ii.ix-p17"></span>**14** Thou hast made us a byword among
the heathen, A shaking of the head among the peoples.

<span id="xxxv.ii.ix-p18"></span>**15** Daily *is* my reproach before
me, And the shame of my face hath *quite* covered me,

<span id="xxxv.ii.ix-p19"></span>**16** Because of the voice of him who
reproacheth and revileth, Because of the face of the adversary and
avenger.

<span id="xxxv.ii.ix-p20"></span>**17** All this is come upon us, and we
have not forgotten thee, Nor dealt perfidiously in thy covenant;

<span id="xxxv.ii.ix-p21"></span>**18** Not turned back hath our heart,
Nor declined have our steps from thy path.

<span id="xxxv.ii.ix-p22"></span>**19** Although thou hast crushed us in
the place of dragons, And covered us with the shadow of death.

<span id="xxxv.ii.ix-p23"></span>**20** If we have forgotten the name of
our God, And have spread forth our hands to a God that is strange;

<span id="xxxv.ii.ix-p24"></span>**21** Shall not God search out this?
For he knoweth the secrets of the heart.

<span id="xxxv.ii.ix-p25"></span>**22** Surely for thy sake we are
killed daily; We are accounted as sheep \[*appointed*\] for slaughter.

<span id="xxxv.ii.ix-p26"></span>**23** Arise, why sleepest thou, O
Lord? Awake, do not forget *us* for ever.

<span id="xxxv.ii.ix-p27"></span>**24** Wherefore thy face dost thou
hide? Wilt thou forget our misery and our affliction?

<span id="xxxv.ii.ix-p28"></span>**25** For humbled to the dust is our
soul; Cleave to the earth doth our belly.

<span id="xxxv.ii.ix-p29"></span>**26** Arise for our help, And redeem
us for the sake of thy loving-kindness.

<span id="xxxv.ii.x"></span>

<span id="xxxv.ii.x-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.ii.x-p2"></span>PSALM 45

<span id="xxxv.ii.x-p3"></span>To the Chief Musician. Upon the lilies.
Of the sons of Korah. Giving instruction. A Song of loves

<span id="xxxv.ii.x-p4"></span>**1** Boiling over is my heart to speak a
goodly theme, Speak shall I myself of my works concerning the King: My
tongue is as the pen of a swift writer.

<span id="xxxv.ii.x-p5"></span>**2** Thou art fair above the sons of
men; Diffused is grace on thy lips; Because God hath blessed thee for
ever.

<span id="xxxv.ii.x-p6"></span>**3** Gird thy sword upon thy thigh, O
mighty one! With majesty and glory.

<span id="xxxv.ii.x-p7"></span>**4** And in thy majesty prosper thou;
Ride forth upon the word of truth, and meekness and righteousness; And
thy right hand shall teach thee terrible things:

<span id="xxxv.ii.x-p8"></span>**5** Thy arrows *are* sharp (so that the
people fall under thee) In the hearts of the enemies of the king.

<span id="xxxv.ii.x-p9"></span>**6** Thy throne, O God! *is* for ever
and ever; The scepter of rectitude *is* the scepter of thy kingdom.

<span id="xxxv.ii.x-p10"></span>**7** Thou lovest righteousness and
hatest impiety; Because anointed thee hath God, thy God, With the oil of
gladness above thy fellows.

<span id="xxxv.ii.x-p11"></span>**8** Myrrh, and aloes and cassia
\[*are*\] *in* all thy garments, Out of the ivory palaces, whence they
have made thee glad.

<span id="xxxv.ii.x-p12"></span>**9** The daughters of kings \[*were*\]
among thy maids of honor; Stand did thy consort at thy right hand in
gold of Ophir.

<span id="xxxv.ii.x-p13"></span>**10** Hearken, O daughter! and consider
and incline thy ear; And forget thy people, and the house of thy father.

<span id="xxxv.ii.x-p14"></span>**11** And enamored shall be the King
with thy beauty; For he *is* thy Lord, and thou shalt worship him.

<span id="xxxv.ii.x-p15"></span>**12** And the daughter of Tyre \[*shall
come*\] with a present; Thy favor entreat shall the rich among the
people.

<span id="xxxv.ii.x-p16"></span>**13** All glorious is the daughter of
the King within; Of garments embroidered with gold *is* her clothing.

<span id="xxxv.ii.x-p17"></span>**14** In raiment of needle-work she
shall be brought to the King; Her virgins that follow her, her
companions shall be brought to thee.

<span id="xxxv.ii.x-p18"></span>**15** They shall be brought with joy
and exultation; They shall enter into the palace of the King.

<span id="xxxv.ii.x-p19"></span>**16** Instead of thy fathers shall be
thy children; Thou shalt make them princes in all the earth.

<span id="xxxv.ii.x-p20"></span>**17** I will make thy name to be
remembered throughout all generation; Therefore celebrate thee shall the
peoples for ever and ever.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xi"></span>

<span id="xxxv.ii.xi-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.ii.xi-p2"></span>PSALM 46

<span id="xxxv.ii.xi-p3"></span>To the Chief Musician. Of the sons of
Korah. Upon Alamoth. A Song

<span id="xxxv.ii.xi-p4"></span>**1** God is to us a protection and
strength; A help in troubles he is found exceedingly.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xi-p5"></span>**2** Therefore we will not fear when
moved shall be the earth, And fall shall the mountains into the heart of
the sea.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xi-p6"></span>**3** \[*When*\] roar and rage
tempestuously shall the waters thereof; \[*When*\] shake shall the
mountains with the swelling thereof. Selah.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xi-p7"></span>**4** The streams of her river shall
make glad the city of God, The Sanctuary of the tabernacles of the Most
High.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xi-p8"></span>**5** God *is* in the midst of her; she
shall not be moved: Help her will God at the dawn of the morning.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xi-p9"></span>**6** Rage did the peoples, moved were
the kingdoms: He uttered his voice, melt did the earth.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xi-p10"></span>**7** Jehovah of armies *is* with us; A
fortress for us *is* the God of Jacob. Selah.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xi-p11"></span>**8** Come ye, consider the works of
Jehovah, What desolations he hath wrought in the earth.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xi-p12"></span>**9** He maketh to cease battles, even
to the ends of the earth; He breaketh the bow, he shattereth in pieces
the arms; The chariot he burneth with fire.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xi-p13"></span>**10** Be still and know that I am God:
I will be exalted among the heathen; I will be exalted in the earth.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xi-p14"></span>**11** Jehovah of armies is with us; A
fortress for us *is* the God of Jacob. Selah.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xii"></span>

<span id="xxxv.ii.xii-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.ii.xii-p2"></span>PSALM 47

<span id="xxxv.ii.xii-p3"></span>To the Chief Musician. Of the sons of
Korah. Upon Alamoth. A Song

<span id="xxxv.ii.xii-p4"></span>**1** O all ye peoples! clap the hand;
Shout unto God with the voice of exultation;

<span id="xxxv.ii.xii-p5"></span>**2** For Jehovah *is* high, terrible,
A great king over all the earth.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xii-p6"></span>**3** He hath put in order the people
under us, And the nations under our feet.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xii-p7"></span>**4** He hath chosen for us our
inheritance, The glory of Jacob, whom he hath loved. Selah.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xii-p8"></span>**5** Gone up is God with a shout,
Jehovah with the sound of a trumpet.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xii-p9"></span>**6** Sing psalms to God, sing psalms;
Sing psalms to our King, sing psalms;

<span id="xxxv.ii.xii-p10"></span>**7** For king of all the earth is
God; Sing praises, all ye who understand!

<span id="xxxv.ii.xii-p11"></span>**8** The kingdom he hath obtained
over the heathen; God sitteth upon the throne of his holiness.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xii-p12"></span>**9** The princes of the peoples are
assembled together To the people of the God of Abraham: For to God
belong the shields of the earth: He is greatly exalted.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xiii"></span>

<span id="xxxv.ii.xiii-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.ii.xiii-p2"></span>PSALM 48

<span id="xxxv.ii.xiii-p3"></span>A Song of a Psalm. Of the sons of
Korah

<span id="xxxv.ii.xiii-p4"></span>**1** Great is Jehovah and to be
praised greatly In the city of our God, in the mountain of his holiness.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xiii-p5"></span>**2** Beautiful for situation, the joy
of the whole earth, The mountain of Zion, on the sides of the north, The
city of the great King.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xiii-p6"></span>**3** God in her palaces is known for
a defense.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xiii-p7"></span>**4** For behold! the kings assembled,
They passed away together.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xiii-p8"></span>**5** They themselves saw, so they
marveled; They were frightened, they fled precipitately,

<span id="xxxv.ii.xiii-p9"></span>**6** Fear seized upon them there,
Pain as of one in travail.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xiii-p10"></span>**7** By the east wind thou breakest
in pieces the ships of Tarshish.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xiii-p11"></span>**8** As we have heard, so have we
seen In the city of Jehovah of Hosts, In the city of our God: God will
establish it for ever. Selah

<span id="xxxv.ii.xiii-p12"></span>**9** We have waited, O God! for thy
mercy In the midst of thy temple,

<span id="xxxv.ii.xiii-p13"></span>**10** As *is* thy name, O God! So
*is* thy praise unto the ends of the earth: Of righteousness full is thy
right hand.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xiii-p14"></span>**11** Rejoice shall Mount Zion,
Exult shall the daughters of Judah, Because of thy judgments.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xiii-p15"></span>**12** Encompass Zion, and walk round
about her. Number the towers thereof,

<span id="xxxv.ii.xiii-p16"></span>**13** Set your heart to her walls,
Exalt her towers, That ye may make report to the generations to come.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xiii-p17"></span>**14** For this God is our God for
ever and ever: He will be our guide even unto death.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xiv"></span>

<span id="xxxv.ii.xiv-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.ii.xiv-p2"></span>PSALM 49

<span id="xxxv.ii.xiv-p3"></span>To the Chief Musician. Of the sons of
Korah. A Psalm

<span id="xxxv.ii.xiv-p4"></span>**1** Hear this all ye peoples; Give
ear all ye inhabitants of the world:

<span id="xxxv.ii.xiv-p5"></span>**2** Both ye sons of Adam, and ye sons
of men, Rich and poor together.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xiv-p6"></span>**3** My mouth shall speak of wisdoms,
And the meditation of my heart is of understanding.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xiv-p7"></span>**4** I will incline to a parable my
ear: I will open upon the harp my enigma.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xiv-p8"></span>**5** Wherefore should I fear in the
days of evil? The iniquity of my heel shall compass me about.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xiv-p9"></span>**6** They trust in their wealth, And
in the multitude of their riches do glory.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xiv-p10"></span>**7** The brother shall not be able to
redeem; None shall give to God the price of his redemption.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xiv-p11"></span>**8** And precious shall be the
redemption of their soul, And *their* continuance for ever:

<span id="xxxv.ii.xiv-p12"></span>**9** That he should still live for
ever, And not see the grave.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xiv-p13"></span>**10** For he shall see that wise men
die, Together the fool and the brutish person shall perish, And leave to
strangers their wealth.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xiv-p14"></span>**11** Their inward thought is \[*how
to make*\] their houses \[*to continue*\] for ever, Their
dwelling-places from generation to generation: They have called out
their names upon the earth.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xiv-p15"></span>**12** And man in honor shall not
abide; He hath become like the beasts: they perish.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xiv-p16"></span>**13** This their way *is* foolishness
in them, And their posterity in their saying will acquiesce. Selah.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xiv-p17"></span>**14** Like sleep in the grave they
are laid; Death shall feed them; And have dominion over them shall the
upright in the morning, And their strength shall wax old; The grave
*shall receive* them from their dwelling.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xiv-p18"></span>**15** But God shall redeem my soul
from the hand of the grave; For he hath taken me up. Selah.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xiv-p19"></span>**16** Be not thou afraid when a man
shall become rich, When increased shall be the glory of his house;

<span id="xxxv.ii.xiv-p20"></span>**17** For he shall not at his death
carry all away: Descend not after him shall his glory:

<span id="xxxv.ii.xiv-p21"></span>**18** For his soul in his lifetime he
will bless, And they shall praise thee when thou doest well to thyself.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xiv-p22"></span>**19** He shall come to the age of his
fathers, Even for ever he shall not see the light.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xiv-p23"></span>**20** Man *is* in honor, and will not
understand: He hath become like the beasts: they shall perish.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xv"></span>

<span id="xxxv.ii.xv-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.ii.xv-p2"></span>PSALM 50

<span id="xxxv.ii.xv-p3"></span>A Song, of Asaph

<span id="xxxv.ii.xv-p4"></span>**1** The God of gods, Jehovah hath
spoken, And called the earth From the rising of the sun unto the going
down thereof.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xv-p5"></span>**2** Out of Zion, the Perfection of
beauty, God hath shined.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xv-p6"></span>**3** Come shall our God, and shall not
keep silence; A fire before him shall devour, And round about him a
tempest shall rage exceedingly.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xv-p7"></span>**4** He shall call to the heavens from
above, And to the earth, to judge his people.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xv-p8"></span>**5** “Gather together to me my meek
ones, (*will he say*), “Those who strike a covenant with me over
sacrifices.”

<span id="xxxv.ii.xv-p9"></span>**6** And declare shall the heavens his
righteousness: For God is judge himself. Selah.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xv-p10"></span>**7** “Hear, O my people! and I will
speak; “O Israel! and I will announce to thee: “God, \[*even*\] thy God
am I.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xv-p11"></span>**8** “Not for thy sacrifices will I
reprove thee; “And thy burnt-offerings *are* before me continually.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xv-p12"></span>**9** “I will not take out of thy house
a calf, “*Nor* out of thy folds he-goats:

<span id="xxxv.ii.xv-p13"></span>**10** “For mine are all the beasts of
the forest, “The cattle upon a thousand hills.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xv-p14"></span>**11** “I know all the birds of the
mountains; “And the wild beasts of the field are at my command.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xv-p15"></span>**12** “If I am hungry, I will not tell
thee: “For mine is the world and the fullness thereof.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xv-p16"></span>**13** “Will I eat the flesh of bulls,
“And the blood of goats will I drink?

<span id="xxxv.ii.xv-p17"></span>**14** “Sacrifice unto God praise, “And
pay unto the Most High thy vows.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xv-p18"></span>**15** “Call upon me in the day of
trouble; “I will deliver thee, and thou shalt glorify me.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xv-p19"></span>**16** “But unto the wicked said hath
God, “What hast thou to do to declare my statutes, “\[*Or*\] that thou
shouldest take my covenant into thy lips?

<span id="xxxv.ii.xv-p20"></span>**17** “Also thou hatest correction,
“And castest my words behind thee.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xv-p21"></span>**18** “If thou seest a thief, thou
wilt run with him, “And with adulterers is thy portion.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xv-p22"></span>**19** “Thy mouth thou puttest forth to
evil, “And thy tongue frameth deceit,

<span id="xxxv.ii.xv-p23"></span>**20** “Thou wilt sit against thy
brother; “Thou wilt speak against the sons of thy mother; “Thou wilt set
forth slander.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xv-p24"></span>**21** “These things thou hast done,
and I kept silence; “Thou thoughtest that I would be like thyself’: “I
will reprove thee, and set them in order before thine eyes.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xv-p25"></span>**22** “Now consider this, ye who
forget God, “Lest I seize upon you and there be none to deliver.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xv-p26"></span>**23** “He who sacrificeth praise will
glorify me: “And he who ordereth his way to him will I show the
salvation of God.”

<span id="xxxv.ii.xvi"></span>

<span id="xxxv.ii.xvi-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.ii.xvi-p2"></span>PSALM 51

<span id="xxxv.ii.xvi-p3"></span>To the Chief Musician. A Psalm of
David, when Nathan the prophet came to him, after he had gone in to
Bathsheba

<span id="xxxv.ii.xvi-p4"></span>**1** Have pity upon me, O God!
according to thy mercy; According to the multitude of thy compassions
blot out my iniquities.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xvi-p5"></span>**2** Multiply to wash me from my sin,
And from my wickedness do thou cleanse me.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xvi-p6"></span>**3** For my sins I know, And my
wickedness is before me continually.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xvi-p7"></span>**4** Against thee, against thee only,
have I sinned, And that which was displeasing in thy sight have I done;
That thou mayest be justified when thou speakest, And be pure in giving
judgment.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xvi-p8"></span>**5** Behold in iniquity I was born,
And in sin conceive me did my mother.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xvi-p9"></span>**6** Behold, truth thou hast loved in
the inmost parts, And in secret, wisdom thou hast made me know.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xvi-p10"></span>**7** Thou shalt purge me with hyssop,
and I shall be clean; Thou shalt wash me, and I shall be whiter than
snow.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xvi-p11"></span>**8** Make me to hear joy and
gladness; And exult shall the bones which thou hast broken.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xvi-p12"></span>**9** Hide thy face from my sins, And
all my iniquities blot out.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xvi-p13"></span>**10** A heart \[*that is*\] clean
create in me, O God! And a spirit \[*that is*\] right renew in my inward
parts.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xvi-p14"></span>**11** Cast me not away from thy face,
And the Spirit of thy holiness take not from me.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xvi-p15"></span>**12** Restore to me the joy of thy
salvation, And with a free spirit uphold me.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xvi-p16"></span>**13** I will teach transgressors thy
ways, the ungodly to time shall be converted.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xvi-p17"></span>**14** Deliver me from bloods, O God!
O God of my salvation! And sing aloud shall my tongue of thy
righteousness.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xvi-p18"></span>**15** O Lord! my lips do thou open,
And my mouth shall show forth thy praise.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xvi-p19"></span>**16** For thou wilt not accept a
sacrifice; Though I should give a burnt-offering, it would not please
thee.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xvi-p20"></span>**17** The sacrifices of God are an
afflicted spirit: A heart afflicted and contrite, O God! thou wilt not
despise.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xvi-p21"></span>**18** Do good in thy good pleasure to
Zion; Build thou the walls of Jerusalem.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xvi-p22"></span>**19** Then shalt thou accept the
sacrifices of righteousness, The burnt-offering and oblation;  <span
id="fr_327"></span>[328](#fn_327) Then shall come upon thy altar calves.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xvii"></span>

<span id="xxxv.ii.xvii-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.ii.xvii-p2"></span>PSALM 52

<span id="xxxv.ii.xvii-p3"></span>To the Chief Musician. A lesson of
instruction of David: when Doeg the Edomite came and told Saul, and said
to him, that David had come into the house of Abimelech

<span id="xxxv.ii.xvii-p4"></span>**1** Why dost thou glory in thy
wickedness, O mighty man? The goodness of God *continueth* daily.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xvii-p5"></span>**2** Thy tongue reckoneth up
mischiefs, Like a razor \[*that is*\] sharp working deceitfully.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xvii-p6"></span>**3** Thou lovest wickedness more than
goodness; Falsehood more than to speak righteousness. Selah.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xvii-p7"></span>**4** Thou lovest all words of deceit,
O thou tongue of guilefulness!

<span id="xxxv.ii.xvii-p8"></span>**5** Likewise God shall destroy thee
for ever: He shall lay hold on thee and pluck thee out of thy
tabernacle, And root thee out of the land of the living. Selah.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xvii-p9"></span>**6** See it also shall the righteous
ones, and shall fear, And at him they shall laugh.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xvii-p10"></span>**7** Behold! the man who made not
God his strength; And trusted in the abundance of his riches, And was
strong in his wickedness.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xvii-p11"></span>**8** But as for me *I shall be* like
an olive-tree \[*that is*\] green in the house of God: I have trusted in
the goodness of God for ever and ever.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xvii-p12"></span>**9** I will celebrate thee for ever,
because thou hast done \[*it*:\]  <span
id="fr_328"></span>[329](#fn_328) I will wait on thy name, For it is
good in the presence of thy meek ones.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xviii"></span>

<span id="xxxv.ii.xviii-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.ii.xviii-p2"></span>PSALM 53

<span id="xxxv.ii.xviii-p3"></span>To the Chief Musician, upon Mahalath.
A lesson of instruction ofDavid

<span id="xxxv.ii.xviii-p4"></span>**1** The fool hath said in his
heart, “There is not a God:” They have corrupted \[*all good order*,\]
they have done abominable work: There is none who doeth good.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xviii-p5"></span>**2** God from heaven looked down
upon the sons of men, To see if there was any who did understand, Who
did seek after God.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xviii-p6"></span>**3** Every one of them hath gone
back; They have all together become corrupt: There is none that doeth
good, not even one.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xviii-p7"></span>**4** Have they no knowledge, all
*these* workers of iniquity? Eating my people \[*as*\] they eat bread:
Upon Jehovah they have not called.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xviii-p8"></span>**5** There were they afraid with
fear, where there was not fear; For scattered hath Jehovah the bones of
him that encampeth against thee: Thou hast put them to shame because God
hath despised them.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xviii-p9"></span>**6** Who shall give out of Zion
deliverance to Israel? When bring back shall God the captivity of his
people, Rejoice shall Jacob, exult shall Israel.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xix"></span>

<span id="xxxv.ii.xix-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.ii.xix-p2"></span>PSALM 54

<span id="xxxv.ii.xix-p3"></span>To the Chief Musician, on Neginoth. A
lesson of instruction of David. When the Ziphims came and said to Saul,
“Doth not David hide himself with us?”

<span id="xxxv.ii.xix-p4"></span>**1** O God! by thy name save me, And
by thy strength judge me.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xix-p5"></span>**2** O God! hear my prayer, Give ear
to the words of my mouth.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xix-p6"></span>**3** For strangers have risen up
against me, And terrible ones have sought after my soul: They have not
set God before them. Selah.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xix-p7"></span>**4** Behold! God is a helper to me;
The Lord is with those who uphold my soul.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xix-p8"></span>**5** He shall repay evil to my
adversaries: In thy truth cut them off.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xix-p9"></span>**6** Willingly will I sacrifice to
thee; I will celebrate thy name, O Jehovah! for it is good.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xix-p10"></span>**7** For out of all trouble he hath
delivered me; And \[*punishment*\] upon my adversaries mine eye hath
seen.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xx"></span>

<span id="xxxv.ii.xx-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.ii.xx-p2"></span>PSALM 55

<span id="xxxv.ii.xx-p3"></span>To the Chief Musician on Neginoth. A
lesson of instruction of David

<span id="xxxv.ii.xx-p4"></span>**1** Give ear, O God! to my prayer, And
hide not thyself from my supplication.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xx-p5"></span>**2** Attend to me, and answer me: I
will wail in my address, and will become tumultuous.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xx-p6"></span>**3** By reason of the voice of the
enemy — Under the oppression of the ungodly; For they cast upon me
iniquity, In wrath they set themselves against me.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xx-p7"></span>**4** My heart trembleth within me, And
the terrors of death have fallen upon me.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xx-p8"></span>**5** Fear and trembling are come upon
me, And horror hath overwhelmed me.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xx-p9"></span>**6** And I said, “Who will give me
wings like a dove? “I will fly away and be at rest.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xx-p10"></span>**7** “Lo! I will flee far away, “I
will repose in the desert. Selah.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xx-p11"></span>**8** “I will hasten my escape from the
tempestuous whirlwind.”

<span id="xxxv.ii.xx-p12"></span>**9** Destroy, O Lord! divide their
tongue: For I have seen oppression and strife in the city.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xx-p13"></span>**10** By day and night they go round
it upon the walls thereof: And labor and sorrow are in the midst of it.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xx-p14"></span>**11** Wickedness  <span
id="fr_329"></span>[330](#fn_329) is in the midst of it; And fraud and
deceit depart not from the streets thereof.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xx-p16"></span>**12** Truly it was not an enemy who
reproached me, For \[*then*\] I could have borne \[*it*:\] *It was* not
an adversary who magnified himself against me, For \[*then*\] I would
have hid himself from him.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xx-p17"></span>**13** But thou, a man according to my
own rank, My guide, and my familiar friend.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xx-p18"></span>**14** We sweetly exchanged our secret
thoughts; Into the house of God we walked in company.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xx-p19"></span>**15** Let death seize upon them, Let
them descend into the grave alive; For wickedness  <span
id="fr_330"></span>[331](#fn_330) *is* I, their dwelling, in the midst
of them.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xx-p21"></span>**16** As for me, to God; will I cry,
And Jehovah shall save me.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xx-p22"></span>**17** In the evening, and the morning,
and at noonday Will I pray, and cry aloud; And he shall hear my voice.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xx-p23"></span>**18** He hath redeemed into peace my
soul From the battle which was against me: For many were with me.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xx-p24"></span>**19** Hear shall God, and shall
afflict them, Even he who sitteth from ancient time. Selah. Because they
have no changes, And fear not God.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xx-p25"></span>**20** He hath set his hands against
those who were at peace with him: He hath broken his covenant.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xx-p26"></span>**21** Smoother than butter are the
words of his mouth, And *in* his heart *is* war; Softer are his words
than oil, And \[*yet*\] they *are* darts.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xx-p27"></span>**22** Cast upon Jehovah whatever
blessings thou askest from him,  <span id="fr_331"></span>[332](#fn_331)
And he shall feed thee; He shall not suffer for ever the righteous man
to stagger.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xx-p29"></span>**23** Thou, O God! shalt cast them
into the pit of corruption: The men of blood and deceit shall not live
out half their days: But as for me, I will hope in thee.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxi"></span>

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxi-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxi-p2"></span>PSALM 56

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxi-p3"></span>To the Chief Musician upon, the silent
dove in distant places. Michtam of David, when the Philistines took him
in Gath

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxi-p4"></span>**1** Have mercy upon me, O God, For
swallow me up doth man; He daily assaulting doth oppress me.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxi-p5"></span>**2** Swallow me up do *my* enemies
daily: Truly many *strive* to oppress me, *O Jehovah*, Most High!

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxi-p6"></span>**3** In the day when I was afraid, I
in thee did trust.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxi-p7"></span>**4** In God I will praise his word; In
God have I trusted; I will not fear what flesh can do to me.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxi-p8"></span>**5** Every day my words disquiet me;
Against me *are* all their thoughts for evil.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxi-p9"></span>**6** They assemble together, they hide
themselves, My heels they watch, Because they desire my soul.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxi-p10"></span>**7** In *their* iniquity *they think*
there is escape for them: In *thy* wrath the peoples thou wilt cast
down, O God!

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxi-p11"></span>**8** My wanderings thou numbereth,
even thou: Put my tears into thy bottle; Are they not in thy register?

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxi-p12"></span>**9** Then my enemies shall be turned
back in the day when I cry: This I know, because God is with me.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxi-p13"></span>**10** In God will I praise \[*his*\]
word; In Jehovah will I praise \[*his*\] word.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxi-p14"></span>**11** In God have I trusted; I will
not fear what man can do to me.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxi-p15"></span>**12** Upon me, O God! are thy vows, I
will render praises to thee.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxi-p16"></span>**13** For thou hast delivered my soul
from death: Hast thou not *also delivered* my feet from falling? That I
may walk before God in the light of the living.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxii"></span>

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxii-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxii-p2"></span>PSALM 57

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxii-p3"></span>To the Chief Musician. Destroy not.
Michtam of David. When he fled from the face of Saul in the cave

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxii-p4"></span>**1** Have mercy upon me, O God! have
mercy upon me; For in thee my soul doth trust; And in the shadow of thy
wings will I hope, Until iniquity pass away.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxii-p5"></span>**2** I will cry to God Most High, Who
perfecteth \[*his work*\] towards me.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxii-p6"></span>**3** He shall send from Heaven, And
shall save me from the reproach of him who swalloweth me up: Send forth
shall God his mercy and his truth.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxii-p7"></span>**4** My soul is in the midst of
lions; I lie among those who are set on fire, — Among the sons of men,
whose teeth are spears and arrows, And their tongue a sword \[*that
is*\] sharp.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxii-p8"></span>**5** Be thou exalted above the
heavens, O God! Above all the earth thy glory.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxii-p9"></span>**6** A net they have prepared for my
steps: Bowed down is my soul: They have digged before me a pit, *But*
they have fallen into it. Selah

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxii-p10"></span>**7** Prepared *is* my heart, O God!
prepared *is* my heart: I will sing, and chant psalms.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxii-p11"></span>**8** Awake my tongue, awake nablum
 <span id="fr_332"></span>[333](#fn_332) and harp: I will awake at dawn
of day.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxii-p13"></span>**9** I will celebrate thee, among
the peoples, O Lord! I will sing psalms to thee among the nation:

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxii-p14"></span>**10** For great unto the heavens is
thy goodness, And unto the clouds thy truth.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxii-p15"></span>**11** Be thou exalted, above the
heavens, O God! Above all the earth thy glory.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxiii"></span>

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxiii-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxiii-p2"></span>PSALM 58

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxiii-p3"></span>To the Chief Musician. Destroy not.
Michtam of David

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxiii-p4"></span>**1** Do ye indeed, O ye
congregation! speak righteousness? Uprightly do ye judge? O ye sons of
men!

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxiii-p5"></span>**2** Yea rather in *your* heart
wickedness ye plot, On the earth violence your hands weigh out.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxiii-p6"></span>**3** Estranged are the ungodly from
the womb, They have gone astray from their birth speaking falsehood.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxiii-p7"></span>**4** They have poison like the
poison of a serpent, \[*They are*\] like the deaf adder which stoppeth
her ear;

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxiii-p8"></span>**5** Which listeneth not to the
voice of the enchanter, — Of him who exerciseth enchantment skillfully.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxiii-p9"></span>**6** O God! break their teeth in
their mouth: The jawbones of the lions break, O Jehovah!

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxiii-p10"></span>**7** Let them melt away like water,
let them be gone: Let them bend their bow, and let their arrows be as if
broken.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxiii-p11"></span>**8** Like a snail which melteth
away let them vanish; Like the untimely birth of a woman which doth not
see the sun.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxiii-p12"></span>**9** Before your pots can feel the
fire of the bramble, *Like* flesh yet raw as a whirlwind he shall carry
him away.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxiii-p13"></span>**10** Rejoice shall the righteous
when he seeth the vengeance; His hands he shall wash in the blood of the
ungodly.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxiii-p14"></span>**11** And men  <span
id="fr_333"></span>[334](#fn_333) shall say, “Truly there is fruit for
the righteous, “Truly there is a God who judgeth in the earth.”

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxiv"></span>

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxiv-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxiv-p2"></span>PSALM 59

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxiv-p3"></span>To the Chief Musician. Destroy not.
Michtam of David. When Saul sent, and they watched the house to kill him

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxiv-p4"></span>**1** Deliver me from my enemies, O my
God! from those who rise up against me set me on high.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxiv-p5"></span>**2** Deliver me from the workers of
iniquity, And from men of bloods save me:

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxiv-p6"></span>**3** For lo! they have laid snares
for my soul; Gathered together against me have the strong men; Not
\[*for*\] my sin, nor \[*for*\] my wickedness, O Jehovah!

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxiv-p7"></span>**4** Without *any* iniquity *of mine*
they have run and prepared themselves. Awake and come to meet me, and
behold.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxiv-p8"></span>**5** And thou, O Jehovah, God of
armies! the God of Israel! Awake to visit all the nations; Do not have
compassion upon any who transgress wickedly. Selah.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxiv-p9"></span>**6** They will return at evening;
They will make a noise like a dog, And go round about the city.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxiv-p10"></span>**7** Behold they will prate with
their mouth; Swords are in their lips; “For who,” *say they*, “will
hear?”

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxiv-p11"></span>**8** But thou, O Jehovah! shalt
laugh at them; Thou shalt hold in derision all the nations.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxiv-p12"></span>**9** His strength with thee I will
put in trust; For God is my fortress.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxiv-p13"></span>**10** The God of my mercy shall
prevent me; God will make me see my desire upon my enemies.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxiv-p14"></span>**11** Slay them not, lest my people
should forget; Make them to wander by thy power; And bring them down, O
Lord, our shield!

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxiv-p15"></span>**12** The sin of their mouth, the
words of their lips: Let them be taken in their pride: of cursing and
lying let them speak.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxiv-p16"></span>**13** Consume, in thy fury consume
them, that they may be no more; And let men know that God ruleth in
Jacob, Even to the ends of the earth. Selah.  <span
id="fr_334"></span>[335](#fn_334)

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxiv-p19"></span>**14** And they will return at
evening; They will bark like a dog, And go round about the city.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxiv-p20"></span>**15** They will wander up and down
for food; If they be not satisfied they will even stay all night.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxiv-p21"></span>**16** But as for me, I will sing of
thy strength, I will praise in the morning thy mercy; For thou hast been
a fortress to me, And a refuge in the day of my trouble.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxiv-p22"></span>**17** My strength is with thee, I
will sing psalms; For God *is* my fortress, the God of my mercy.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxv"></span>

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxv-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxv-p2"></span>PSALM 60

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxv-p3"></span>To the Chief Musician upon Shushan
Eduth. Michtam of David to teach. When he fought against the Syrians of
Mesopotamia and against the Syrians of Zobah; and when Joab, having
returned, smote of the Edomites in the Valley of Salt twelve thousand

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxv-p4"></span>**1** O God! thou hast cast us off,
thou hast scattered us; Thou hast been angry, O return to us!

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxv-p5"></span>**2** To tremble thou hast made the
earth; Thou hast caused it to open wide; Heal the breaches thereof for
it shaketh.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxv-p6"></span>**3** Thou hast showed to thy people a
hard thing, Thou hast made us drunk with the wine of stupefaction.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxv-p7"></span>**4** Thou hast given to those who fear
thee a banner, That it may be displayed before *thy* truth. Selah.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxv-p8"></span>**5** That thy beloved ones may be
delivered, Save with thy right hand and hear me.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxv-p9"></span>**6** God hath spoken in his holiness;
I will rejoice: I will divide Shechem, And the valley of Succoth I will
measure.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxv-p10"></span>**7** Mine *shall be* Gilead, and mine
*shall be* Manasseh; And Ephraim *shall be* the strength of my head;
Judah, my lawgiver.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxv-p11"></span>**8** Moab *shall be* the pot for my
washing; Over Edom will I cast my shoe; O Palestina! triumph thou over
me.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxv-p12"></span>**9** Who will bring me into the city
fortified? Who will lead me into Edom?

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxv-p13"></span>**10** Wilt not thou, O God! who hadst
cast us off? \[*thou*\] O God! \[*who*\] didst not go forth with our
armies?

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxv-p14"></span>**11** Grant us relief from trouble,
For vain *is* the help of man.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxv-p15"></span>**12** Through God we shall do
valiantly: And he it is who shall tread down our adversaries.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxvi"></span>

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxvi-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxvi-p2"></span>PSALM 61

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxvi-p3"></span>To the Chief Musician upon Neginoth. A
Psalm of David

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxvi-p4"></span>**1** Hear, O God! my cry, Attend to
my prayer.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxvi-p5"></span>**2** From the end of the earth to
thee will I cry, when vexed is my heart: To the rock which is higher
than I thou shalt lead me.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxvi-p6"></span>**3** For thou hast been a hope to me,
A tower of strength from the face of the enemy.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxvi-p7"></span>**4** I will dwell in thy tabernacle
for ever; I will be safe under the covert of thy wings. Selah.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxvi-p8"></span>**5** For thou, O God! hast heard my
vows: Thou hast given an inheritance to those who fear thy name.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxvi-p9"></span>**6** Days upon days to the king thou
shalt add, His years *shall be* as many generations.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxvi-p10"></span>**7** He shall dwell for ever in the
presence of God: Mercy and truth do thou prepare: thou shalt preserve
him.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxvi-p11"></span>**8** So will I sing unto thy name
for ever, That I may perform my vows every day.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxvii"></span>

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxvii-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxvii-p2"></span>PSALM 62

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxvii-p3"></span>To the Chief Musician upon Jeduthun.
A Psalm of David

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxvii-p4"></span>**1** Nevertheless towards God silent
is my soul: From him is my salvation.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxvii-p5"></span>**2** Nevertheless he is my reek and
my salvation, My fortress: *therefore* I shall not be moved greatly.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxvii-p6"></span>**3** How long will ye continue to
lay snares against a man? Ye shall be slain all of you: As an inclining
wall shall ye be, and a fence that is shaken.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxvii-p7"></span>**4** Yet from his elevation they
consult to east him down: They delight in falsehood: With their mouth
they bless, And in their hearts they curse. Selah.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxvii-p8"></span>**5** Nevertheless towards God be
thou silent O my soul: For from him *is* my expectation.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxvii-p9"></span>**6** Nevertheless he *only is* my
rock, and my salvation: My fortress; I shall not fall.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxvii-p10"></span>**7** In God *is* my salvation and
my glory; The rock of my strength; my hope *is* in God.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxvii-p11"></span>**8** Hope in him at all times, O ye
people! Pour out before his face your hearts: God *is* our hope. Selah.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxvii-p12"></span>**9** Nevertheless vanity are the
sons of Adam; A lie the sons of men: When put all together in a balance
they are found lighter than vanity itself.  <span
id="fr_335"></span>[336](#fn_335)

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxvii-p14"></span>**10** Trust not in oppression and
robbery; be not vain: \[*Upon*\] riches if they abound set not your
heart.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxvii-p15"></span>**11** Once God hath spoken; Twice
this I have heard, “That power belongeth to God;” And to thee, O Lord!
*belongeth* mercy; Truly thou wilt render to every man according to his
work.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxviii"></span>

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxviii-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxviii-p2"></span>PSALM 63

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxviii-p3"></span>A Psalm of David, when he was in the
wilderness of Judea

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxviii-p4"></span>**1** O God! my God art thou; Early
will I seek thee: Thirsted for thee hath my soul, Longed for thee hath
my flesh, In this land \[*that is*\] inhospitable and dry, without
water.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxviii-p5"></span>**2** Thus in the sanctuary have I
beheld thee, To see thy power and thy glory.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxviii-p6"></span>**3** Because better *is* thy mercy
than life, My lips shall praise thee.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxviii-p7"></span>**4** Thus will I bless thee in my
life; In thy name I will lift up my hands.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxviii-p8"></span>**5** As with marrow and farness
satisfied shall be my soul, And with lips of rejoicing shall my mouth
praise *thee*

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxviii-p9"></span>**6** Surely I will remember thee
upon my bed; In the watches *of the night* I will meditate upon thee;

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxviii-p10"></span>**7** Because thou hast been a help
to me: And in the shadow of thy wings I will shout for joy.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxviii-p11"></span>**8** Cleaved hath my soul to
\[*literally after*\] thee; Sustain me shall thy right hand.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxviii-p12"></span>**9** And they whilst they seek to
destroy my soul, Shall go into the lowest parts of the earth.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxviii-p13"></span>**10** They shall east him down to
the edge of the sword: The portion of foxes they shall be.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxviii-p14"></span>**11** But the king shall rejoice
in God, And glory shall every one who sweareth by him: For stopped shall
be the mouth of those who speak falsehood.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxix"></span>

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxix-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxix-p2"></span>PSALM 64

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxix-p3"></span>To the Chief Musician. A Psalm of
David

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxix-p4"></span>**1** Hear, O God! my voice in my
prayer: From fear of the enemy preserve my life.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxix-p5"></span>**2** Hide me from the counsel of
malignant men — From the assembly of tire workers of iniquity.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxix-p6"></span>**3** For they have sharpened as a
sword their tongue; They have directed for their arrow a bitter word.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxix-p7"></span>**4** To shoot in secret at the
innocent man: Suddenly they will shoot and not fear.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxix-p8"></span>**5** They encourage themselves in an
impious action; They talk together of secretly laying snares; They say,
“Who shall see them?”

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxix-p9"></span>**6** They have searched out
iniquities, They have accomplished a searching search: And the inward
part of each of them and the heart \[*is*\] deep.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxix-p10"></span>**7** But God shall shoot at them an
arrow; Suddenly shall they be wounded.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxix-p11"></span>**8** And they shall make their own
tongue fall upon themselves, And flee away shall all who see them.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxix-p12"></span>**9** And see shall all men, and
shall declare the work of God, And his doing they shall understand.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxix-p13"></span>**10** Rejoice shall the righteous in
Jehovah, and they shall hope in him; And glory shall all the upright in
heart.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxx"></span>

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxx-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxx-p2"></span>PSALM 65

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxx-p3"></span>To the Chief Musician. A Psalm of
David. A Song

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxx-p4"></span>**1** For thee waiteth praise, O God!
in Zion; And to thee performed shall be the vow.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxx-p5"></span>**2** O thou who hearest prayer! To
thee shall all flesh come.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxx-p6"></span>**3** Words of iniquity  <span
id="fr_336"></span>[337](#fn_336) have prevailed against me: Our crimes
thou shalt expiate.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxx-p8"></span>**4** Blessed is he whom thou wilt
choose, and cause to approach to thee; He shall dwell in thy courts: We
shall be satisfied with the goodness of thy house — Of the sanctuary of
thy palace.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxx-p9"></span>**5** Terrible things in righteousness
wilt thou answer us, O God of our salvation! The hope of all the ends of
the earth, And of the far off places of the sea.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxx-p10"></span>**6** Establishing the mountains by
his power,  <span id="fr_337"></span>[338](#fn_337) Being girded with
might.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxx-p12"></span>**7** Stilling the noise of the seas,
And the noise of their waves, the tumults of the nations.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxx-p13"></span>**8** And afraid shall be the dwellers
in the ends *of the earth* at thy signs; The outgoings of the morning
and evening thou shalt make to shout for joy.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxx-p14"></span>**9** Thou hast visited the earth, and
watered her; Thou hast abundantly enriched her: The river of God is full
of waters: Thou wilt prepare their corn, For so thou hast prepared her.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxx-p15"></span>**10** Her furrows thou dost saturate,
Thou makest the rain to fall into her ridges, With showers thou dost
moisten her, Her buddings thou dost bless.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxx-p16"></span>**11** Thou crownest the year with thy
beneficence, And thy paths will drop fatness.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxx-p17"></span>**12** They drop upon the dwellings of
the wilderness; And with gladness the hills shall be girded.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxx-p18"></span>**13** Clothed are the pastures with
flocks; And the valleys are covered with corn; They shout for joy, they
also sing.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxxi"></span>

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxxi-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxxi-p2"></span>PSALM 66

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxxi-p3"></span>To the Chief Justice,. A Song of a
Psalm

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxxi-p4"></span>**1** Shout joyfully to God all the
earth,

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxxi-p5"></span>**2** Sing the glory of his name, Make
glorious his praise.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxxi-p6"></span>**3** Say unto God: “How terrible art
thou in thy works! “Through the greatness of thy power shall thy enemies
feign submission unto thee.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxxi-p7"></span>**4** “All the earth shall worship
thee, and shall sing to thee, “They shall hymn thy name.” Selah.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxxi-p8"></span>**5** Come ye, and see the works of
God: He is terrible in his doing towards the sons of men.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxxi-p9"></span>**6** He turned the sea into dry
*land*; Through the river  <span id="fr_338"></span>[339](#fn_338) they
passed on foot; There we were glad in him.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxxi-p11"></span>**7** He ruleth by his might over the
world;  <span id="fr_339"></span>[340](#fn_339) His eyes upon the
nations are fixed: The rebels shall not exalt themselves. Selah.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxxi-p13"></span>**8** Bless, O ye people! our God,
And resound the voice of his praise.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxxi-p14"></span>**9** Who hath brought our souls into
life, And hath not suffered our feet to fall.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxxi-p15"></span>**10** For thou hast proved us, O
God! Thou hast tried us as silver is tried:

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxxi-p16"></span>**11** Thou hast brought us into the
net Thou hast laid restraint upon our loins;

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxxi-p17"></span>**12** Thou hast made man to ride
over our heads; We have come into fire and water; And thou hast brought
us into a place of abundance.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxxi-p18"></span>**13** I will come into thy house
with burnt-offerings; I will pay thee my vows,

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxxi-p19"></span>**14** Which my lips have uttered,
And my mouth hath spoken in my affliction.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxxi-p20"></span>**15** Burnt-offerings of fat *lambs*
I will offer to thee with incense of rams; I will bring bullocks with
goats. Selah.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxxi-p21"></span>**16** Come, hear, and I will tell
all you who fear God, What he hath done for my soul.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxxi-p22"></span>**17** To him with my mouth I cried,
And I have exalted him with my tongue.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxxi-p23"></span>**18** If I have regarded iniquity in
my heart, The Lord will not hear me.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxxi-p24"></span>**19** But truly heard me hath God;
He hath attended to the voice of my prayer.

<span id="xxxv.ii.xxxi-p25"></span>**20** Blessed be God who hath not
turned away my prayer, Nor his mercy from me.

<span id="xxxv.iii"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iii-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iii-p2"></span>PSALMS 67—92

<span id="xxxv.iii.i"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iii.i-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iii.i-p2"></span>PSALM 67

<span id="xxxv.iii.i-p3"></span>*To the Chief Musician on Neginoth. A
Psalm \[*or*\] Song*

<span id="xxxv.iii.i-p4"></span>**1** May God have compassion upon us,
and bless us; May he cause his countenance to shine upon us. Selah.

<span id="xxxv.iii.i-p5"></span>**2** That thy way may be known upon the
earth, Among all nations thy salvation.

<span id="xxxv.iii.i-p6"></span>**3** Let the peoples praise thee, O
God! Let all the peoples celebrate thee.

<span id="xxxv.iii.i-p7"></span>**4** Let the peoples rejoice and exult,
For he shall judge the peoples with rectitude, And the nations upon
earth thou shalt guide. Selah.

<span id="xxxv.iii.i-p8"></span>**5** Let the peoples celebrate thee, O
God! Let all the peoples celebrate thee:

<span id="xxxv.iii.i-p9"></span>**6** The earth hath given *her*
increase; God \[*even*\] our own God will bless us.

<span id="xxxv.iii.i-p10"></span>**7** God will bless us; And fear him
shall all the ends of the earth.

<span id="xxxv.iii.ii"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iii.ii-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iii.ii-p2"></span>PSALM 68

<span id="xxxv.iii.ii-p3"></span>To the Chief Musician. A Psalm \[or\]
Song of David

<span id="xxxv.iii.ii-p4"></span>**1** Arise shall God: scattered shall
be his enemies; And flee from before his face shall those who hate him.

<span id="xxxv.iii.ii-p5"></span>**2** As smoke is driven away thou
shalt drive them away; As wax melteth before the fire, perish shall the
ungodly from before the face of God.

<span id="xxxv.iii.ii-p6"></span>**3** But the righteous shall rejoice,
They shell exult before God, And leap for joy.

<span id="xxxv.iii.ii-p7"></span>**4** Sing ye unto God, sing psalms to
his name; Exalt him who rideth upon the clouds whose name is Jah, And
exult before him.

<span id="xxxv.iii.ii-p8"></span>**5** The father of the orphans, and
the judge of the widows, *Is* God in the habitation of his holiness.

<span id="xxxv.iii.ii-p9"></span>**6** God who causeth the solitary to
dwell in a family, Who bringeth forth those who are bound with chains:
But rebels shall dwell in a dry land.

<span id="xxxv.iii.ii-p10"></span>**7** O God! when thou well test forth
before thy people, When thou marchedst through the wilderness; Selah:

<span id="xxxv.iii.ii-p11"></span>**8** The earth was moved, Also the
heavens dropped at the presence of this God: Sinai at the presence of
God, the God of Israel.

<span id="xxxv.iii.ii-p12"></span>**9** A liberal rain thou shalt make
to fall, O God! upon thy inheritance, And when it is weary thou
refreshest it.

<span id="xxxv.iii.ii-p13"></span>**10** Thy congregation shall dwell
therein: Thou wilt provide in thy goodness for the poor, O God!

<span id="xxxv.iii.ii-p14"></span>**11** The Lord shall give the word To
the women who announce the great army.

<span id="xxxv.iii.ii-p15"></span>**12** Kings of armies shall flee —
shall flee; And she who dwelleth within the house shall divide the
spoils.

<span id="xxxv.iii.ii-p16"></span>**13** Though ye should lie among the
pots, *in the ashes*, *Yet shall ye be as* the wings of the dove covered
with silver, And *which* behind is *as* fine yellow gold.

<span id="xxxv.iii.ii-p17"></span>**14** When the Almighty scattered
kings in it, It was white in Salmon.

<span id="xxxv.iii.ii-p18"></span>**15** The mountain of God, the
mountain of Bashan, The mountain of heights, the mountain of Bashan.

<span id="xxxv.iii.ii-p19"></span>**16** Why leap ye, ye mountains of
heights? The mountain in which it hath pleased God to dwell: Yea dwell
*in it* will Jehovah for ever.

<span id="xxxv.iii.ii-p20"></span>**17** The chariots of God \[*are*\]
twenty thousand thousands of angels: The Lord *is* among them, In the
sanctuary as in Sinai.

<span id="xxxv.iii.ii-p21"></span>**18** Thou hast ascended on high;
Thou hast led captive captivity; Thou hast received gifts among men; Yea
even \[*among*\] rebels, That Jehovah God might dwell *in the midst of
his people*

<span id="xxxv.iii.ii-p22"></span>**19** Blessed *be* God day by day:
*This* God will load us with deliverances. Selah.

<span id="xxxv.iii.ii-p23"></span>**20** Our God *is* the God of
salvations; And to Jehovah Lord *belong* the issues of death.

<span id="xxxv.iii.ii-p24"></span>**21** Surely God shall wound the head
of his enemies, The crown of the hair of him who walketh in his
wickedness.

<span id="xxxv.iii.ii-p25"></span>**22** The Lord hath said: “From
Bashan I will bring back; “I will bring back from the depths of the sea:

<span id="xxxv.iii.ii-p26"></span>**23** “That thy foot may be stained
with blood, “The tongue of thy dogs even in that of thy enemies.”

<span id="xxxv.iii.ii-p27"></span>**24** They have seen thy goings, O
God!— The goings of my God, my King, in the sanctuary.

<span id="xxxv.iii.ii-p28"></span>**25** Before went the singers;
\[*Then*\] followed the players on instruments; In the midst \[*were*\]
the damsels striking the timbrels.

<span id="xxxv.iii.ii-p29"></span>**26** In the congregations bless ye
God, \[*Even*\] the Lord, *ye who* are of the fountain of Israel!

<span id="xxxv.iii.ii-p30"></span>**27** There *was* little Benjamin
their ruler, The princes of Judah in their assembly, The princes of
Zebulun, the princes of Naphthali.

<span id="xxxv.iii.ii-p31"></span>**28** Commanded hath thy God thy
strength; Strengthen, O God! what thou hast wrought in us.

<span id="xxxv.iii.ii-p32"></span>**29** From thy temple upon Jerusalem
To thee shall kings bring presents.

<span id="xxxv.iii.ii-p33"></span>**30** Destroy the company of
spearmen, The assembly of bulls, with the calves of the peoples,
Treading with their feet upon pieces of silver: Scatter thou the peoples
that in wars delight.

<span id="xxxv.iii.ii-p34"></span>**31** Princes shall come out of
Egypt; Ethiopia shall speedily stretch forth her hands to God.

<span id="xxxv.iii.ii-p35"></span>**32** O ye kingdoms of the earth!
sing unto God: Sing psalms to the Lord. Selah.

<span id="xxxv.iii.ii-p36"></span>**33** To him who rideth upon the
heavens of heavens *which are* of old: Lo! he shall send forth in his
voice a voice of strength,

<span id="xxxv.iii.ii-p37"></span>**34** Ascribe ye strength to God over
Israel; His majesty and his strength \[*are*\] in the clouds.

<span id="xxxv.iii.ii-p38"></span>**35** Terrible art thou, O God! out
of thy holy places: The God of Israel himself shall give strength and
might to his people. Blessed *be* God!

<span id="xxxv.iii.iii"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iii.iii-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iii.iii-p2"></span>PSALM 69

<span id="xxxv.iii.iii-p3"></span>To the Chief Musician upon Shoshannim.
Of David

<span id="xxxv.iii.iii-p4"></span>**1** Save me, O God! For entered have
the waters even to my soul.

<span id="xxxv.iii.iii-p5"></span>**2** I am sunk into deep mire where
there is no standing place; I am come into the depths of waters, And the
floods of water have overflowed me.

<span id="xxxv.iii.iii-p6"></span>**3** I am weary with crying, Hoarse
is my throat become therewith; Failed have my eyes with waiting for my
God.

<span id="xxxv.iii.iii-p7"></span>**4** More in number than the hairs of
my head are those who hate me without cause: Increased are those who
desire to destroy me, \[*even*\] my lying adversaries: That which I took
not by violence, then I restored it.

<span id="xxxv.iii.iii-p8"></span>**5** O God! thou knowest my
foolishness, And my faults from thee are not hidden.

<span id="xxxv.iii.iii-p9"></span>**6** Let not those be ashamed in me
that wait for thee, O Lord, Jehovah of armies! Let not those be put to
shame in me who seek thee, O God of Israel!

<span id="xxxv.iii.iii-p10"></span>**7** For on thy account I have
suffered reproach; Shame hath covered my face.

<span id="xxxv.iii.iii-p11"></span>**8** A stranger I have been to my
brethren, And an alien I am become to the children of my mother.

<span id="xxxv.iii.iii-p12"></span>**9** For the zeal of thy house hath
eaten me up; And the reproaches of those who reproached thee have fallen
upon me.

<span id="xxxv.iii.iii-p13"></span>**10** And I wept, my soul fasted;
And that was for a reproach to me.

<span id="xxxv.iii.iii-p14"></span>**11** And I made my garment
sackcloth; And I was to them for a jest.

<span id="xxxv.iii.iii-p15"></span>**12** Defame me do those who sit in
the gate; And *I am* the songs of those who drink intoxicating liquor.

<span id="xxxv.iii.iii-p16"></span>**13** But as for me my prayer
\[*is*\] to thee, O Jehovah! *In the* time of *thy* favor, O God! In the
multitude of thy mercy answer me, In the truth of thy salvation.

<span id="xxxv.iii.iii-p17"></span>**14** Rescue me from the mire that I
may not sink; That I may be delivered from my adversaries, And from the
depths of waters.

<span id="xxxv.iii.iii-p18"></span>**15** Let not the flood of waters
overflow me; And let not the deep swallow me up; And let not the pit
dose its mouth upon me.

<span id="xxxv.iii.iii-p19"></span>**16** Answer me, O Jehovah! for good
*is* thy mercy: In the multitude of thy compassions look upon me.

<span id="xxxv.iii.iii-p20"></span>**17** And hide not thy face from thy
servant, for I am afflicted: Hasten! answer me!

<span id="xxxv.iii.iii-p21"></span>**18** Draw near to my soul, redeem
it: On account of my adversaries deliver me.

<span id="xxxv.iii.iii-p22"></span>**19** Thou knowest my reproach, and
my confusion, and my ignominy: Before thee *are* all my adversaries.

<span id="xxxv.iii.iii-p23"></span>**20** Reproach hath broken my heart,
and I am afflicted; And I looked for some one to show compassion, but
there was none; For comforters, but I found *them* not.

<span id="xxxv.iii.iii-p24"></span>**21** And they put into my meat
gall, And in my thirst they gave me vinegar to drink.

<span id="xxxv.iii.iii-p25"></span>**22** Let their table be before them
for a snare; And their prosperity for a net;

<span id="xxxv.iii.iii-p26"></span>**23** Darkened let be their eyes,
that they may not see; And cause their loins continually to tremble.

<span id="xxxv.iii.iii-p27"></span>**24** Pour out upon them thy wrath;
And let the fury of thy indignation take hold of them.

<span id="xxxv.iii.iii-p28"></span>**25** Let their palace be desolate;
In their tents let there not be a dweller.

<span id="xxxv.iii.iii-p29"></span>**26** For him whom thou hast smitten
they have persecuted; And to the grief of those whom thou hast wounded
they have added.

<span id="xxxv.iii.iii-p30"></span>**27** Add iniquity to their
iniquity; And let them not enter into thy righteousness.

<span id="xxxv.iii.iii-p31"></span>**28** Let them be blotted out of the
book of the living; And with the righteous let them not be written.

<span id="xxxv.iii.iii-p32"></span>**29** But as for me I am poor and
sorrowful: Thy salvation shall exalt me.

<span id="xxxv.iii.iii-p33"></span>**30** I will praise the name of God
in a song, And I will magnify him with thanksgiving.

<span id="xxxv.iii.iii-p34"></span>**31** And this will please Jehovah
More than a young bullock that hath horns and hoofs.

<span id="xxxv.iii.iii-p35"></span>**32** Seen it have the afflicted,
