And they shall rejoice at it who seek God; And live shall your heart.

<span id="xxxv.iii.iii-p36"></span>**33** For hearkened hath Jehovah to
the afflicted; And his prisoners he hath not despised.

<span id="xxxv.iii.iii-p37"></span>**34** Praise him let heaven and
earth; The seas and whatever creepeth in them.

<span id="xxxv.iii.iii-p38"></span>**35** For God will save Zion, And
will build the cities of Judah; And they shall dwell there, And possess
it by inheritance.

<span id="xxxv.iii.iii-p39"></span>**36** And the seed of his servants
shall inherit it; And they who love his name shall dwell in it.

<span id="xxxv.iii.iv"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iii.iv-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iii.iv-p2"></span>PSALM 70

<span id="xxxv.iii.iv-p3"></span>To the Chief Musician. Of David. To
call to remembrance

<span id="xxxv.iii.iv-p4"></span>**1** O God! to deliver me, O Jehovah!
to my aid, hasten.

<span id="xxxv.iii.iv-p5"></span>**2** Let those be ashamed and
confounded who seek after my soul; Let those be turned backward and put
to confusion who desire my hurt.

<span id="xxxv.iii.iv-p6"></span>**3** Let those be destroyed for a
reward of their shame, Who say to me, “Aha! Aha!”

<span id="xxxv.iii.iv-p7"></span>**4** Exult and rejoice in thee let all
who seek thee; And let those say, “For ever may God be magnified” —
Those who love thy salvation.

<span id="xxxv.iii.iv-p8"></span>**5** But as for me I am poor and
needy: O God! hasten to me: My help and my deliverer art thou: O
Jehovah! delay not.

<span id="xxxv.iii.v"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iii.v-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iii.v-p2"></span>PSALM 71

<span id="xxxv.iii.v-p3"></span>**1** In thee, O Jehovah! do I put my
trust, Let me not be put to shame for ever.

<span id="xxxv.iii.v-p4"></span>**2** In thy righteousness deliver me,
and rescue me; Incline to me thy ear, and save me.

<span id="xxxv.iii.v-p5"></span>**3** Be thou to me for a rock of
strength, Into which I may enter at all times: Thou hast given
commandment to save me; For my tower and my fortress art thou.

<span id="xxxv.iii.v-p6"></span>**4** O my God! deliver me from the hand
of the ungodly man, — From the hand of the wicked and violent men.

<span id="xxxv.iii.v-p7"></span>**5** For thou art my expectation, O
Lord Jehovah! My trust from my youth.

<span id="xxxv.iii.v-p8"></span>**6** Upon thee have I been sustained
from the womb; Out of my mother’s bowels thou art he who took me: Of
thee is my praise continually.

<span id="xxxv.iii.v-p9"></span>**7** As a prodigy I have been to the
great ones, And yet thou art my strong confidence.

<span id="xxxv.iii.v-p10"></span>**8** Filled shall be my mouth with thy
praise, Daily with thy glory.

<span id="xxxv.iii.v-p11"></span>**9** Cast me not off in the time of my
old age: In the declining of my strength forsake me not.

<span id="xxxv.iii.v-p12"></span>**10** For my enemies have spoken
concerning me, And those who watch for my soul have consulted together,

<span id="xxxv.iii.v-p13"></span>**11** Saying, “God hath forsaken him;
“Follow after him, and ye shall take him; “For there is none to deliver
*him*.”

<span id="xxxv.iii.v-p14"></span>**12** O God! be not far from me: O my
God! to my aid hasten.

<span id="xxxv.iii.v-p15"></span>**13** Let those be put to shame, let
those fail who are the adversaries of my soul: Let those be covered with
reproach mid shame who seek my hurt.

<span id="xxxv.iii.v-p16"></span>**14** But as for me continually will I
hope, And will add to all thy praise.

<span id="xxxv.iii.v-p17"></span>**15** My mouth shall tell of thy
righteousness, Daily of thy salvation; For I know not the number
*thereof*

<span id="xxxv.iii.v-p18"></span>**16** I will go in the strength of the
Lord Jehovah! I will remember thy righteousness alone.

<span id="xxxv.iii.v-p19"></span>**17** O God! thou hast taught me from
my youth; And unto this time will I announce thy wonders.

<span id="xxxv.iii.v-p20"></span>**18** And therefore  <span
id="fr_340"></span>[341](#fn_340) in old age and gray hairs, O God!
forsake me not, Until I have declared thy strength to the generation, To
all who are to come thy might.

<span id="xxxv.iii.v-p22"></span>**19** And thy righteousness, O God! is
very high: For thou hast done great things: O God! who is like to thee?

<span id="xxxv.iii.v-p23"></span>**20** Thou hast made me to see
troubles many and grievous, *But* being turned thou wilt quicken me, And
from the depths of the earth, being turned thou wilt raise me up.

<span id="xxxv.iii.v-p24"></span>**21** Thou wilt multiply my greatness;
And being turned thou wilt comfort me.

<span id="xxxv.iii.v-p25"></span>**22** Moreover, I, even I, will sing
to thee on instruments of music;  <span
id="fr_341"></span>[342](#fn_341) For thy truth, O my God! I will sing
psalms to thee upon the harp, O Holy One of Israel!

<span id="xxxv.iii.v-p27"></span>**23** Exult shall my lips, when I sing
psalms to thee; And my soul which thou hast redeemed.

<span id="xxxv.iii.v-p28"></span>**24** Also my tongue daily shall
declare thy righteousness; For they are put to shame, for they are
disgraced, who seek my hurt.

<span id="xxxv.iii.vi"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iii.vi-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iii.vi-p2"></span>PSALM 72

<span id="xxxv.iii.vi-p3"></span>Of Solomon

<span id="xxxv.iii.vi-p4"></span>**1** O God! thy judgments give to the
King, And thy righteousness to the son of the King

<span id="xxxv.iii.vi-p5"></span>**2** He shall judge thy people in
righteousness, And thy poor ones in judgment.

<span id="xxxv.iii.vi-p6"></span>**3** Bring forth shall the mountains
peace to the people, And the hills in righteousness.

<span id="xxxv.iii.vi-p7"></span>**4** He shall judge the poor ones of
the people; He shall save the children of the afflicted; And shall break
in pieces the calumniator.

<span id="xxxv.iii.vi-p8"></span>**5** They shall fear thee with the
sun; And before the moon the generation of generations shall fear thee.

<span id="xxxv.iii.vi-p9"></span>**6** He shall descend as rain upon the
mown grass; As the showers which water the earth.

<span id="xxxv.iii.vi-p10"></span>**7** Flourish in his days shall the
righteous; And abundance of peace until there be no more moon.

<span id="xxxv.iii.vi-p11"></span>**8** And he shall have dominion from
sea to sea, And from the river even to the ends of the earth.

<span id="xxxv.iii.vi-p12"></span>**9** Before him shall bow the
inhabitants of the desert, And his enemies shall lick the dust.

<span id="xxxv.iii.vi-p13"></span>**10** The kings of Tarshish and of
the isles a present shall bring: The kings of Sheba and Seba a gift
shall offer *to him*

<span id="xxxv.iii.vi-p14"></span>**11** And all kings shall prostrate
themselves before him; All nations shall serve him.

<span id="xxxv.iii.vi-p15"></span>**12** For he shall deliver the poor
who crieth *to him*, And the needy who hath no helper.

<span id="xxxv.iii.vi-p16"></span>**13** He will have compassion upon
the indigent and the poor one, And the souls of the poor ones he will
save.

<span id="xxxv.iii.vi-p17"></span>**14** From fraud and violence he will
redeem their souls, And precious shall be their blood in his eyes.

<span id="xxxv.iii.vi-p18"></span>**15** And he shall live, and there
shall be given to him of the gold of Sheba, And prayer shall be made for
him continually; Daily shall he be blessed.

<span id="xxxv.iii.vi-p19"></span>**16** There shall be *sown* an
handful of corn in the earth on the top of the mountains; The fruit
thereof shall be shaken like \[*that*\] of Lebanon. And they shall go
forth from the city as a plant of the earth.

<span id="xxxv.iii.vi-p20"></span>**17** His name shall be for ever; In
presence of the sun propagated shall be his name: And bless themselves
in him shall all nations, And blessed they shall call him.

<span id="xxxv.iii.vi-p21"></span>**18** Blessed be Jehovah God! the God
of Israel!  <span id="fr_342"></span>[343](#fn_342) Who doeth wonderful
things alone.

<span id="xxxv.iii.vi-p23"></span>**19** And blessed be his glorious
name for ever; And let all the earth be filled with his glory. Amen and
Amen.

<span id="xxxv.iii.vi-p24"></span>**20** Finished are the prayers of
David, the son of Jesse.

<span id="xxxv.iii.vii"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iii.vii-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iii.vii-p2"></span>PART THIRD  <span
id="fr_343"></span>[344](#fn_343)

<span id="xxxv.iii.vii-p4"></span>PSALM 73

<span id="xxxv.iii.vii-p5"></span>A Psalm of Asaph

<span id="xxxv.iii.vii-p6"></span>**1** Yet God is good to Israel, To
those who are right in heart.

<span id="xxxv.iii.vii-p7"></span>**2** As for me, wellnigh slipped had
my feet, My steps were almost gone:

<span id="xxxv.iii.vii-p8"></span>**3** For I was envious at the
foolish, On seeing the prosperity of the ungodly.

<span id="xxxv.iii.vii-p9"></span>**4** For there are no bands to their
death, And vigorous is their strength.

<span id="xxxv.iii.vii-p10"></span>**5** In the \[*common*\] trouble of
man they are not; And with other men they are not scourged.

<span id="xxxv.iii.vii-p11"></span>**6** Therefore encompass them as a
chain doth pride; Covered them hath the raiment of violence.

<span id="xxxv.iii.vii-p12"></span>**7** Their eye projecteth through
fatness; They have passed beyond the thoughts of their heart.

<span id="xxxv.iii.vii-p13"></span>**8** They break forth, and talk
wickedly of extortion: From on high do they speak.

<span id="xxxv.iii.vii-p14"></span>**9** They have set against the
heaven their mouth, And their tongue walketh through the earth.

<span id="xxxv.iii.vii-p15"></span>**10** On this account his people
will return hither, And waters of a full cup will be wrung out to them.

<span id="xxxv.iii.vii-p16"></span>**11** And they say, “How doth God
know? “ “And is there knowledge in the Most High?“

<span id="xxxv.iii.vii-p17"></span>**12** Behold these are the ungodly,
and \[*yet*\]. they are in quiet for ever: They heap up riches.

<span id="xxxv.iii.vii-p18"></span>**13** Surely in vain I have purified
my heart, And washed every day my hands:

<span id="xxxv.iii.vii-p19"></span>**14** And I have been scourged every
day, And my chastisement \[*has been*\] every morning.

<span id="xxxv.iii.vii-p20"></span>**15** If I have said, “I will speak
thus,” Behold! the generation of thy children: I have transgressed.

<span id="xxxv.iii.vii-p21"></span>**16** And although I applied my mind
to know this, A pain fill thing it was in mine eyes,

<span id="xxxv.iii.vii-p22"></span>**17** Until I entered into the
sanctuaries of God, *And* understood their end.

<span id="xxxv.iii.vii-p23"></span>**18** Surely in slippery places thou
hast set them; Thou shalt east them down into destructions.

<span id="xxxv.iii.vii-p24"></span>**19** How have they been destroyed
as in a moment! They have perished, they have been consumed with
terrors.

<span id="xxxv.iii.vii-p25"></span>**20** As it were a dream after a man
is awakened; O Lord! in awaking, their image thou wilt render
contemptible.

<span id="xxxv.iii.vii-p26"></span>**21** For in a ferment was my heart,
And in my reins I was pierced.

<span id="xxxv.iii.vii-p27"></span>**22** And I myself \[*was*\] foolish
and knew not *any thing*; As the beasts have I been before thee.

<span id="xxxv.iii.vii-p28"></span>**23** Nevertheless *I have been*
continually with thee; Thou hast held my right hand.

<span id="xxxv.iii.vii-p29"></span>**24** With thy counsel thou shalt
guide me; And at length to glory thou shalt take me.

<span id="xxxv.iii.vii-p30"></span>**25** Whom have I in heaven *but
thee*? And another with time I have not desired on the earth.

<span id="xxxv.iii.vii-p31"></span>**26** Failed have my flesh and my
heart; *But* the strength of my heart and my portion *is* God for ever.

<span id="xxxv.iii.vii-p32"></span>**27** For lo! those who depart from
thee shall perish: Thou hast destroyed every one who goeth a whoring
from thee.

<span id="xxxv.iii.vii-p33"></span>**28** As for me, to draw near to God
is good for me: I have put in the Lord Jehovah my trust, That I may tell
of all thy works.

<span id="xxxv.iii.viii"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iii.viii-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iii.viii-p2"></span>PSALM 74

<span id="xxxv.iii.viii-p3"></span>An Instruction of Asaph

<span id="xxxv.iii.viii-p4"></span>**1** Wherefore, O God! hast thou
cast us off for ever? \[*Why*\] smoketh thy wrath against the flock of
thy pastures?

<span id="xxxv.iii.viii-p5"></span>**2** Remember thy congregation which
thou hast possessed of old;  <span id="fr_344"></span>[345](#fn_344)
*Which* thou hast redeemed, the rod of thy inheritance, This Mount Zion
in which thou hast dwelt.

<span id="xxxv.iii.viii-p7"></span>**3** Lift up thy strokes to
desolations perpetual, Against every enemy who doeth mischief to the
sanctuary.

<span id="xxxv.iii.viii-p8"></span>**4** Roared *like lions* have thy
adversaries in the midst of thy sanctuaries; They have set up their
signs *for* signs.

<span id="xxxv.iii.viii-p9"></span>**5** He was renowned as doing an
excellent work Who lifted up the axes upon the thick trees.  <span
id="fr_345"></span>[346](#fn_345)

<span id="xxxv.iii.viii-p11"></span>**6** And now the carved works
thereof together, With the hatchet and with hammers they break in
pieces.

<span id="xxxv.iii.viii-p12"></span>**7** They have set on fire thy
sanctuaries; Leveling it with the ground, they have polluted the
dwelling-place of thy name.

<span id="xxxv.iii.viii-p13"></span>**8** They have said in their heart,
“Let us destroy them altogether.” They have burned all the tabernacles
of God in the land.

<span id="xxxv.iii.viii-p14"></span>**9** Our signs we see not; There is
no longer a prophet, Nor is there with us one who knoweth how long! —

<span id="xxxv.iii.viii-p15"></span>**10** How long, O God! shall the
adversary reproach? Shall the enemy blaspheme thy name for ever?

<span id="xxxv.iii.viii-p16"></span>**11** How long wilt thou withdraw
thy hand, and thy right hand? In the midst, of thy bosom consume them.

<span id="xxxv.iii.viii-p17"></span>**12** But God *is* my king from the
beginning, Working salvations in the midst of the earth.

<span id="xxxv.iii.viii-p18"></span>**13** Thou didst divide  <span
id="fr_346"></span>[347](#fn_346) by thy power the sea; Thou didst break
the heads of dragons in the waters.

<span id="xxxv.iii.viii-p20"></span>**14** Thou didst break the head of
the leviathan; Thou gavest him *for* food to *thy* people in the
wilderness.

<span id="xxxv.iii.viii-p21"></span>**15** Thou didst cleave the
fountain and the torrent: Thou didst dry up mighty rivers.

<span id="xxxv.iii.viii-p22"></span>**16** Thine is the day; thine also
is the night: Thou hast ordained the light and the sun.

<span id="xxxv.iii.viii-p23"></span>**17** Thou hast fixed all the
boundaries of the earth: The summer and the winter thou hast made.

<span id="xxxv.iii.viii-p24"></span>**18** Remember this: the enemy hath
reproached Jehovah; And a worthless people hath done despite to thy
name.

<span id="xxxv.iii.viii-p25"></span>**19** Give not to the beast the
soul of thy turtle dove: The congregation of thy poor ones forget not
for ever.

<span id="xxxv.iii.viii-p26"></span>**20** Have regard to *thy*
covenant; For filled are the dark places of the earth with the abodes of
violence.

<span id="xxxv.iii.viii-p27"></span>**21** Let not the afflicted one
return ashamed; Let the poor and needy one praise thy name.

<span id="xxxv.iii.viii-p28"></span>**22** Arise, O God! plead thy own
cause: Remember thy reproach, *which is done thee* by the foolish man
daily.

<span id="xxxv.iii.viii-p29"></span>**23** Forget not the voice of thy
adversaries: The tumult of those who rise up against thee ascendeth
continually.

<span id="xxxv.iii.ix"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iii.ix-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iii.ix-p2"></span>PSALM 75

<span id="xxxv.iii.ix-p3"></span>To the Chief Musician. Destroy not. A
Psalm of Asaph. A song

<span id="xxxv.iii.ix-p4"></span>**1** We will celebrate thee, O God! we
will celebrate *thee*; And near is thy name: they will declare thy
wonders.

<span id="xxxv.iii.ix-p5"></span>**2** When I shall have taken the
congregation, I in uprightness will judge.

<span id="xxxv.iii.ix-p6"></span>**3** Dissolved is the earth, and all
the inhabitants thereof: will establish the pillars of it. Selah.

<span id="xxxv.iii.ix-p7"></span>**4** I said to the fools, “Act not
foolishly;” And to the ungodly, “Raise not up the horn.”

<span id="xxxv.iii.ix-p8"></span>**5** Raise not up on high your horn;
And speak not with a stiff neck.

<span id="xxxv.iii.ix-p9"></span>**6** For neither from the east, nor
from the west, Nor from the wilderness are exaltations.

<span id="xxxv.iii.ix-p10"></span>**7** For God is judge: tie bringeth
low, and he setteth up.

<span id="xxxv.iii.ix-p11"></span>**8** For a cup *is* in the hand of
Jehovah, and the wine is turbid; It is full of mixture, and he shall
pour forth of it. Surely the dregs thereof they shall wring out;. And
drink *of it* shall all the wicked of the earth.

<span id="xxxv.iii.ix-p12"></span>**9** But as for me I will publish for
ever, I will sing psalms to the God of Jacob.

<span id="xxxv.iii.ix-p13"></span>**10** And all the horns of the
ungodly I will break; But exalted shall be the horns of the righteous.

<span id="xxxv.iii.x"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iii.x-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iii.x-p2"></span>PSALM 76

<span id="xxxv.iii.x-p3"></span>To the Chief Musician on Neginoth. A
Psalm of Asaph. A Song

<span id="xxxv.iii.x-p4"></span>**1** Known in Judah is God; In Israel
great is his name.

<span id="xxxv.iii.x-p5"></span>**2** And in Salem was his tabernacle,
And his dwelling-place in Zion.

<span id="xxxv.iii.x-p6"></span>**3** There he broke the arrows of the
bow, The shield, and the sword, and the battle. Selah.

<span id="xxxv.iii.x-p7"></span>**4** More glorious, more terrible *art*
thou Than the mountains of prey.

<span id="xxxv.iii.x-p8"></span>**5** Spoiled were the stout in heart,
They slept their sleep: And none of the men of might have found their
hands.

<span id="xxxv.iii.x-p9"></span>**6** At thy rebuke, O God of Jacob!
Cast into a deep sleep were the chariot and the horse.

<span id="xxxv.iii.x-p10"></span>**7** Thou *art* terrible \[*even*\]
thou; And who shall stand before thy face when thou art angry?

<span id="xxxv.iii.x-p11"></span>**8** From the heavens thou hast made
judgment to be heard: The earth was afraid and was still,

<span id="xxxv.iii.x-p12"></span>**9** When God arose to judgment, To
save all the meek of the earth. Selah.

<span id="xxxv.iii.x-p13"></span>**10** Surely the wrath of men shall
praise thee, The remainder of wrath thou wilt restrain.

<span id="xxxv.iii.x-p14"></span>**11** Vow and pay to Jehovah your God:
Let all who are round about him bring a present to the terrible one.

<span id="xxxv.iii.x-p15"></span>**12** He will cut off the spirit of
princes: *He* *is* terrible to the kings of the earth.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xi"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iii.xi-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iii.xi-p2"></span>PSALM 77

<span id="xxxv.iii.xi-p3"></span>To the Chief Musician upon Jeduthun. A
Psalm of Asaph

<span id="xxxv.iii.xi-p4"></span>**1** My voice \[*I lifted up*\] to
God, and I cried; My voice \[*I lifted up*\] to God, and he heard me.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xi-p5"></span>**2** In the day of my affliction the
Lord I sought: My hand in the night was stretched out and relaxed not;
Refuse consolation did my soul.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xi-p6"></span>**3** I will remember God, and will be
disquieted; I will meditate, and oppressed with sorrow shall be my
spirit. Selah.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xi-p7"></span>**4** Thou hast held the watches of my
eyes: I am troubled, and will not speak.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xi-p8"></span>**5** I have recounted the days of old,
The years of ages past.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xi-p9"></span>**6** I will call to remembrance my
song in the night: With my heart I will meditate, And search diligently
shall my spirit.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xi-p10"></span>**7** For ever will the Lord east off?
And will he be favorable no more?

<span id="xxxv.iii.xi-p11"></span>**8** Gone for ever is his mercy? Fail
doth his oracle from generation to generation?

<span id="xxxv.iii.xi-p12"></span>**9** Forgotten to be merciful hath
God? Hath he shut up in anger his compassions? Selah.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xi-p13"></span>**10** And I said my disease \[*is
only for a season*;\] The years of the right hand of the Most High \[*I
will wait for*.\]

<span id="xxxv.iii.xi-p14"></span>**11** I will remember the works of
God; Surely I will remember thy wonders from the beginning.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xi-p15"></span>**12** And I will meditate on all thy
works, And on thy doings I will muse.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xi-p16"></span>**13** O God! in the sanctuary *are*
thy ways: What god *is* so great as God?

<span id="xxxv.iii.xi-p17"></span>**14** Thou art the God who doest
wonders; Thou hast made known among the peoples thy strength.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xi-p18"></span>**15** Thou hast redeemed by \[*thy*\]
arm thy people, The sons of Jacob and Joseph. Selah.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xi-p19"></span>**16** See thee did the waters, O God!
see thee did the waters; They were afraid; also tremble did the deeps.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xi-p20"></span>**17** The clouds poured out waters;
The heavens gave forth a voice: Also thine arrows went abroad.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xi-p21"></span>**18** The voice of thy thunder was in
the circuit, The lightnings illumined the world; The earth trembled and
was shaken.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xi-p22"></span>**19** In the sea are thy ways, And
thy paths in the great waters; And thy footsteps are not known.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xi-p23"></span>**20** Thou leadest like sheep thy
people By the hand of Moses and Aaron.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p2"></span>PSALM 78

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p3"></span>A lesson of Instruction \[of\] Asaph

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p4"></span>**1** Give ear, O my people! to my
law: Incline your ears to the words of my month.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p5"></span>**2** I will open in a parable my
mouth; I will utter enigmas from ancient Sae.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p6"></span>**3** What we have heard and known,
And our’ fathers have related to us,

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p7"></span>**4** We will not conceal from their
children to the generation to come, Recounting the praises of Jehovah
and his might, And the wonders which he hath done.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p8"></span>**5** And he established a testimony
in, Jacob, And a law he appointed in Israel; For lie commanded our
fathers To make them known to their children;

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p9"></span>**6** That the generations to come
might know them, *That* the children to be born might arise, And declare
*them* to their children.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p10"></span>**7** That they might set in God
their hope, And not forget the works of God; But that his commandments
they might observe,

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p11"></span>**8** And not be as their fathers, A
generation rebellious and provoking; A generation which set not their
heart might, And whose spirit was not faithful towards God.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p12"></span>**9** The children of Ephraim, armed
\[*and*\] shooting with the bow, Were turned back in the day of battle.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p13"></span>**10** They kept not the covenant of
God, And in his law they refused to walk.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p14"></span>**11** And they forget his works, And
the wonders which he had shown them.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p15"></span>**12** In the sight of their fathers
he wrought marvelously; In the land of Egypt, in the field of Zoan.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p16"></span>**13** He divided the sea, and caused
them to pass through, And made the waters to stand as an heap.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p17"></span>**14** And he led them by a cloud in
the day; And all the night by the light of fire.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p18"></span>**15** He clave the rocks in the
wilderness, And made them to drink in great deeps.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p19"></span>**16** And he brought forth streams
from the rock, And made the waters to descend like rivers.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p20"></span>**17** Yet they continued still to
sin against him, To provoke the Most High in the wilderness.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p21"></span>**18** And they tempted God in their
heart, By asking food for their soul.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p22"></span>**19** And they spake against God:
They said, “Can God prepare a table in the wilderness?”

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p23"></span>**20** Behold! he smote the reek, and
gush out did the waters; And rivers overflowed. “Can he give bread also?
“Will he prepare flesh for his people?”

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p24"></span>**21** Therefore Jehovah heard and
was wroth: And a fire was kindled in Jacob: And wrath also ascended
against Israel;

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p25"></span>**22** Because they believed not in
God, And trusted not in his salvation.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p26"></span>**23** But he had commanded the
clouds from above, And the doors of heaven he had opened,

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p27"></span>**24** And had rained down upon them
manna for food, And the corn of heaven he had given them:

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p28"></span>**25** The bread of the mighty ones
man had eaten: Meat he had sent them to the full.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p29"></span>**26** He caused to blow an east wind
in the heavens; And he raised up by his power the south wind.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p30"></span>**27** And he rained upon them flesh
as dust, And as the sand of the sea leathered fowl;

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p31"></span>**28** And he caused *it* to fall in
the midst of his camp, Round about his tabernacles.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p32"></span>**29** And they did eat and were
filled exceedingly, And their desire he brought to them.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p33"></span>**30** They were not estranged from
their desire: The meat was still in their mouth,

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p34"></span>**31** When the wrath of God ascended
against them, And slew their fat ones, And brought low the chosen of
Israel.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p35"></span>**32** In all these *things* they
sinned still, And believed not his wonders.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p36"></span>**33** And he consumed in vanity
their days, And their years in haste.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p37"></span>**34** When he slew them, they sought
him; They returned, and hastened early to God.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p38"></span>**35** And they remembered that God
was their Rock, And *that* the Most High God was their Redeemer.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p39"></span>**36** And they flattered \[*him*\]
with their mouth, And with their tongue they lied to him:

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p40"></span>**37** But their heart was not right
before him, And they were not faithful in his covenant.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p41"></span>**38** Yet he *who* *is*
compassionate expiated their iniquity, And did not destroy them: And he
multiplied to turn away his anger, And did not stir up all his
indignation.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p42"></span>**39** And he remembered that they
were flesh; A breath that passeth, and returneth not.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p43"></span>**40** How often did they provoke him
in the desert, \[*And*\] grieve him in the wilderness!

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p44"></span>**41** And they returned and tempted
God, And the Holy One of Israel they limited.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p45"></span>**42** They remembered not his hand
In the day that he redeemed them from the oppressor,

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p46"></span>**43** When he set in Egypt his
signs, And his miracles in the field of Zoan.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p47"></span>**44** When he turned into blood
their rivers; And their streams, that they might not drink of them.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p48"></span>**45** He sent among them a mixture
which devoured them; And the frog which destroyed them.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p49"></span>**46** And he gave to the caterpillar
their fruit; And their labors to the locusts.  <span
id="fr_347"></span>[348](#fn_347)

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p51"></span>**47** And he destroyed with hail
their vine, And their wild fig-trees with hailstones.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p52"></span>**48** And he gave lip to the hail
their cattle, And their flocks to thunderbolts.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p53"></span>**49** He sent upon them the
fierceness of his wrath, Fury, anger, and affliction, A mission of evil
angels.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p54"></span>**50** He made a path for his anger:
He kept not from death their soul, And their cattle to the pestilence he
shut up.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p55"></span>**51** And he smote all the firstborn
in Egypt: The beginning of \[*their*\] strength in the tents of Ham.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p56"></span>**52** And he made to go forth like
sheep his people, And led them like a flock in the wilderness.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p57"></span>**53** And he conducted *them* in
safety, and they were not afraid: And their enemies cover did the sea.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p58"></span>**54** And he brought them to the
border of his holiness, This mountain, *which* his right hand acquired.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p59"></span>**55** And he expelled from before
their face the heathen; And made them to fall into the lot of all
inheritance; And caused to dwell in their tents the children of Israel.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p60"></span>**56** But they tempted and provoked
God Most High, And his testimonies they kept not.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p61"></span>**57** And they turned back and dealt
perfidiously like their fathers: They started aside like a bow that is
deceitful.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p62"></span>**58** And they provoked him to anger
with their high places; And with their graven images they moved him to
anger.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p63"></span>**59** Hear it did God, and was
wroth, And he abhorred exceedingly Israel.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p64"></span>**60** And he forsook the habitation
of Shiloh, The tabernacle where he dwelt among men.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p65"></span>**61** And he gave into captivity his
strength, And his beauty into the hand of the enemy.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p66"></span>**62** And he shut up to the sword
his people, And with his own inheritance was wroth.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p67"></span>**63** Their chosen devour did the
fire, And their virgins were not applauded.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p68"></span>**64** Their priests by the sword did
fall; And their widows made no lamentation.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p69"></span>**65** But the Lord awoke as one
asleep, As a mighty man who crieth out by reason of wine.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p70"></span>**66** And he smote his enemies
behind; Everlasting disgrace he put upon them.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p71"></span>**67** And he rejected the tabernacle
of Joseph, And the tribe of Ephraim he chose not:

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p72"></span>**68** But he chose the tribe of
Judah, The mountain of Zion, which lie loved:

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p73"></span>**69** And built like high places his
sanctuary, Like the earth which he hath founded for ever.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p74"></span>**70** And he chose David his
servant, And took him from the folds of sheep:

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p75"></span>**71** From following the suckling
ewes he took him, To feed Jacob his people, And Israel his inheritance:

<span id="xxxv.iii.xii-p76"></span>**72** And he fed them in the
integrity of his heart, And by the prudence of his hands he guided
there.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xiii"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iii.xiii-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iii.xiii-p2"></span>PSALM 79

<span id="xxxv.iii.xiii-p3"></span>A Psalm of Asaph

<span id="xxxv.iii.xiii-p4"></span>**1** O God! come have the heathen
into thy inheritance; They have polluted the temple of thy holiness;
They have laid Jerusalem in heaps. \[fowls of the heavens;

<span id="xxxv.iii.xiii-p5"></span>**2** They have given the dead bodies
of thy servants for food to the fowls of the heavens; The flesh of thy
meek ones to the beasts of the earth.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xiii-p6"></span>**3** They have shed their blood like
water around Jerusalem: And there was not *one* to bury *them*

<span id="xxxv.iii.xiii-p7"></span>**4** We have been a reproach to our
neighbors; A scorn and a derision to those who are around us.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xiii-p8"></span>**5** How long, O Jehovah! wilt thou
be wroth for ever? Burn like fire shall thy jealousy?

<span id="xxxv.iii.xiii-p9"></span>**6** Pour out thy wrath upon the
heathen who have not known thee, And upon the kingdoms which upon thy
name do not call:

<span id="xxxv.iii.xiii-p10"></span>**7** For they have devoured Jacob,
And his dwelling they have laid waste.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xiii-p11"></span>**8** Remember not against us former
iniquities: Make haste, let thy compassions prevent us; For we are
afflicted exceedingly.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xiii-p12"></span>**9** Help us, O God of our
salvation! for the glory of thy name; And deliver us, and be merciful to
our sins, for the sake of thy name.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xiii-p13"></span>**10** Wherefore should the heathen
say, “Where is their God?” Let be made known among the heathen in our
sight The vengeance of the blood of thy servants which is shed.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xiii-p14"></span>**11** Let the sighing of the
prisoner come before thy face: According to the greatness of thy arm,
Reserve the children of death:  <span id="fr_348"></span>[349](#fn_348)

<span id="xxxv.iii.xiii-p16"></span>**12** And recompense our neighbors
sevenfold into their bosom, Their reproach with which they have
reproached thee, O Jehovah!

<span id="xxxv.iii.xiii-p17"></span>**13** And we thy people, and the
sheep of thy pastures, Will confess to thee for ever; From generation to
generation declaring thy praise.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xiv"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iii.xiv-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iii.xiv-p2"></span>PSALM 80

<span id="xxxv.iii.xiv-p3"></span>To the Chief Musician upon Shoshannim
Eduth. A Psalm of Asaph

<span id="xxxv.iii.xiv-p4"></span>**1** O Shepherd of Israel, give ear!
Who leadest Joseph like a flock; Thou who sittest between the cherubim,
shine forth.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xiv-p5"></span>**2** Before Ephraim, and Benjamin,
and Manasseh, Stir up thy strength, and come for our salvation.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xiv-p6"></span>**3** Turn us again, O God! and cause
to shine thy face, And we shall be safe.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xiv-p7"></span>**4** O Jehovah God of armies! How
long wilt thou be incensed against the prayer of thy people?

<span id="xxxv.iii.xiv-p8"></span>**5** Thou hast fed us with bread of
tears; And hast given us tears to drink in great measure.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xiv-p9"></span>**6** Thou hast made us a strife to
our neighbors: And our enemies laugh *at us* among themselves.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xiv-p10"></span>**7** O God of armies! turn us again,
And cause to shine thy face upon us, And we shall be safe.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xiv-p11"></span>**8** A vine out of Egypt thou hast
brought: Thou hast expelled the heathen, and planted it,.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xiv-p12"></span>**9** Thou hast cleansed *the ground*
before it: Thou hast rooted its roots, And it hath filled the land.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xiv-p13"></span>**10** Covered were the mountains
with its shadow, And its branches *were like* the cedars of God.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xiv-p14"></span>**11** It sent forth its branches to
the sea, And to the river its shoots.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xiv-p15"></span>**12** Why then hast thou broken down
its hedges, So that tear it in pieces do all who pass by the way?

<span id="xxxv.iii.xiv-p16"></span>**13** Wasted it hath the boar out of
the forest; And the wild beast of the field hath eaten it up.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xiv-p17"></span>**14** O God of armies! return, I
beseech *thee*, Look down from heaven, and behold, And visit this vine,

<span id="xxxv.iii.xiv-p18"></span>**15** And the vineyard which planted
hath thy right hand, And \[*look*\] upon the shoot  <span
id="fr_349"></span>[350](#fn_349) *which* thou hast strengthened for
thyself.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xiv-p20"></span>**16** It is burnt with fire; it is
cut down; At the rebuke of thy countenance they perish.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xiv-p21"></span>**17** Let thy hand be upon the Man
of thy right hand, Upon the son of man whom thou hast strengthened for
thyself,

<span id="xxxv.iii.xiv-p22"></span>**18** And we will not go back from
thee: Thou shalt quicken us, and upon thy name we will call.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xiv-p23"></span>**19** O Jehovah, God of armies! turn
us again; Cause to shine thy face, And we shall be safe.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xv"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iii.xv-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iii.xv-p2"></span>PSALM 81

<span id="xxxv.iii.xv-p3"></span>To the Chief Musician upon Gittith. Of
Asaph

<span id="xxxv.iii.xv-p4"></span>**1** Exult to God our strength: Shout
for joy to the God of Jacob.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xv-p5"></span>**2** Take a song, and bring forth the
timbrel, The harp of pleasantness with the nablum.  <span
id="fr_350"></span>[351](#fn_350)

<span id="xxxv.iii.xv-p7"></span>**3** Sound the trumpet  <span
id="fr_351"></span>[352](#fn_351) at the new moon; At the time appointed
on the day of our sacrifice.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xv-p9"></span>**4** For a statute to Israel *is*
this, A judgment to the God of Jacob.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xv-p10"></span>**5** For a testimony in Joseph he set
it, When he went forth over the land of Egypt! A language which I
understood not I heard.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xv-p11"></span>**6** “I removed from the burden his
shoulder: “His hands from the pots were removed.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xv-p12"></span>**7** “In trouble thou didst cry, and
I rescued thee: “I answered thee in the secret place of thunder: “I
proved thee at the waters of Meribah. Selah.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xv-p13"></span>**8** “Hear, O my people! and I will
protest to thee: “O Israel! if thou wilt hearken to me.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xv-p14"></span>**9** “Let there not be in thee a
strange god: “Neither worship thou a foreign god.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xv-p15"></span>**10** “I *am* Jehovah thy God, “Who
brought thee out of the land of Egypt: “Open wide thy mouth, and I will
fill it.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xv-p16"></span>**11** “But my people hearkened not to
my voice, “And Israel would have none of me.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xv-p17"></span>**12** “And I gave them up to the
hardness of their heart: “They shall walk in their own counsels.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xv-p18"></span>**13** “O if my people had hearkened
to me! “*If* Israel in my ways had walked!

<span id="xxxv.iii.xv-p19"></span>**14** “Soon their enemies I would
have brought low, “And against their adversaries I would have turned my
hand:

<span id="xxxv.iii.xv-p20"></span>**15** “The haters of Jehovah would
have lied to him, “And their time should have been for ever:

<span id="xxxv.iii.xv-p21"></span>**16** “And I would have fed them with
the fat of corn: “And from the rock with honey I would have satisfied
thee.”

<span id="xxxv.iii.xvi"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iii.xvi-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iii.xvi-p2"></span>PSALM 82

<span id="xxxv.iii.xvi-p3"></span>A Psalm of Asaph

<span id="xxxv.iii.xvi-p4"></span>**1** God sitteth in the assembly of
God: In the midst of the gods he will judge.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xvi-p5"></span>**2** How long will ye judge unjustly?
And the faces of the ungodly will ye lift up? Selah.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xvi-p6"></span>**3** Judge the poor and the orphan;
The helpless and the destitute justify ye.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xvi-p7"></span>**4** Rescue the poor one and the
afflicted one: From the hand of the ungodly ones deliver *them*

<span id="xxxv.iii.xvi-p8"></span>**5** *But* they know not, neither do
they understand *any thing*: In darkness they walk, *Although* moved are
all the foundations of the earth.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xvi-p9"></span>**6** As for me, I have said, “Ye are
gods, “And children of the Most High all of you:

<span id="xxxv.iii.xvi-p10"></span>**7** “Surely as a man ye shall die;
“And as one \[*of the people*,\] O princes! ye shall fall.”

<span id="xxxv.iii.xvi-p11"></span>**8** Arise, O God! judge the earth:
For thou shalt inherit all nations.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xvii"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iii.xvii-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iii.xvii-p2"></span>PSALM 83

<span id="xxxv.iii.xvii-p3"></span>A Song \[or\] Psalm, of Asaph

<span id="xxxv.iii.xvii-p4"></span>**1** O God! keep not silence with
thyself; Hold not thy peace, and be not still, O God!

<span id="xxxv.iii.xvii-p5"></span>**2** For behold! thy enemies make a
tumult: And those who hate thee have lifted up the head.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xvii-p6"></span>**3** Against thy people they have
craftily formed a design, And have consulted against thy hidden ones.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xvii-p7"></span>**4** They have said, “Come and let
us cut them off from being a nation; “And let there be no remembrance of
the name of Israel any more.”

<span id="xxxv.iii.xvii-p8"></span>**5** For they have consulted with
the heart together; Against thee a covenant they have made.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xvii-p9"></span>**6** The tents of Edom, and of the
Ishmaelites; Of Moab and of the Hagarenes.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xvii-p10"></span>**7** Gebal, and Ammon, and Amalek;
The Philistines with the inhabitants of Tyre.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xvii-p11"></span>**8** Also Assur is associated with
them: They have been an arm to the sons of Lot. Selah.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xvii-p12"></span>**9** Do to them as to the
Midianites, As to Sisera, as to Jabin, at the brook Kishon.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xvii-p13"></span>**10** They perished at Endor; They
became manure for the earth.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xvii-p14"></span>**11** Make them, \[*even*\] their
princes, like Oreb, and like Zeeb; And like Zebah, and like Zalmunna,
all their princes.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xvii-p15"></span>**12** Who have said, “Let us take
in possession for ourselves “The habitations of God.”

<span id="xxxv.iii.xvii-p16"></span>**13** O my God! make them like a
whirling ball; Like stubble before the wind.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xvii-p17"></span>**14** As fire burneth a forest, And
as the flame kindleth the mountains,

<span id="xxxv.iii.xvii-p18"></span>**15** So pursue them with thy
tempest, And with thy whirlwind terrify them.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xvii-p19"></span>**16** Fill their faces with shame;
That they may seek thy name, O Jehovah!

<span id="xxxv.iii.xvii-p20"></span>**17** Let them be ashamed, and
terrified for ever;  <span id="fr_352"></span>[353](#fn_352) And let
them be confounded, and perish.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xvii-p22"></span>**18** And let them know that thou,
even thou, art, thy name Jehovah, Thou alone the Most High over all the
earth.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xviii"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iii.xviii-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iii.xviii-p2"></span>PSALM 84

<span id="xxxv.iii.xviii-p3"></span>To The Chief Musician Upon Gittith.
A Psalm of the sons of Korah

<span id="xxxv.iii.xviii-p4"></span>**1** How amiable are thy
tabernacles, O Jehovah of armies!

<span id="xxxv.iii.xviii-p5"></span>**2** Long, yea, even faint doth my
soul after the courts of Jehovah: My heart and my flesh leap for joy
towards the living God.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xviii-p6"></span>**3** Also the sparrow hath found a
house for herself, And the swallow a nest for herself, Where she may
place her young ones: O thine altars! thou Jehovah of armies! my King
and my God!

<span id="xxxv.iii.xviii-p7"></span>**4** Blessed *are* those who dwell
in thy house: Continually they will be praising thee. Selah.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xviii-p8"></span>**5** Blessed *is* the man whose
strength is in thee; The ways \[*are*\] in their heart.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xviii-p9"></span>**6** They passing through the
valley of weeping, will together make it a fountain; Also the cisterns
the rain will cover.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xviii-p10"></span>**7** They will journey from
strength to strength; Seen will be the God of gods in Zion.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xviii-p11"></span>**8** O Jehovah, God of armies!
hear my prayer: Hearken, O God of Jacob! Selah.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xviii-p12"></span>**9** Our shield do thou behold, O
God! And look upon the face of thy Christ.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xviii-p13"></span>**10** For better is one day in thy
courts than a thousand elsewhere. I would rather be a doorkeeper in the
house of my God, Than dwell in the tents of ungodliness.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xviii-p14"></span>**11** For a sun and shield *is*
Jehovah God *to us*; Grace and glory give will Jehovah; He will not
withhold *any* good from those who walk uprightly.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xviii-p15"></span>**12** O Jehovah of armies! Blessed
*is* the man who confideth in thee.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xix"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iii.xix-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iii.xix-p2"></span>PSALM 85

<span id="xxxv.iii.xix-p3"></span>To the Chief Musician. A Psalm of the
sons of Korah

<span id="xxxv.iii.xix-p4"></span>**1** Thou hast been favorable, O
Jehovah! to thy land: Thou hast brought back the captivity of Jacob.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xix-p5"></span>**2** Thou hast taken away the
iniquity of thy people: Thou hast covered all their sins. Selah

<span id="xxxv.iii.xix-p6"></span>**3** Thou hast turned away all thy
anger: Thou hast drawn back the fury of thy indignation.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xix-p7"></span>**4** Turn us, O God of our salvation!
And relax thy anger against us.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xix-p8"></span>**5** Wilt thou for ever be angry with
us? Wilt thou prolong thy wrath from age to age?

<span id="xxxv.iii.xix-p9"></span>**6** Wilt not thou being turned *to
us* quicken us? And thy people will rejoice in thee.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xix-p10"></span>**7** Show us, O Jehovah! thy mercy;
and thy salvation grant unto us.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xix-p11"></span>**8** I will hear what God Jehovah
will speak: Surely he will speak peace to his people and to his meek
ones, And they will not return to folly.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xix-p12"></span>**9** Surely near to those who fear
him is his salvation, That dwell may glory in our land.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xix-p13"></span>**10** Mercy and truth shall meet
together; Righteousness and peace shall kiss \[*each other*.\]

<span id="xxxv.iii.xix-p14"></span>**11** Truth out of the earth shall
spring up; And righteousness from heaven shall look down.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xix-p15"></span>**12** Likewise Jehovah will give
that which is good: And our land shall yield her increase.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xix-p16"></span>**13** Righteousness before him shall
go; And shall set in the way her steps.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xx"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iii.xx-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iii.xx-p2"></span>PSALM 86

<span id="xxxv.iii.xx-p3"></span>A Prayer of David

<span id="xxxv.iii.xx-p4"></span>**1** Incline, O Jehovah, thy ear,
answer me; For poor and needy *am* I.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xx-p5"></span>**2** Keep my soul, for I am meek: O
thou, my God! save thy servant who trusteth in thee.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xx-p6"></span>**3** Have compassion upon me, O
Jehovah! For to thee do I cry daily.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xx-p7"></span>**4** Gladden the soul of thy servant;
For to thee, O Lord! my soul I lift up.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xx-p8"></span>**5** For thou, O Lord! *art* good, and
gracious, Plenteous in mercy to all who call upon thee.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xx-p9"></span>**6** Listen, O Jehovah! to my prayer,
Attend to the voice of my supplications.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xx-p10"></span>**7** In the day of my trouble I will
cry to thee: For thou wilt answer me.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xx-p11"></span>**8** There is none like unto thee, O
Lord! among the gods; And *there* is none \[*who can work*\] according
to thy works.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xx-p12"></span>**9** All the nations which thou hast
made shall come, And shall worship before thy face, O Lord! And glory
they shall give to thy name:

<span id="xxxv.iii.xx-p13"></span>**10** For great art thou, And doing
wonders, thou God alone.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xx-p14"></span>**11** Show me, O Jehovah! thy ways; I
will walk in thy truth: Unite my heart to fear thy name.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xx-p15"></span>**12** I will celebrate thee, O Lord
my God! with my whole heart; And I will glorify thy name for ever;

<span id="xxxv.iii.xx-p16"></span>**13** For thy mercy hath been great
towards me; And thou hast delivered my soul from the lower grave.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xx-p17"></span>**14** O God! the proud have risen up
against me, And a company of mighty men have sought after my soul; And
they have not set thee before them.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xx-p18"></span>**15** And thou, O Lord! \[*art*\] a
God compassionate and gracious; Slow to anger; and plenteous in mercy
and truth.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xx-p19"></span>**16** Look to me, and have pity upon
me: Give thy strength to thy servant, And save the son of thy handmaid.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xx-p20"></span>**17** Make with me a sign for good:
And see shall my adversaries and be ashamed; For thou, O Jehovah! hast
secured me and comforted me.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxi"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxi-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxi-p2"></span>PSALM 87

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxi-p3"></span>A Psalm \[or\] Song of the sons of
Korah

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxi-p4"></span>**1** His foundations \[*are*\] in the
holy mountains.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxi-p5"></span>**2** Love doth Jehovah the gates of
Zion More than all the tabernacles of Jacob.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxi-p6"></span>**3** Glorious things are spoken of
thee, O city of God! Selah.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxi-p7"></span>**4** I will make mention of Rahab,
and Babel among those who know me: Behold the Philistines, and Tyre,
with Ethiopia, He is born there! Selah.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxi-p8"></span>**5** And of Zion it shall be said,
“Man and man is born in her; “And the Most High himself will establish
her.”

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxi-p9"></span>**6** The Lord will recount when he
writeth the peoples, “He is born there.” Selah.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxi-p10"></span>**7** And the singers as the players
upon instruments: All my springs *are* in thee.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxii"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxii-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxii-p2"></span>PSALM 88

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxii-p3"></span>A Song of a Psalm of the sons of
Korah. To the Chief Musician, upon Machalath, to make humble. An
instruction of Heman the Ezrahite

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxii-p4"></span>**1** O Jehovah! God of my salvation!
By day I cry, by night before thee.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxii-p5"></span>**2** Come into thy presence let my
prayer; Incline thy ear to my cry;

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxii-p6"></span>**3** For filled with troubles is my
soul; And my life to hell  <span id="fr_353"></span>[354](#fn_353) hath
drawn near.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxii-p8"></span>**4** I am counted with those who go
down to the sepulcher,  <span id="fr_354"></span>[355](#fn_354) I have
been as a man who hath no strength:

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxii-p10"></span>**5** Free among the dead, As the
slain lying in the grave, Whom thou rememberest no more, And who from
thy hand are cut off.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxii-p11"></span>**6** Thou hast laid me in the
lowest pit, In thick darkness, in the deeps.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxii-p12"></span>**7** Upon me lieth heavy thy
indignation; And with all thy waves thou hast afflicted me. Selah.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxii-p13"></span>**8** Thou hast removed my
acquaintances from me: Thou hast made me abominations to them: I am shut
up that I cannot go forth.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxii-p14"></span>**9** My eye mourneth because of my
affliction; I invoke thee, O Jehovah! daily: I stretch out to thee my
hands.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxii-p15"></span>**10** Wilt thou for the dead do a
miracle? Shall the dead rising up praise thee? Selah.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxii-p16"></span>**11** Shall thy loving-kindness be
declared in the grave? Thy truth in destruction?

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxii-p17"></span>**12** Shall thy wonders be known in
darkness? And thy righteousness in the land of forgetfulness?

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxii-p18"></span>**13** But as for me to thee, O
Jehovah! have I cried, And in the morning my prayer shall prevent thee.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxii-p19"></span>**14** Wherefore, O Jehovah! wilt
thou reject my soul? \[*Wherefore*\] wilt thou hide thy face from me?

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxii-p20"></span>**15** Afflicted am I, and ready to
die from my youth; I have suffered thy terrors by doubting.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxii-p21"></span>**16** Passed over me hath thy
fierce wrath: Thy terrors have cut me off.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxii-p22"></span>**17** They have encompassed me as
waters daily; They have surrounded me together.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxii-p23"></span>**18** Thou hast removed from me
lover and companion; And my acquaintances are darkness.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiii"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p2"></span>PSALM 89

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p3"></span>An Instruction of Ethan, the
Ezrahite

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p4"></span>**1** The mercies of Jehovah for
ever will I sing: From generation to generation will I celebrate thy
truth with my mouth.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p5"></span>**2** For I have said, For ever
Mercy shall be built up: The heavens thou shalt establish; thy truth
\[*is*\] in them.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p6"></span>**3** “I have made a covenant with
my chosen: “I have sworn to David my servant:

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p7"></span>**4** “For ever will I establish thy
seed, “And I will build up from age to age thy throne.” Selah.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p8"></span>**5** And celebrate shall the
heavens thy wondrous work, O Jehovah! Also thy truth in the congregation
of the saints.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p9"></span>**6** For who in the clouds can be
compared to Jehovah? Who is like unto Jehovah among the sons of the
gods?

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p10"></span>**7** God is terrible exceedingly
in the assembly of the saints, And to be feared above all who are around
him.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p11"></span>**8** O Jehovah, God of armies! who
*is* a strong God like thee? And thy truth is round about thee.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p12"></span>**9** Thou governest the pride of
the sea: When rise up do the waves thereof, thou restrainest them.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p13"></span>**10** Thou hast overthrown Egypt
as a wounded mail; With the arm of thy strength thou hast scattered thy
enemies.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p14"></span>**11** Thine are the heavens, thine
also is the earth: The world, and the fullness thereof thou hast formed.
 <span id="fr_355"></span>[356](#fn_355)

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p16"></span>**12** The north and the south thou
hast created: Tabor and Hermon in thy name shall exult.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p17"></span>**13** Thou hast an arm of might:
Thou wilt strengthen thy hand, Thou wilt exalt thy right hand.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p18"></span>**14** Righteousness and judgment
*are* the seat of thy throne: Mercy and truth shall go before thy face.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p19"></span>**15** Blessed is the people that
know the joyful sound! O Jehovah! in the brightness of thy countenance
they shall walk.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p20"></span>**16** In thy name shall they exult
daily; And in thy righteousness shall they glory:

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p21"></span>**17** For the glory of their
strength art thou; And in thy favor exalted shall be our horn.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p22"></span>**18** For to Jehovah *is* our
buckler; And to. the Holy One of Israel *is* our King.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p23"></span>**19** Then thou spakest in vision
to thy meek ones, And saidst, “I have laid help upon a Mighty One; “I
have exalted one chosen from among the people.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p24"></span>**20** “I have found David my
servant; “With the oil of my holiness have I anointed him.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p25"></span>**21** “Therefore, my hand shall be
established with him: “Yea, my arm shall strengthen him.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p26"></span>**22** “The enemy shall not exact
upon him, “Nor shall the son of iniquity afflict him.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p27"></span>**23** “And I will break in pieces
before his face his oppressors; “And those who hate him I will smite.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p28"></span>**24** “And my truth and my mercy
*shall be* with him: “And in my name exalted shall be his horn.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p29"></span>**25** “And I will set in the sea
his hand, “And in the rivers his right hand.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p30"></span>**26** “He shall cry to me, ‘My
Father art thou, “‘My God, the Rock of my salvation.’

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p31"></span>**27** “Also I myself my firstborn
will make him, “Higher than the kings of the earth.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p32"></span>**28** “And for ever will I keep
for him my mercy, “And my covenant shall stand firm with him.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p33"></span>**29** “And I will establish for
ever his seed, “And his throne as the days of heaven.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p34"></span>**30** “If forsake shall his
children my law, “And in my judgments shall not walk;

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p35"></span>**31** “If my ordinances they shall
profane, “And my statutes they shall not keep;

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p36"></span>**32** “Then will I visit with my
rod their transgressions, “And with stripes their iniquity.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p37"></span>**33** “But my mercy will I not
withdraw from him; “Nor will I be false in my truth.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p38"></span>**34** “I will not profane my
covenant, “And that which is gone forth from my lips I will not alter.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p39"></span>**35** “Once have I sworn by my
holiness, “If to David I lie —

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p40"></span>**36** “His seed for ever shall
endure; “And his throne as the sun before me.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p41"></span>**37** “As the moon it shall be
established for ever, “And \[*as*\] a faithful witness in the heaven.”
Selah.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p42"></span>**38** But thou, even thou, hast
abhorred and rejected *him*; Thou hast been wroth with thy anointed.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p43"></span>**39** Thou hast made to cease the
covenant of thy servant; Thou hast profaned to the earth his crown.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p44"></span>**40** Thou hast broken down all
his walls; Thou hast made his fortresses a ruin.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p45"></span>**41** Plundered him have all who
pass by the way: He hath been a reproach to his neighbors.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p46"></span>**42** Thou hast exalted the right
hand of his oppressors; Thou hast made glad all his adversaries.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p47"></span>**43** Also thou hast blunted the
edge of his sword, And hast not made him to stand in battle.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p48"></span>**44** Thou hast effaced his
splendor, And his throne to the ground thou hast east down.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p49"></span>**45** Thou hast shortened the days
of his youth; Thou hast covered him with disgrace. Selah.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p50"></span>**46** How long, O Jehovah! wilt
thou hide thyself for ever? Burn like fire shall thy indignation?

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p51"></span>**47** Remember how short-lived I
am!  <span id="fr_356"></span>[357](#fn_356) Wherefore in vain shouldst
thou have created all the sons of men?

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p53"></span>**48** What man shall live, and
shall not see death? *And* shall deliver his soul from the hand of the
grave? Selah.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p54"></span>**49** Where *are* thy former
compassions, O Lord? Thou hast sworn to David in thy truth.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p55"></span>**50** Remember, O Lord! the
reproach of thy servants: I have sustained in my bosom all *those*
\[*reproaches*\] of the mighty peoples,

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p56"></span>**51** With which thy enemies have
reproached thee, O Jehovah! With which they have reproached the
footsteps of thy Messiah.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiii-p57"></span>**52** Blessed *be* Jehovah for
evermore. Amen and Amen!

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiv"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiv-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiv-p2"></span>PART FOURTH.  <span
id="fr_357"></span>[358](#fn_357)

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiv-p4"></span>PSALM 90

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiv-p5"></span>A Psalm of Moses, the man of God

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiv-p6"></span>**1** O Lord! a dwelling-place thou
hast been to us from generation to generation.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiv-p7"></span>**2** Before the mountains were
brought forth, And \[*before*\] thou hadst formed the earth and the
world, Even from everlasting to everlasting, thou art God.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiv-p8"></span>**3** Thou shalt turn man to
destruction, And shalt say, “Return ye sons of Adam.”

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiv-p9"></span>**4** For a thousand years in thy
sight *are* as yesterday when it is past, And *as* a watch in the night.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiv-p10"></span>**5** Thou overflowest them;  <span
id="fr_358"></span>[359](#fn_358) they will be a sleep: In the morning
as grass he shall grow.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiv-p12"></span>**6** In the morning he (*or* it)
shall flourish and grow: At the evening he (*or* it) shall be cut down,
and shall wither.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiv-p13"></span>**7** For we fail by thy anger, And
by thy indignation are we affrighted.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiv-p14"></span>**8** Thou hast set our iniquities
before thee, Our secret sins in the light of thy countenance.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiv-p15"></span>**9** For all our days are passed
away in thy indignation: We have spent our years as if a thought.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiv-p16"></span>**10** In the days of our years
*there are* seventy years; And if through strength, eighty years, Yet is
their pride \[*but*\] grief and labor; For it passeth by quickly, and we
fly away.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiv-p17"></span>**11** Who knoweth the power of thy
anger? And according to thy fear is thy wrath.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiv-p18"></span>**12** Teach us so to number our
days, And we shall apply our heart to wisdom.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiv-p19"></span>**13** Return, O Jehovah! how long?
Be pacified towards thy servants.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiv-p20"></span>**14** Satiate us early with thy
goodness, And we will exult and rejoice all our days.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiv-p21"></span>**15** Make us joyful according to
the days of our affliction; *According* to the years in which we have
seen evil.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiv-p22"></span>**16** Let thy work appear towards
thy servants, And thy glory upon their children.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxiv-p23"></span>**17** And let there be the beauty
of the Lord our God upon us; And the work of our hands direct thou upon
us; Yea, the work of our hands direct thou.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxv"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxv-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxv-p2"></span>PSALM 91

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxv-p3"></span>**1** He who dwelleth in the secret
place of the Most High, Under the shadow of the Almighty shall abide.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxv-p4"></span>**2** I will say to Jehovah, “*Thou
art* my hope and my fortress:” *He is* my God; I will hope in him.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxv-p5"></span>**3** Surely he shall deliver thee
from the snare of the fowler, From the noxious pestilence:

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxv-p6"></span>**4** With his wings he shall protect
thee; And under his feathers thou shalt be safe; *Thy* shield and *thy*
buckler *shall be* his truth.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxv-p7"></span>**5** Thou shalt not be afraid at the
terror of the night; At the arrow which flieth by day;

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxv-p8"></span>**6** At the destruction which in
darkness walketh: At the pestilence which wasteth at noon-day.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxv-p9"></span>**7** There shall fall at thy side a
thousand, And ten thousand at thy right hand: To thee it shall not come
nigh.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxv-p10"></span>**8** Only with thine eyes shalt thou
behold, And the reward of the ungodly thou shalt see.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxv-p11"></span>**9** Because thou, O Jehovah! *art*
my protection; The Most High thou hast made thy refuge.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxv-p12"></span>**10** There shall not befall thee
\[*any*\] evil, And the plague shall not come nigh thy tabernacle:

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxv-p13"></span>**11** For to his angels he hath
given charge concerning thee, To keep thee in all thy ways.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxv-p14"></span>**12** Upon their hands they shall
bear thee, Lest thou dash against a stone thy foot.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxv-p15"></span>**13** Over the lion and asp thou
shalt walk; Thou shalt tread upon the young lion and dragon.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxv-p16"></span>**14** Because on me he hath reposed,
I will deliver him; I will exalt him because he hath known my name.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxv-p17"></span>**15** He will call upon me, and I
will answer him: With him will I be in trouble; I will deliver him, and
will glorify him.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxv-p18"></span>**16** With length of days will I
satisfy him, And will show him my salvation.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxvi"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxvi-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxvi-p2"></span>PSALM 92

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxvi-p3"></span>**1** It is good to give thanks to
Jehovah, To sing psalms to thy name, O Most High!

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxvi-p4"></span>**2** To proclaim in the morning thy
goodness, And thy truth in the night.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxvi-p5"></span>**3** Upon the psaltery, and upon the
nablum,  <span id="fr_359"></span>[360](#fn_359) Upon higgaion with the
harp.  <span id="fr_360"></span>[361](#fn_360)

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxvi-p8"></span>**4** For thou hast made me glad, O
Jehovah! in thy works; In the works of thy hands I will exult.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxvi-p9"></span>**5** How magnificent are thy works,
O Jehovah! Exceeding deep are thy thoughts.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxvi-p10"></span>**6** The man that is foolish shall
not know them, Neither shall he who is void of wisdom understand them.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxvi-p11"></span>**7** When the wicked flourish as
the grass, And all the workers of iniquity spring up, \[*It is*\] that
they may perish for ever.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxvi-p12"></span>**8** But thou *art* exalted for
evermore, O Jehovah!

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxvi-p13"></span>**9** For lo! thine enemies, O
Jehovah! For lo! thine enemies shall perish; Scattered shall be all the
workers of iniquity:

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxvi-p14"></span>**10** But thou shalt exalt my horn
like *that* of the unicorn. I am anointed with fresh oil.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxvi-p15"></span>**11** And mine eye shall see
\[*ruin*\] on my oppressors: \[*Of destruction*,\] on those who rise up
against me — On those who trouble me hear shall my ears.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxvi-p16"></span>**12** The righteous as the palm
tree shall flourish, As the cedar in Lebanon he shall be multiplied.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxvi-p17"></span>**13** Planted in the house of
Jehovah, In the courts of our God, they shall flourish.

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxvi-p18"></span>**14** Still shall they bud forth in
old age; Fat and green shall they be;

<span id="xxxv.iii.xxvi-p19"></span>**15** That they may proclaim that
upright is Jehovah, my Rock, And *that* there is no iniquity in him.

<span id="xxxv.iv"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iv-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iv-p2"></span>PSALMS 93—118

<span id="xxxv.iv.i"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iv.i-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iv.i-p2"></span>PSALM 93

<span id="xxxv.iv.i-p3"></span>**1** Jehovah hath reigned, He hath put
on glory, Put on hath Jehovah strength; He hath girded himself: Also he
hath established the world, It shall not be moved.

<span id="xxxv.iv.i-p4"></span>**2** Fixed is thy throne; \[*Even as*\]
from that time  <span id="fr_361"></span>[362](#fn_361) thou art, and
from eternity.  <span id="fr_362"></span>[363](#fn_362)

<span id="xxxv.iv.i-p8"></span>**3** Raised have the floods, O Jehovah!
Raised have the floods their voice; Raise shall the floods their waves.

<span id="xxxv.iv.i-p9"></span>**4** By reason of the voices  <span
id="fr_363"></span>[364](#fn_363) of the great waters Terrible are the
waves of the sea: Terrible on high is Jehovah.

<span id="xxxv.iv.i-p11"></span>**5** Thy testimonies are verified
exceedingly; To thy house *is* glory; The holiness of Jehovah *is* for
length of days.

<span id="xxxv.iv.ii"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iv.ii-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iv.ii-p2"></span>PSALM 94

<span id="xxxv.iv.ii-p3"></span>**1** O Jehovah! God of vengeances! O
God of vengeances! shine forth.

<span id="xxxv.iv.ii-p4"></span>**2** Lift up thyself; O judge of the
earth! Render a reward to the proud.

<span id="xxxv.iv.ii-p5"></span>**3** How long shall the ungodly, O
Jehovah! How long shall the ungodly triumph?

<span id="xxxv.iv.ii-p6"></span>**4** They pour forth, they speak hard
things, Extol themselves do all the workers of iniquity.

<span id="xxxv.iv.ii-p7"></span>**5** Thy people, O Jehovah! they break
in pieces; And thy inheritance they afflict:

<span id="xxxv.iv.ii-p8"></span>**6** The widow, and the stranger they
slay, And the orphans they put to death.

<span id="xxxv.iv.ii-p9"></span>**7** And they have said, “God shall not
see, “The God of Jacob shall not know..”

<span id="xxxv.iv.ii-p10"></span>**8** Understand, ye stupid among the
people! And ye fools! when will ye be wise?

<span id="xxxv.iv.ii-p11"></span>**9** He who planted the ear shall not
He hear? He who formed the eye, shall not He see?

<span id="xxxv.iv.ii-p12"></span>**10** He who chastiseth the nations,
shall not He correct? He who teacheth man knowledge?

<span id="xxxv.iv.ii-p13"></span>**11** Jehovah knoweth the thoughts of
men that they are vain.

<span id="xxxv.iv.ii-p14"></span>**12** Blessed *is* the man whom thou
hast instructed, O God! And out of thy law hast taught;

<span id="xxxv.iv.ii-p15"></span>**13** To give him rest from days of
evil, Whilst there is digged for the ungodly \[*man*\] a pit.

<span id="xxxv.iv.ii-p16"></span>**14** Surely Jehovah will not cast off
his people, And his inheritance he will not forsake.

<span id="xxxv.iv.ii-p17"></span>**15** For return shall judgment unto
righteousness, And \[*follow*\] after him shall all the upright in
heart.

<span id="xxxv.iv.ii-p18"></span>**16** Who will rise up for me against
my adversaries? Who will stand up for me against the workers of
iniquity?

<span id="xxxv.iv.ii-p19"></span>**17** Unless Jehovah had been a help
to me, My soul had well-nigh dwelt in silence.

<span id="xxxv.iv.ii-p20"></span>**18** If I said, “Slidden hath my
foot,” Thy goodness, O Jehovah! hath sustained me.

<span id="xxxv.iv.ii-p21"></span>**19** In the multitude of my thoughts,
Within me thy comforts cheer my soul.

<span id="xxxv.iv.ii-p22"></span>**20** Shall the throne of iniquities
have fellowship with thee, Framing molestation for law?

<span id="xxxv.iv.ii-p23"></span>**21** They will gather together
against the soul of the righteous, And the blood of the innocent they
will condemn.

<span id="xxxv.iv.ii-p24"></span>**22** But Jehovah hath been to me for
a fortress; And my God for the rock of my confidence:

<span id="xxxv.iv.ii-p25"></span>**23** And he shall retribute upon them
their own iniquity, And in their wickedness he shall destroy them;
Destroy them shall Jehovah our God.

<span id="xxxv.iv.iii"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iv.iii-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iv.iii-p2"></span>PSALM 95

<span id="xxxv.iv.iii-p3"></span>**1** Come let us exult to Jehovah; Let
us shout for joy to the Rock of our salvation.

<span id="xxxv.iv.iii-p4"></span>**2** Let us come before his face with
praise, In psalms let us shout for joy unto him.

<span id="xxxv.iv.iii-p5"></span>**3** For a great God *is* Jehovah, And
a great King, above all gods.

<span id="xxxv.iv.iii-p6"></span>**4** For in his hand *are* the deep
places of the earth; And the heights of the mountains are his.

<span id="xxxv.iv.iii-p7"></span>**5** For his is the sea, and he made
it; And the dry land his hands formed.

<span id="xxxv.iv.iii-p8"></span>**6** Come ye, let us worship, and fall
down; Let us kneel before the face of Jehovah, our Maker.

<span id="xxxv.iv.iii-p9"></span>**7** For he *is* our God, And we
\[*are*\] the people of his pastures, And the flock of his hand; To-day,
if his voice ye will hear,

<span id="xxxv.iv.iii-p10"></span>**8** Harden not your heart, as in
Meribah; As in the day of Massah in the desert,

<span id="xxxv.iv.iii-p11"></span>**9** When tempt me did your fathers;
They proved me, though they had seen my work.

<span id="xxxv.iv.iii-p12"></span>**10** Forty years I strove with this
generation, And said, “They are a people erring in heart, “And they have
not known my ways.”

<span id="xxxv.iv.iii-p13"></span>**11** Wherefore I swear in my wrath,
“If they shall enter into my rest —”

<span id="xxxv.iv.iv"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iv.iv-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iv.iv-p2"></span>PSALM 96

<span id="xxxv.iv.iv-p3"></span>**1** Sing ye to Jehovah a song that is
new, Sing to Jehovah all the earth.

<span id="xxxv.iv.iv-p4"></span>**2** Sing to Jehovah, bless his name;
Publish from day to day his salvation.

<span id="xxxv.iv.iv-p5"></span>**3** Tell among the heathen his glory;
Among all the peoples his wonders.

<span id="xxxv.iv.iv-p6"></span>**4** For great *is* Jehovah, and to be
praised highly; Terrible \[*is*\] he above all gods.

<span id="xxxv.iv.iv-p7"></span>**5** For all the gods of the nations
are vanities; But Jehovah made the heavens.

<span id="xxxv.iv.iv-p8"></span>**6** Strength and majesty *go* before
him; Power and glory *are* in his sanctuary.

<span id="xxxv.iv.iv-p9"></span>**7** Ascribe to Jehovah, O ye
congregations of peoples! Ascribe to Jehovah glory and strength.

<span id="xxxv.iv.iv-p10"></span>**8** Ascribe to Jehovah the glory of
his name; Bring an offering, and enter into his courts.

<span id="xxxv.iv.iv-p11"></span>**9** Worship before Jehovah in the
beauty of the sanctuary; Tremble before his face let the whole earth.

<span id="xxxv.iv.iv-p12"></span>**10** Say ye among the heathen,
“Jehovah reigneth; “Truly established shall be the world, it shall not
be moved: “He shall judge the peoples in righteousness.”

<span id="xxxv.iv.iv-p13"></span>**11** Rejoice let the heavens, and
exult let the earth; Thunder let the sea, and the fullness thereof.

<span id="xxxv.iv.iv-p14"></span>**12** Exult let the field, and all
that is in it; Shout for joy together let all the trees of the wood

<span id="xxxv.iv.iv-p15"></span>**13** Before Jehovah; for he cometh,
For he cometh to judge the earth: He shall judge the world in
righteousness, And the peoples in his truth.

<span id="xxxv.iv.v"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iv.v-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iv.v-p2"></span>PSALM 97

<span id="xxxv.iv.v-p3"></span>**1** Jehovah reigneth: Exult let the
earth, Rejoice let the great islands.

<span id="xxxv.iv.v-p4"></span>**2** Clouds and darkness *are* round
about him; Righteousness and judgment *are* the seat of his throne.

<span id="xxxv.iv.v-p5"></span>**3** A fire before his face shall go,
And shall burn up round about his enemies.

<span id="xxxv.iv.v-p6"></span>**4** Enlighten did his lightnings the
world; See and tremble shall the earth.

<span id="xxxv.iv.v-p7"></span>**5** The mountains like wax melted at
the presence of Jehovah, At the presence of the Lord of the whole earth.

<span id="xxxv.iv.v-p8"></span>**6** Declared have the heavens his
righteousness, And seen have all the peoples his glory.

<span id="xxxv.iv.v-p9"></span>**7** Confounded be all those who serve
graven images, Who glory in *their* inventions: Worship before him let
all the gods.

<span id="xxxv.iv.v-p10"></span>**8** Heard and rejoiced hath Zion;
Exulted have the daughters of Judah, Because of thy judgments, O
Jehovah!

<span id="xxxv.iv.v-p11"></span>**9** For thou, O Jehovah! *art* high
above all the earth: Exceedingly exalted art thou above all gods.

<span id="xxxv.iv.v-p12"></span>**10** Ye who love Jehovah, hate evil:
He preserveth the souls of his meek ones; From the hand of the ungodly
he will deliver them.

<span id="xxxv.iv.v-p13"></span>**11** Light is sown for the righteous,
And for the upright in heart joy.

<span id="xxxv.iv.v-p14"></span>**12** Rejoice, O ye righteous! in
Jehovah, And celebrate the memory of his holiness.

<span id="xxxv.iv.vi"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iv.vi-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iv.vi-p2"></span>PSALM 98

<span id="xxxv.iv.vi-p3"></span>A Psalm

<span id="xxxv.iv.vi-p4"></span>**1** Sing ye to Jehovah a song that is
new, For marvels he hath done: Salvation wrought for him hath his own
right hand, And the arm of his holiness.

<span id="xxxv.iv.vi-p5"></span>**2** Made known hath Jehovah his
salvation: In the sight of the heathen he hath revealed his
righteousness.

<span id="xxxv.iv.vi-p6"></span>**3** He hath remembered his goodness
and *his* truth towards the house of Israel: Seen have all the ends of
the earth the salvation of our God.

<span id="xxxv.iv.vi-p7"></span>**4** Exult to Jehovah all the earth;
Make a loud noise, and exult, and sing psalms.

<span id="xxxv.iv.vi-p8"></span>**5** Sing psalms to Jehovah upon the
harp, Upon the harp, and with the voice of song:

<span id="xxxv.iv.vi-p9"></span>**6** With trumpets, and the voice of
the cornet, Sing psalms before the King, Jehovah.

<span id="xxxv.iv.vi-p10"></span>**7** Roar let the sea, and the
fullness thereof; The world, and those who dwell therein.

<span id="xxxv.iv.vi-p11"></span>**8** Let the floods clap the hand:
Together let the mountains exult

<span id="xxxv.iv.vi-p12"></span>**9** Before Jehovah: for he cometh to
judge the earth; He shall judge the world in righteousness, And the
peoples with rectitude.

<span id="xxxv.iv.vii"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iv.vii-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iv.vii-p2"></span>PSALM 99

<span id="xxxv.iv.vii-p3"></span>**1** Jehovah reigneth; tremble let the
people: He dwelleth *between* the cherubim; moved let be the earth.

<span id="xxxv.iv.vii-p4"></span>**2** Jehovah in Zion is great; And
exalted is he above all nations.

<span id="xxxv.iv.vii-p5"></span>**3** They shall acknowledge thy great
and terrible name: It is holy.

<span id="xxxv.iv.vii-p6"></span>**4** And the strength of the king
loveth judgment; Thou hast established rectitude; Judgement and
righteousness in Jacob thou hast done.

<span id="xxxv.iv.vii-p7"></span>**5** Exalt ye Jehovah our God, And
worship at his footstool: He is holy.

<span id="xxxv.iv.vii-p8"></span>**6** Moses and Aaron among his
priests, And Samuel among those who call upon his name; They cried to
Jehovah and he answered them.

<span id="xxxv.iv.vii-p9"></span>**7** In the pillar of the cloud he
spake to them: They kept his testimonies And his statutes which he gave
them.

<span id="xxxv.iv.vii-p10"></span>**8** O Jehovah, our God! thou didst
answer them: A God propitious thou wast to them, And \[*yet*\] taking
vengeance upon their works.

<span id="xxxv.iv.vii-p11"></span>**9** Exalt ye Jehovah our God, And
worship at the mountain of his holiness; For holy *is* Jehovah our God.

<span id="xxxv.iv.viii"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iv.viii-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iv.viii-p2"></span>PSALM 100

<span id="xxxv.iv.viii-p3"></span>A Psalm for praising

<span id="xxxv.iv.viii-p4"></span>**1** Sing aloud to Jehovah,  <span
id="fr_364"></span>[365](#fn_364) all ye *inhabitants* of the earth.

<span id="xxxv.iv.viii-p6"></span>**2** Serve Jehovah with gladness;
