Come into his presence with exultation.

<span id="xxxv.iv.viii-p7"></span>**3** Know that Jehovah He is God; He
made us, and not we ourselves: *We are* his people, and the flock of his
pasture.

<span id="xxxv.iv.viii-p8"></span>**4** Enter his gates with praise, his
courts with exultation; Celebrate him,  <span
id="fr_365"></span>[366](#fn_365) bless his name:

<span id="xxxv.iv.viii-p10"></span>**5** For good is Jehovah, For ever
*endureth* his mercy, And from generation to generation his truth.

<span id="xxxv.iv.ix"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iv.ix-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iv.ix-p2"></span>PSALM 101

<span id="xxxv.iv.ix-p3"></span>A Psalm of David

<span id="xxxv.iv.ix-p4"></span>**1** Of mercy and judgment I will sing;
To thee, O Jehovah, will I sing psalms.

<span id="xxxv.iv.ix-p5"></span>**2** I will act wisely in a perfect
way, Until thou comest to me; I will walk in the integrity of my heart
in the midst of my house.

<span id="xxxv.iv.ix-p6"></span>**3** I will not set before my eyes a
wicked thing; The work of those who turn aside I hate; It shall not
adhere to me.

<span id="xxxv.iv.ix-p7"></span>**4** A heart perverse shall depart from
me; Evil I will not know.

<span id="xxxv.iv.ix-p8"></span>**5** He who slandereth in secret his
neighbor, him will I destroy: The lofty in look and the wide in heart
him I will not suffer.

<span id="xxxv.iv.ix-p9"></span>**6** My eyes *shall be* upon the
faithful of the land, That they may dwell with me: He who walketh in an
upright way, \[*Even*\] he shall minister to me.

<span id="xxxv.iv.ix-p10"></span>**7** He shall not dwell in the midst
of my house, he who worketh deceit; He who speaketh lies shall not be
established before my eyes.

<span id="xxxv.iv.ix-p11"></span>**8** Early will I destroy all the
ungodly of the land; That I may cut off from the city of Jehovah all the
workers of iniquity.

<span id="xxxv.iv.x"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iv.x-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iv.x-p2"></span>PSALM 102

<span id="xxxv.iv.x-p3"></span>A Prayer for the afflicted when he shall
be shut up, and shall pour out his meditation before Jehovah

<span id="xxxv.iv.x-p4"></span>**1** O Jehovah! hear my prayer, And let
my cry to thee come.

<span id="xxxv.iv.x-p5"></span>**2** Hide not thy face from me in the
day of my afflictions; Incline to me thy ear; In the day when I cry,
make haste, answer me.

<span id="xxxv.iv.x-p6"></span>**3** For consumed like smoke are  <span
id="fr_366"></span>[367](#fn_366) my days, And my bones as a hearth are
burnt up.

<span id="xxxv.iv.x-p8"></span>**4** Smitten like grass, and withered is
my heart, Because I have forgotten to eat my bread.

<span id="xxxv.iv.x-p9"></span>**5** By reason of the voice of my
groaning, Cleave do my bones to my flesh.

<span id="xxxv.iv.x-p10"></span>**6** I am become like a pelican of the
desert, I am become as an owl of the solitudes;

<span id="xxxv.iv.x-p11"></span>**7** I have watched and am as the
sparrow *Which is* solitary upon the roof of the house.

<span id="xxxv.iv.x-p12"></span>**8** Daily reproach me do my enemies;
And those who are mad against me, by me have sworn.

<span id="xxxv.iv.x-p13"></span>**9** For ashes as bread I have eaten,
And my drink with weeping  <span id="fr_367"></span>[368](#fn_367) I
have mingled.

<span id="xxxv.iv.x-p15"></span>**10** Because of thy indignation and
thy wrath; For thou hast lifted me up and cast me down.

<span id="xxxv.iv.x-p16"></span>**11** My days *are* as a shadow which
declineth; And as grass I am dried up.

<span id="xxxv.iv.x-p17"></span>**12** And thou, O Jehovah! for ever
shalt dwell, And thy memorial from generation to generation.

<span id="xxxv.iv.x-p18"></span>**13** Thou thyself shalt arise, thou
shalt have mercy upon Zion; For it is time to compassionate her, For
come is the appointed time.

<span id="xxxv.iv.x-p19"></span>**14** For take pleasure do thy servants
in her stones, And upon her dust they will have compassion.

<span id="xxxv.iv.x-p20"></span>**15** And fear shall the Gentiles the
name of Jehovah, And all the kings of the earth thy glory.

<span id="xxxv.iv.x-p21"></span>**16** For Jehovah hath builded Zion, He
hath appeared in his glory.

<span id="xxxv.iv.x-p22"></span>**17** He hath regarded the prayer of
the solitary, And hath not despised their prayer.

<span id="xxxv.iv.x-p23"></span>**18** This shall be written for the
generation to come, And the people \[*to be*\] created shall praise him.

<span id="xxxv.iv.x-p24"></span>**19** For he hath looked from the high
*place* of his holiness, Jehovah from the heavens upon the earth hath
looked,

<span id="xxxv.iv.x-p25"></span>**20** To hear the groaning of the
prisoners To release the sons of death;

<span id="xxxv.iv.x-p26"></span>**21** That declared in Zion may be the
name of Jehovah, And his praise in Jerusalem;

<span id="xxxv.iv.x-p27"></span>**22** When gathered shall be the
peoples together, And the kingdoms to serve Jehovah.

<span id="xxxv.iv.x-p28"></span>**23** He hath afflicted in the way my
strength, He hath shortened my days.

<span id="xxxv.iv.x-p29"></span>**24** I said, O my God! take me not
away in the midst of my days; *For* throughout generations of
generations *are* thy years.

<span id="xxxv.iv.x-p30"></span>**25** Aforetime the earth thou hast
founded; And the work of thy hands serve the heavens.

<span id="xxxv.iv.x-p31"></span>**26** They shall perish but thou shalt
endure; And they all as a garment shall grow old; As a vesture thou
shalt change them, and they shall be changed.

<span id="xxxv.iv.x-p32"></span>**27** But thou *art always* the same,
And thy years shall not fail.

<span id="xxxv.iv.x-p33"></span>**28** The children of thy servants
shall dwell, And their seed before thee shall be established.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xi"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iv.xi-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iv.xi-p2"></span>PSALM 103

<span id="xxxv.iv.xi-p3"></span>Of David

<span id="xxxv.iv.xi-p4"></span>**1** Bless, O my soul! Jehovah, And all
my inward parts *bless* his holy name.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xi-p5"></span>**2** Bless, O my soul! Jehovah, And
forget not all his bounties.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xi-p6"></span>**3** Who forgiveth all thy iniquities;
Who healeth all thy infirmities;

<span id="xxxv.iv.xi-p7"></span>**4** Who redeemeth from the grave thy
life; Who crowneth thee with mercy and compassions;

<span id="xxxv.iv.xi-p8"></span>**5** Who satisfieth with good thy
mouth: Renewed as *that* of the eagle shall be thy youth.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xi-p9"></span>**6** Execute doth Jehovah righteousness
And judgments for all who are oppressed.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xi-p10"></span>**7** He made known his ways to Moses,
To the children of Israel his doings.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xi-p11"></span>**8** Compassionate and merciful *is*
Jehovah, Slow to anger and abundant in goodness.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xi-p12"></span>**9** He will not always chide; Neither
for ever will he keep \[*his anger*.\]

<span id="xxxv.iv.xi-p13"></span>**10** Not according to our sins hath
he dealt with us, Nor according to our iniquities hath he recompensed
us.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xi-p14"></span>**11** For in proportion to the height
of the heavens above the earth, Hath been the greatness of his goodness
upon those who fear him.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xi-p15"></span>**12** As far distant as is the east
from the west, So far hath he removed from us our sills.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xi-p16"></span>**13** As a father is compassionate
towards his children, So is Jehovah compassionate towards those who fear
him.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xi-p17"></span>**14** For he knoweth of what we are
made; He hath remembered that dust are we.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xi-p18"></span>**15** Man... as grass *are* his days:
As a flower of the field, so he flourisheth.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xi-p19"></span>**16** As soon as the wind passeth over
it, it is not; And know it no more shall the place thereof.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xi-p20"></span>**17** But the goodness of Jehovah *is*
from everlasting to everlasting upon those who fear him, And his
righteousness upon the children’s children;

<span id="xxxv.iv.xi-p21"></span>**18** To those who keep his covenant,
And are mindful of his statutes to do them.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xi-p22"></span>**19** Jehovah in the heavens hath
established his throne; And his kingdom over all hath dominion.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xi-p23"></span>**20** Bless Jehovah, *ye* his angels
mighty in strength! Who do his commandment, in hearing the voice of his
word.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xi-p24"></span>**21** Bless Jehovah, all *ye* his
armies! Ye ministers of his, who do his pleasure.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xi-p25"></span>**22** Bless Jehovah, all ye his works!
In all places of his dominion: Bless, O my soul! Jehovah.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xii"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iv.xii-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iv.xii-p2"></span>PSALM 104

<span id="xxxv.iv.xii-p3"></span>**1** Bless, O my soul! Jehovah: O
Jehovah, my God! thou art great exceedingly; With praise and honor thou
hast clothed thyself.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xii-p4"></span>**2** Being arrayed with light as with
a garment; Spreading out the heavens as a curtain;

<span id="xxxv.iv.xii-p5"></span>**3** Flooring in the waters his upper
rooms; Making the clouds his chariot; Walking upon the wings of the
wind:

<span id="xxxv.iv.xii-p6"></span>**4** Making the winds his messengers;
His ministers a fire that flameth.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xii-p7"></span>**5** He hath founded the earth upon
its foundations, So that it shall not be moved for ever.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xii-p8"></span>**6** With the deep as with a garment
he hath covered it: Above the mountains stand shall the waters.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xii-p9"></span>**7** At thy rebuke they shall flee; At
the voice of thy thunder they shall suddenly pass away.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xii-p10"></span>**8** Ascend shall the mountains and
descend shall the valleys To the place which thou hast founded for them.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xii-p11"></span>**9** A boundary thou hast set, they
shall not pass over *it*: They shall not return to cover the earth.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xii-p12"></span>**10** Sending out springs by the
valleys, *Which* between the hills shall run.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xii-p13"></span>**11** Drink *thereof* shall all the
beasts of the field: Quench shall the wild asses their thirst.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xii-p14"></span>**12** Nigh time the fowl of the
heaven shall dwell, From the midst of the branches they shall send out
their voice.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xii-p15"></span>**13** Watering the mountains from his
chambers: From the fruit of thy works satisfied shall be the earth.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xii-p16"></span>**14** Making grass to grow for
cattle, And herb for the service of mm: That he may bring forth bread
out of the earth.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xii-p17"></span>**15** And wine cheereth the heart of
man, To make *his* face to shine with oil, And bread sustaineth the
heart of man.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xii-p18"></span>**16** Satiated shall be the trees of
Jehovah; The cedars of Lebanon which he hath planted:

<span id="xxxv.iv.xii-p19"></span>**17** For there the birds build their
nests: \[*As for*\] the stork, the fir trees are her dwelling.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xii-p20"></span>**18** The high mountains *are* for
the deer; The rocks a place of shelter for the hedgehogs.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xii-p21"></span>**19** He hath made the moon for set
times: The sun knoweth his going down.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xii-p22"></span>**20** Thou makest darkness, and it is
night; Wherein do creep forth all the beasts of the forest.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xii-p23"></span>**21** The lions roar after their
prey, And in seeking from God their food.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xii-p24"></span>**22** Rise shall the sun, and they
shall gather themselves together, And in their dens shall lie down.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xii-p25"></span>**23** Go forth shall man to his work,
And to his labor, until the evening.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xii-p26"></span>**24** How magnificent are thy works!
O Jehovah! All things in wisdom thou hast made: Filled is the earth with
thy riches.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xii-p27"></span>**25** This sea great, and wide in
extent; Therein are creeping things inntanerable, Beasts both small and
great.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xii-p28"></span>**26** There the ships go, And the
leviathan, which thou hast formed to sport in it.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xii-p29"></span>**27** All things on thee do wait,
That thou mayest give *them* their food in its season.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xii-p30"></span>**28** Thou shalt give it them, they
shall gather \[*it*:\] Thou shalt open thy hand, they shall be satisfied
with good.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xii-p31"></span>**29** Thou shalt hide thy face, they
shall be afraid: Thou shalt take away their spirit, they shall die, and
to their dust shall return.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xii-p32"></span>**30** Thou shalt send forth thy
Spirit, they shall be created: And thou shalt renew the face of the
earth.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xii-p33"></span>**31** Glory be to Jehovah for ever:
Rejoice let Jehovah in his works.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xii-p34"></span>**32** He looketh upon the earth, and
it trembleth: If he touch the mountains, they shall smoke.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xii-p35"></span>**33** I will sing to Jehovah whilst I
live: I will sing psalms to my God as long as I have my being.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xii-p36"></span>**34** Let my speech be acceptable to
him: I will rejoice in Jehovah.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xii-p37"></span>**35** Perish let sinners from the
earth, And the ungodly till they cease to be any more. Bless, O my soul!
Jehovah. Hallelujah.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiii"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiii-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiii-p2"></span>PSALM 105

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiii-p3"></span>**1** Celebrate ye Jehovah; invoke his
name: Announce among the peoples his works.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiii-p4"></span>**2** Sing ye to him: sing psalms to
him: Speak of all his wonders.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiii-p5"></span>**3** Rejoice ye in his holy name:
Rejoice let the heart of those who seek Jehovah.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiii-p6"></span>**4** Seek ye Jehovah, and his
strength; Seek his face continually.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiii-p7"></span>**5** Remember the marvelous works
which he hath done; His wonders, and the judgments of his mouth.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiii-p8"></span>**6** *Ye* seed of Abraham, his
servant, The sons of Jacob his chosen one:

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiii-p9"></span>**7** He *is* Jehovah our God; Through
all the earth are his judgments.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiii-p10"></span>**8** He hath remembered for ever his
covenant, The word *which* he commanded to a thousand generations:

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiii-p11"></span>**9** Which he made with Abraham, And
his oath *which he swore* to Isaac;

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiii-p12"></span>**10** And established it to Jacob
for a law, To Israel for an everlasting covenant:

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiii-p13"></span>**11** Saying, “To thee will I give
the land of Canaan, “The cord of your inheritance.”

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiii-p14"></span>**12** When they were very few in
number; And strangers in it;

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiii-p15"></span>**13** And walked about from nation
to nation, From *one* kingdom to another people,

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiii-p16"></span>**14** He did not suffer men to hurt
them; And rebuked for their sake kings;

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiii-p17"></span>**15** *Saying*, “Touch not my
anointed ones, “And to my prophets do no harm.”

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiii-p18"></span>**16** And he called a famine upon
the land; All the stall of bread he broke.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiii-p19"></span>**17** He sent before them a man, For
a slave sold was Joseph.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiii-p20"></span>**18** They afflicted in the fetters
his feet: The iron entered into his soul:

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiii-p21"></span>**19** Until the time that his word
came: The word of Jehovah tried him.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiii-p22"></span>**20** Send did the king and loosed
him; Even the ruler of the peoples, and freed him.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiii-p23"></span>**21** He made him lord over his
house; And ruler over all his substance:

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiii-p24"></span>**22** To bind his princes at his
pleasure; And to teach his elders wisdom.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiii-p25"></span>**23** And come did Israel into
Egypt; And Jacob sojourned in the land of Ham.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiii-p26"></span>**24** And he increased his people
exceedingly, He multiplied them above their oppressors.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiii-p27"></span>**25** He turned their heart so that
they hated his people, And dealt craftily with his servants.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiii-p28"></span>**26** He sent Moses, his servant;
Aaron, whom he chose.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiii-p29"></span>**27** They set among them the words
of his signs, And *his* miracles in the land of Ham.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiii-p30"></span>**28** He sent darkness, and made it
dark; And they were not rebellious against his words.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiii-p31"></span>**29** He turned their waters into
blood, And killed their fish.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiii-p32"></span>**30** Their land brought forth
frogs, *Yea even* within the chambers of their kings.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiii-p33"></span>**31** He spake and there came a
swarm of flies, Lice in all their borders.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiii-p34"></span>**32** He gave them for rain, hail,
Flaming fire upon their land.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiii-p35"></span>**33** And he smote their vines and
their fig-trees; And destroyed *every* tree of their border.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiii-p36"></span>**34** He spake, and there came the
locust, And the caterpillar without number;

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiii-p37"></span>**35** And they devoured all the
herbage in their land, And consumed the fruit of their ground.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiii-p38"></span>**36** And he smote all the firstborn
in their land, The beginning of all their strength.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiii-p39"></span>**37** And he brought them forth with
silver and gold: And not one among their tribes was a feeble person.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiii-p40"></span>**38** Glad was Egypt at their
departure; For fallen upon them had their terror.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiii-p41"></span>**39** He spread out a cloud for a
covering; And fire to give light by the night.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiii-p42"></span>**40** He  <span
id="fr_368"></span>[369](#fn_368) asked, and brought quails, And with
the bread of heaven he filled them.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiii-p44"></span>**41** He opened the rock, and there
gushed out waters; They ran in the dry *places like* a river.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiii-p45"></span>**42** For he remembered the word of
his holiness, *Which he had spoken* to Abraham his servant.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiii-p46"></span>**43** And he brought forth his
people with joy, With exultation his chosen ones.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiii-p47"></span>**44** And he gave them the lands of
the nations: And the labor of the peoples they inherited.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiii-p48"></span>**45** That they might keep his
ordinances, And that his law they might observe. Hallelujah.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiv"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiv-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiv-p2"></span>PSALM 106

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiv-p3"></span>Hallelujah

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiv-p4"></span>**1** Celebrate Jehovah, for he is
good; For to everlasting *is* his mercy.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiv-p5"></span>**2** Who shall express the mighty acts
of Jehovah? Who shall declare all his praise?

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiv-p6"></span>**3** Blessed are they who keep
judgment, *Blessed* is he who doeth righteousness at all times.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiv-p7"></span>**4** Remember me, O Jehovah! with the
good will \[*which thou* *bearest towards*\] thy people. Visit me with
thy salvation;

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiv-p8"></span>**5** That I may see the good of thy
chosen ones, That I may rejoice in the joy of thy nation, That I may
glory with thy heritage.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiv-p9"></span>**6** We have sinned with our fathers,
We have acted iniquitously, we have done wickedly.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiv-p10"></span>**7** Our fathers in Egypt understood
not thy wonders; They remembered not the multitude of thy kindnesses;
And they rebelled at the sea, at the Red Sea.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiv-p11"></span>**8** Yet he saved them for the sake
of his own name, That. he might cause to be known his power.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiv-p12"></span>**9** And he rebuked the Red Sea, and
it was dried up; And he made them walk in the deeps as in a desert.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiv-p13"></span>**10** And he saved them from the hand
of the enemy, And redeemed them from the hand of the adversary.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiv-p14"></span>**11** And cover did the waters their
oppressors: One of them was not left.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiv-p15"></span>**12** Then they believed his words;
They sang his praise.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiv-p16"></span>**13** They made haste, they forgat
his works; They did not wait for his counsel;

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiv-p17"></span>**14** And they lusted greatly in the
desert, And tempted God in the wilderness.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiv-p18"></span>**15** And he gave them their request;
But sent leanness into their souls.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiv-p19"></span>**16** And they envied Moses in the
camp, And Aaron, the saint of Jehovah.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiv-p20"></span>**17** Open did the earth and
swallowed up Dathan, And covered over the tent of Abiram.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiv-p21"></span>**18** And kindled was a fire in their
company, The flame burned up the ungodly.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiv-p22"></span>**19** They made a calf in Horeb, And
worshipped before the molten image.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiv-p23"></span>**20** And they changed their glory
Into the likeness of an ox that eateth hay.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiv-p24"></span>**21** They forgat God their Savior,
Who had done great things in Egypt;

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiv-p25"></span>**22** Miracles in the land of Ham,
Terrible things at the Red Sea.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiv-p26"></span>**23** And he said that he would
destroy them, Unless Moses his chosen had stood in the breach before his
face, To turn away his wrath, that he might not destroy *them*

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiv-p27"></span>**24** And they despised the land of
pleasantness; They believed not his word;

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiv-p28"></span>**25** And they mutinied in their
tents, They hearkened not to the voice of Jehovah.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiv-p29"></span>**26** And he lifted tip his hand
against them, To destroy them in the desert:

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiv-p30"></span>**27** And to scatter their seed among
the heathen, And to disperse them throughout the lands.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiv-p31"></span>**28** And they joined themselves to
Baal-peor, And ate the sacrifices of *things* dead.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiv-p32"></span>**29** And they provoked *God* to
anger by their works: And break in upon them did the plague.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiv-p33"></span>**30** Then stood up Phinehas, and
executed judgment: And stayed was the plague.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiv-p34"></span>**31** And *that* was imputed to him
for righteousness From generation to generation, even for ever.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiv-p35"></span>**32** And they provoked *him* to
anger at the waters of strife, And it turned out in to Moses on their
account:

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiv-p36"></span>**33** For they embittered his spirit,
And he spake \[*rashly*\] with his lips.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiv-p37"></span>**34** They did not destroy the
nations, As Jehovah had commanded them:

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiv-p38"></span>**35** And they were mingled with the
heathen, And learned their works:

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiv-p39"></span>**36** And they served their idols;
Which were to them for ruin.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiv-p40"></span>**37** And they sacrificed their sons
and their daughters to demons;

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiv-p41"></span>**38** And they shed innocent blood,
The blood of their sons and of their daughters, Whom they sacrificed to
the idols of Canaan; And polluted was the land with bloods.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiv-p42"></span>**39** And they were defiled in their
own works, And were adulterous in their own inventions.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiv-p43"></span>**40** Then  <span
id="fr_369"></span>[370](#fn_369) burn did the wrath of Jehovah against
his people, And he abhorred his inheritance;

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiv-p45"></span>**41** And he delivered them into the
hands of the heathen; And those had dominion over them who hated them:

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiv-p46"></span>**42** And subdue them did their
enemies, And they were afflicted under their hand.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiv-p47"></span>**43** Many times did he deliver them;
But they provoked *him* with their counsels, And were oppressed in their
iniquity.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiv-p48"></span>**44** Yet he saw when they were in
distress, And heard their cry:

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiv-p49"></span>**45** And he remembered towards them
his covenant; And it repented him according to the greatness of his
mercies.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiv-p50"></span>**46** And he made them to find pity
Before all who had led them captive.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiv-p51"></span>**47** Save us, O Jehovah, our God!
And gather us from among the heathen, That we may celebrate thy holy
name, That we may glory in thy praise.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xiv-p52"></span>**48** Blessed *be* Jehovah, the God
of Israel, From everlasting to everlasting; And say let all the people,
Amen. Praise ye Jehovah.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xv"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iv.xv-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iv.xv-p2"></span>PART FIFTH.  <span
id="fr_370"></span>[371](#fn_370)

<span id="xxxv.iv.xv-p4"></span>PSALM 107

<span id="xxxv.iv.xv-p5"></span>**1** “Celebrate Jehovah, for he is
good, “For to everlasting is his mercy.”

<span id="xxxv.iv.xv-p6"></span>**2** Say *this* let the redeemed of
Jehovah, Whom he hath redeemed from the hand of the afflicter.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xv-p7"></span>**3** Whom he hath gathered from the
lands, From the east, and from the west, From the north, and from the
south.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xv-p8"></span>**4** They wandered from the way in the
solitary desert; A city of habitation they found not:

<span id="xxxv.iv.xv-p9"></span>**5** Hungry, also thirsty, *So that*
their soul within them fainted.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xv-p10"></span>**6** Then they cried to Jehovah in
their distress, And from their troubles he delivered them.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xv-p11"></span>**7** And he directed them by a right
way, That they might come to a city of habitation.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xv-p12"></span>**8** Let them celebrate before Jehovah
his mercy, His marvelous works before the sons of men.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xv-p13"></span>**9** For he hath satisfied the soul
that longeth, And the soul that is famished he hath filled with good.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xv-p14"></span>**10** Those who dwell in darkness, and
in the shadow of death, Bound in affliction and iron;

<span id="xxxv.iv.xv-p15"></span>**11** Because they rebelled against
the words of God, And the counsel of the Most High they despised:

<span id="xxxv.iv.xv-p16"></span>**12** And he humbled with trouble
their heart; They were afflicted and *there was* none to help *them*

<span id="xxxv.iv.xv-p17"></span>**13** They cried to Jehovah in their
distress: From their troubles he delivered them.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xv-p18"></span>**14** He rescued them from darkness
and the shadow of death, And their chains he broke asunder.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xv-p19"></span>**15** Let them celebrate before
Jehovah his mercy, And his marvelous works before the sons of men.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xv-p20"></span>**16** For he hath broken the gates of
brass, And the bars of iron he hath shivered.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xv-p21"></span>**17** Fools on account of the way of
their transgression; And on account of their iniquities are afflicted.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xv-p22"></span>**18** All food loathe doth their soul;
And they approach the gates of death.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xv-p23"></span>**19** Then they cry to Jehovah in
their trouble: From their straits he sayeth them.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xv-p24"></span>**20** He sendeth his word, and healeth
them, And rescueth them from all their corruptions.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xv-p25"></span>**21** Let them celebrate before
Jehovah his mercy, And his marvelous works before the sons of men.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xv-p26"></span>**22** And let them sacrifice
sacrifices of praise, And announce his works with exultation.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xv-p27"></span>**23** Those who go down to the sea in
ships, Trading in the great waters,

<span id="xxxv.iv.xv-p28"></span>**24** These men see the works of
Jehovah, His wonders in the deep.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xv-p29"></span>**25** He speaketh and raiseth the wind
of storm, And lifteth high the waves thereof.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xv-p30"></span>**26** They mount up to the heavens,
They descend into the deeps; Their soul in  <span
id="fr_371"></span>[372](#fn_371) *their* distress is melted away.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xv-p32"></span>**27** They are tossed and stagger as a
drunken man, And all their skill is swallowed up.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xv-p33"></span>**28** And they cry to Jehovah in their
distress, And from their troubles he bringeth them out.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xv-p34"></span>**29** He maketh the storm a calm, So
that quiet are the waves thereof.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xv-p35"></span>**30** And they rejoice because they
are stilled; And he leadeth them unto the haven of their desire.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xv-p36"></span>**31** Let them celebrate before
Jehovah his mercy, And his wonders before the sons of men;

<span id="xxxv.iv.xv-p37"></span>**32** And let them exalt him in the
congregation of the people, And in the assembly of the elders let them
praise him.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xv-p38"></span>**33** He turneth rivers into a desert,
And springs of water into dryness;

<span id="xxxv.iv.xv-p39"></span>**34** A land that is fruitful into
saltness, For the wickedness of those who dwell therein.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xv-p40"></span>**35** He turneth the desert into a
pool of water, And the land of barrenness into springs of water.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xv-p41"></span>**36** And there he causeth to dwell
the famished, That they may prepare a city of habitation;

<span id="xxxv.iv.xv-p42"></span>**37** And sow fields, and plant
vineyards, And eat the fruit of increase.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xv-p43"></span>**38** And he blesseth them, and they
multiply exceedingly; And their cattle he doth not diminish,.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xv-p44"></span>**39** Afterwards they are diminished
and brought low, By reason of anguish, affliction, and sorrow.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xv-p45"></span>**40** He poureth contempt upon
princes, And maketh them to wander in the waste where there is no path.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xv-p46"></span>**41** And he raiseth the afflicted
from *his* misery, And maketh like a flock \[*his*\] families.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xv-p47"></span>**42** See shall the upright ones and
shall rejoice: And all iniquity shall stop her mouth.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xv-p48"></span>**43** Who is wise, and he will observe
these things, And they shall understand the loving-kindness of Jehovah?

<span id="xxxv.iv.xvi"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iv.xvi-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iv.xvi-p2"></span>PSALM 108

<span id="xxxv.iv.xvi-p3"></span>A Song of a Psalm of David

<span id="xxxv.iv.xvi-p4"></span>**1** Prepared *is* my heart, O God!
prepared is my heart, I will chant and will sing psalms, even with my
glory.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xvi-p5"></span>**2** Awake, psaltery and harp: I will
arise at the dawn of day.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xvi-p6"></span>**3** I will celebrate thee, among the
peoples, O Jehovah! And will sing psalms to thee among the nations:

<span id="xxxv.iv.xvi-p7"></span>**4** For great above the heavens, is
thy goodness; And unto the clouds is thy truth.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xvi-p8"></span>**5** Be thou exalted above the
heavens, O God! And above all the earth thy glory:

<span id="xxxv.iv.xvi-p9"></span>**6** That thy beloved ones may be
delivered: Save by thy right hand, and hear me.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xvi-p10"></span>**7** God hath spoken in his holiness;
I will rejoice: I will divide Shechem, And the valley of Succoth I will
measure.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xvi-p11"></span>**8** Mine *is* Gilead, mine is
Manasseh; And Ephraim *is* the strength of my head; Judah my lawgiver.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xvi-p12"></span>**9** Moab the pot for my washing;
Over Edom will I cast my shoe; Over Palestina will I triumph.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xvi-p13"></span>**10** Who will lead me into the city
fortified? Who will lead me even into Edom?

<span id="xxxv.iv.xvi-p14"></span>**11** Wilt not thou, O God! who hadst
cast us off? And \[*thou*\] O God! \[*who*\] didst not go forth with our
armies?

<span id="xxxv.iv.xvi-p15"></span>**12** Grant us relief from  <span
id="fr_372"></span>[373](#fn_372) trouble; For vain is the help of man.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xvi-p17"></span>**13** Through God we shall do
valiantly, And he shall tread down our adversaries.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xvii"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iv.xvii-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iv.xvii-p2"></span>PSALM 109

<span id="xxxv.iv.xvii-p3"></span>To the Chief Musician. A Psalm of
David

<span id="xxxv.iv.xvii-p4"></span>**1** O God of my praise! be not
silent;

<span id="xxxv.iv.xvii-p5"></span>**2** For the mouth of the ungodly
man, and the mouth of deceit upon me are opened; They have talked with
me with a tongue of guile:

<span id="xxxv.iv.xvii-p6"></span>**3** And with words of hatred they
have encompassed me, And have fought against me without a cause.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xvii-p7"></span>**4** \[*In return*\] for my love they
have been my adversaries; But I *set myself* to prayer.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xvii-p8"></span>**5** And they have requited me evil
for good, And hatred for my love.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xvii-p9"></span>**6** Set thou over him an ungodly
man; And let the adversary stand at his right hand.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xvii-p10"></span>**7** When he is judged let him go
forth condemned,  <span id="fr_373"></span>[374](#fn_373) And let his
prayer be turned into sin.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xvii-p12"></span>**8** Let his days be few; His office
let another receive.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xvii-p13"></span>**9** Let his children be fatherless,
And his wife a widow.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xvii-p14"></span>**10** And in wandering let his
children wander and beg,  <span id="fr_374"></span>[375](#fn_374) And
seek \[*for bread*\] out of their waste places.  <span
id="fr_375"></span>[376](#fn_375)

<span id="xxxv.iv.xvii-p17"></span>**11** Catch let the extortioner all
which he hath, And let strangers plunder his labor.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xvii-p18"></span>**12** Let there be none prolonging
mercy to him; And let there be none to have compassion upon his orphans.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xvii-p19"></span>**13** Let his posterity be
destroyed;  <span id="fr_376"></span>[377](#fn_376) In the generation
following let their name be blotted out.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xvii-p21"></span>**14** Remembered let be the iniquity
of his fathers before Jehovah; And the wickedness  <span
id="fr_377"></span>[378](#fn_377) of his mother let it not be blotted
out.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xvii-p23"></span>**15** Let them be before Jehovah
continually, And let him blot out from the earth their memorial;

<span id="xxxv.iv.xvii-p24"></span>**16** Because he remembered not to
do mercy, And persecuted the man \[*that was*\] wretched and poor, And
afflicted in heart, to put *him* to death.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xvii-p25"></span>**17** He loved cursing, and let it
come upon him: He delighted not in blessing, and let it be far from him.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xvii-p26"></span>**18** And let him be clothed with
cursing as with a garment; And let it come as water into his entrails,
And as oil into his bones.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xvii-p27"></span>**19** Let it be to him as a mantle
to cover him, And as a girdle with which continually he may gird himself

<span id="xxxv.iv.xvii-p28"></span>**20** Let this be the recompense
 <span id="fr_378"></span>[379](#fn_378) of my adversaries from Jehovah,
And of those who speak evil against my soul.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xvii-p30"></span>**21** But thou, O Jehovah, my Lord!
deal thou with me for the sake of thy name: Because good *is* thy mercy,
deliver me;

<span id="xxxv.iv.xvii-p31"></span>**22** For poor and needy I am, And
my heart is wounded within me.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xvii-p32"></span>**23** As a shadow when it declineth,
I walk about; I am shaken off as the locust.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xvii-p33"></span>**24** My knees are become feeble
through fasting; And my flesh hath fallen away from *its* fatness.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xvii-p34"></span>**25** But I am become a reproach to
them; When they see me they shake their head.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xvii-p35"></span>**26** Help me, O Jehovah, my God!
Save me according to thy mercy.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xvii-p36"></span>**27** And they shall know that this
is thy hand, *That* thou, O Jehovah! hast done it.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xvii-p37"></span>**28** They shall curse, but thou
shalt bless; When they rise up they shall be put to shame; But thy
servant shall rejoice.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xvii-p38"></span>**29** Clothed shall be my
adversaries with disgrace, And they shall be covered as with a garment
with their own shame.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xvii-p39"></span>**30** I will praise Jehovah greatly
with my mouth; And in the midst of the great I will celebrate him:

<span id="xxxv.iv.xvii-p40"></span>**31** Because he standeth at the
right hand of the poor one, To save from condemnations his soul.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xviii"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iv.xviii-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iv.xviii-p2"></span>PSALM 110

<span id="xxxv.iv.xviii-p3"></span>A Psalm of David

<span id="xxxv.iv.xviii-p4"></span>**1** Jehovah said to my Lord, “Sit
thou at my right hand, “Until I make thy enemies thy footstool.”

<span id="xxxv.iv.xviii-p5"></span>**2** The scepter of thy power send
shall Jehovah out of Zion: Rule thou in the midst of thy enemies.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xviii-p6"></span>**3** Thy people *shall come* with
voluntary offerings, On the day *of the assembling* of thy army, In
beauty of holiness: From the womb as from the morning dawn To thee *has
been* the dew of thy youth.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xviii-p7"></span>**4** Sworn hath Jehovah, and he will
not repent: “Thou art a priest for ever “According to the manner of
Melchisedek.”

<span id="xxxv.iv.xviii-p8"></span>**5** The Lord at thy right hand Hath
crushed in the day of his wrath kings.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xviii-p9"></span>**6** He shall judge among the
heathen, He shall fill *all* with ruins; He shall crush the head over a
great country.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xviii-p10"></span>**7** Of the torrent in the way he
shall drink, Therefore shall he lift up the head.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xix"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iv.xix-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iv.xix-p2"></span>PSALM 111

<span id="xxxv.iv.xix-p3"></span>Hallelujah

<span id="xxxv.iv.xix-p4"></span>**1** <span
id="xxxv.iv.xix-p4.1"></span>א I will celebrate Jehovah with *my* whole
heart, <span id="xxxv.iv.xix-p4.2"></span>ב In the congregation of the
just, and in the assembly.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xix-p5"></span>**2** <span
id="xxxv.iv.xix-p5.1"></span>ג Great are the works of Jehovah, <span
id="xxxv.iv.xix-p5.2"></span>ד Sought out of all who have pleasure in
them.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xix-p6"></span>**3** <span
id="xxxv.iv.xix-p6.1"></span>ה Beautiful and honorable  <span
id="fr_379"></span>[380](#fn_379) *is* his work; <span
id="xxxv.iv.xix-p7.1"></span>ו And his righteousness endureth for ever.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xix-p8"></span>**4** <span
id="xxxv.iv.xix-p8.1"></span>ז He hath made a memorial by his wonderful
works: <span id="xxxv.iv.xix-p8.2"></span>ח Merciful and compassionate
*is* Jehovah.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xix-p9"></span>**5** <span
id="xxxv.iv.xix-p9.1"></span>ט A portion he hath given to those who fear
him: <span id="xxxv.iv.xix-p9.2"></span>י He will remember for ever his
covenant.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xix-p10"></span>**6** <span
id="xxxv.iv.xix-p10.1"></span>כ The might of his works he hath
proclaimed to his people, <span id="xxxv.iv.xix-p10.2"></span>ל To give
them the heritage of the heathen.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xix-p11"></span>**7** <span
id="xxxv.iv.xix-p11.1"></span>מ The works of his hands *are* truth and
judgment: <span id="xxxv.iv.xix-p11.2"></span>נ True *are* all his
statutes,

<span id="xxxv.iv.xix-p12"></span>**8** <span
id="xxxv.iv.xix-p12.1"></span>ס And established for ever — <span
id="xxxv.iv.xix-p12.2"></span>ע Made in truth and rectitude.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xix-p13"></span>**9** <span
id="xxxv.iv.xix-p13.1"></span>פ Redemption he hath sent to his people;
<span id="xxxv.iv.xix-p13.2"></span>ץ He hath commanded for ever his
covenant: <span id="xxxv.iv.xix-p13.3"></span>ק Holy and terrible *is*
his name.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xix-p14"></span>**10** <span
id="xxxv.iv.xix-p14.1"></span>ר The beginning of wisdom is the fear of
Jehovah; <span id="xxxv.iv.xix-p14.2"></span>ש A good understanding
*have* all those who do them: <span id="xxxv.iv.xix-p14.3"></span>ת His
praise endureth for ever.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xx"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iv.xx-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iv.xx-p2"></span>PSALM 112

<span id="xxxv.iv.xx-p3"></span>Hallelujah

<span id="xxxv.iv.xx-p4"></span>**1** <span
id="xxxv.iv.xx-p4.1"></span>א Blessed is the man who feareth Jehovah;
<span id="xxxv.iv.xx-p4.2"></span>ב In his commandments he will delight
greatly.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xx-p5"></span>**2** <span
id="xxxv.iv.xx-p5.1"></span>ג Mighty on the earth shall be his seed:
<span id="xxxv.iv.xx-p5.2"></span>ד The generation of the upright ones
shall be blessed.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xx-p6"></span>**3** <span
id="xxxv.iv.xx-p6.1"></span>ה Wealth and riches *shall be* in his house;
<span id="xxxv.iv.xx-p6.2"></span>ו And his righteousness endureth for
ever.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xx-p7"></span>**4** <span
id="xxxv.iv.xx-p7.1"></span>ז There ariseth in darkness light to the
upright ones: <span id="xxxv.iv.xx-p7.2"></span>ח *He is* merciful and
compassionate and righteous.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xx-p8"></span>**5** <span
id="xxxv.iv.xx-p8.1"></span>ט A good man showeth pity and lendeth; <span
id="xxxv.iv.xx-p8.2"></span>י He manageth his affairs  <span
id="fr_380"></span>[381](#fn_380) in uprightness.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xx-p10"></span>**6** <span
id="xxxv.iv.xx-p10.1"></span>כ Truly he shall not for ever be moved;
<span id="xxxv.iv.xx-p10.2"></span>ל In everlasting remembrance shall be
the righteous one.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xx-p11"></span>**7** <span
id="xxxv.iv.xx-p11.1"></span>מ Of evil tidings he shall not be afraid;
<span id="xxxv.iv.xx-p11.2"></span>נ Established is his heart, because
he trusteth in Jehovah.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xx-p12"></span>**8** <span
id="xxxv.iv.xx-p12.1"></span>ס Sustained *is* his heart, he shall not be
afraid, <span id="xxxv.iv.xx-p12.2"></span>ע Until he see *his* *desire*
upon his adversaries.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xx-p13"></span>**9** <span
id="xxxv.iv.xx-p13.1"></span>פ He hath dispersed; he hath given to the
poor ones; <span id="xxxv.iv.xx-p13.2"></span>ץ His righteousness
continueth for ever; <span id="xxxv.iv.xx-p13.3"></span>ק His horn shall
be exalted with glory.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xx-p14"></span>**10** <span
id="xxxv.iv.xx-p14.1"></span>ר The ungodly one shall see *it*, and be
incensed; <span id="xxxv.iv.xx-p14.2"></span>ש With his teeth he shall
gnash and waste away: <span id="xxxv.iv.xx-p14.3"></span>ת The desire of
the ungodly ones shall perish.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxi"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxi-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxi-p2"></span>PSALM 113

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxi-p3"></span>Hallelujah

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxi-p4"></span>**1** Praise ye, O ye servants of
Jehovah! Praise ye the name of Jehovah.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxi-p5"></span>**2** Let the name of Jehovah be
blessed, From henceforth and for ever.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxi-p6"></span>**3** From the rising of the sun even
to his going down, Worthy to be praised *is* the name of Jehovah.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxi-p7"></span>**4** High above all nations *is*
Jehovah, Above the heavens is his glory.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxi-p8"></span>**5** Who *is* like Jehovah our God,

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxi-p9"></span>**6** Who hath his dwelling on high,
 <span id="fr_381"></span>[382](#fn_381) Who humbleth himself to behold
*that which* is done in heaven and on earth?

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxi-p11"></span>**7** Who raiseth from the dust the
needy one; From the dunghill he lifteth up the wretched one;

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxi-p12"></span>**8** To make him sit with princes,
With the princes of his people.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxi-p13"></span>**9** Who causeth the barren woman to
dwell with a family, Rejoicing that *she is* a mother of children.
Hallelujah.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxii"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxii-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxii-p2"></span>PSALM 114

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxii-p3"></span>**1** When Israel went forth from
Egypt, The house of Jacob from a people barbarous;

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxii-p4"></span>**2** \[*Then*\] was Judah for his
holiness, Israel, his dominions.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxii-p5"></span>**3** The sea saw, and fled, Jordan
was turned backward.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxii-p6"></span>**4** The mountains leaped as rams,
The hills as the lambs of the flock.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxii-p7"></span>**5** What ailed thee, O sea! that
thou fleddest? *And thou*, O Jordan! *that* thou wast turned back?

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxii-p8"></span>**6** Ye mountains, *that* ye leaped
like rams; Ye hills, as the lambs of the flock?

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxii-p9"></span>**7** At the presence of the Lord,
tremble, O earth! At the presence of the God of Jacob;

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxii-p10"></span>**8** Who turned the rock into pools
of water, The flinty rock into a fountain of waters.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxiii"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxiii-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxiii-p2"></span>PSALM 115

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxiii-p3"></span>**1** Not to us, O Jehovah! not to
us, But to thy name give glory, On account of thy mercy, on account of
thy truth.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxiii-p4"></span>**2** Why should the heathen say,
“Where *is* now their God?”

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxiii-p5"></span>**3** But our God *is* in the heaven:
Whatever pleased him he hath done.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxiii-p6"></span>**4** Their idols *are* silver and
gold, The work of the hands of men.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxiii-p7"></span>**5** A mouth have they,  <span
id="fr_382"></span>[383](#fn_382) and they do not speak: Eyes have they,
and they do not see:

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxiii-p9"></span>**6** Ears have they, and they do not
hear: Noses have they, and they do not smell:

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxiii-p10"></span>**7** Hands have they, and they do
not feel: Feet have they, and they do not walk: They do not speak
through their throat.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxiii-p11"></span>**8** Like to them shall be those
who make them, And every one who trusteth in them.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxiii-p12"></span>**9** O Israel! trust thou in
Jehovah: Their help and their shield is He:

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxiii-p13"></span>**10** O house of Aaron! trust in
Jehovah: Their help and their shield is he:

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxiii-p14"></span>**11** Ye who fear Jehovah! trust in
Jehovah: Their help and their shield *is* He.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxiii-p15"></span>**12** Jehovah hath remembered us;
he will bless us; He will bless the house of Israel; He will bless the
house of Aaron.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxiii-p16"></span>**13** He will bless those who fear
Jehovah, The small together with the great.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxiii-p17"></span>**14** Jehovah will add to you, To
you and to your children.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxiii-p18"></span>**15** Blessed are ye of Jehovah,
Who made heaven and earth.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxiii-p19"></span>**16** The heavens, the heavens
*are* Jehovah’s: But the earth he hath given to the sons of men.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxiii-p20"></span>**17** The dead shall not praise
*thee*, O God! Nor any who go down into silence.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxiii-p21"></span>**18** But as for us we will bless
God, From this time, and even for evermore. Hallelujah.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxiv"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxiv-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxiv-p2"></span>PSALM 116

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxiv-p3"></span>**1** I have loved, because heard hath
Jehovah the voice of my prayer;

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxiv-p4"></span>**2** Because he hath inclined his ear
to me, When in my straits I called upon him.  <span
id="fr_383"></span>[384](#fn_383)

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxiv-p6"></span>**3** They encompassed me, the snares
of death, And the sorrows of the grave found me: Trouble and grief I
found.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxiv-p7"></span>**4** And on the name of Jehovah I
will call: “I beseech thee, O Jehovah! deliver my soul.”

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxiv-p8"></span>**5** Merciful *is* Jehovah and
righteous; And our God *is* compassionate.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxiv-p9"></span>**6** Guard doth Jehovah the simple: I
was brought low and he saved me.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxiv-p10"></span>**7** Return, O my soul! to thy rest;
For Jehovah hath dealt kindly with thee.  <span
id="fr_384"></span>[385](#fn_384)

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxiv-p12"></span>**8** Because thou hast rescued my
soul from death My eye from tears, My foot from falling.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxiv-p13"></span>**9** I will walk before Jehovah in
the land of the living.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxiv-p14"></span>**10** I have believed, for I will
speak: “I am afflicted greatly.”

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxiv-p15"></span>**11** I said in my fear, “Every man
is a liar.”

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxiv-p16"></span>**12** What shall I render to
Jehovah? All his benefits *are* upon me.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxiv-p17"></span>**13** The cup of salvation I will
take, And upon the name of Jehovah I will call.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxiv-p18"></span>**14** My vows to, Jehovah I will
perform Now in the presence of all his people.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxiv-p19"></span>**15** Precious in the eyes of
Jehovah is the death of his meek ones.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxiv-p20"></span>**16** Come! O Jehovah! for I, *am*
thy servant; I *am* thy servant, the son of thy handmaid; Thou hast
broken my fetters.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxiv-p21"></span>**17** To thee will I sacrifice the
sacrifice of praise, And upon the name of Jehovah will I call.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxiv-p22"></span>**18** My vows to Jehovah will I
perform Now in the presence of all his people,

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxiv-p23"></span>**19** In the courts of the house of
Jehovah In the midst of thee, O Jerusalem! Hallelujah.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxv"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxv-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxv-p2"></span>PSALM 117

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxv-p3"></span>**1** Praise ye Jehovah, all ye
nations! Celebrate him all ye peoples!

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxv-p4"></span>**2** For great towards us is his
mercy, And the truth of Jehovah *continueth* for ever. Hallelujah.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxvi"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxvi-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxvi-p2"></span>PSALM 118

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxvi-p3"></span>**1** Celebrate ye Jehovah! for *he
is* good: For to everlasting *endureth* his mercy.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxvi-p4"></span>**2** Let now Israel say: “For  <span
id="fr_385"></span>[386](#fn_385) to everlasting *endureth* his mercy.”

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxvi-p6"></span>**3** Let now the house of Aaron say:
“For to everlasting *endureth* his mercy.”

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxvi-p7"></span>**4** Let now those who fear Jehovah
say: “For to everlasting *endureth* his mercy.”

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxvi-p8"></span>**5** In my distress I called upon
God; God answered me *by setting me* at large.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxvi-p9"></span>**6** Jehovah *is* with me: I will not
fear what man can do to me.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxvi-p10"></span>**7** Jehovah *is* with me among
those who help me, And I shall see *my desire* upon my adversaries.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxvi-p11"></span>**8** It is better to hope in Jehovah
Than to place confidence in man:

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxvi-p12"></span>**9** It is better to hope in Jehovah
Than to place confidence in princes.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxvi-p13"></span>**10** All the nations encompassed
me: *But* in the name of Jehovah I will surely cut them off.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxvi-p14"></span>**11** They encompassed me, yea they
encompassed me, *But* in the name of Jehovah I will surely cut them
off’.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxvi-p15"></span>**12** They encompassed me as bees:
They were extinguished as a fire of thorns: In the name of Jehovah I
will surely cut them off.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxvi-p16"></span>**13** Thou hast thrust and  <span
id="fr_386"></span>[387](#fn_386) thrust at me, that I might fall: But
Jehovah helped me.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxvi-p18"></span>**14** My strength and *my* song is
God, And he hath become to me salvation.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxvi-p19"></span>**15** The voice of exultation and
salvation is in the tabernacles of the righteous: The right hand of
Jehovah hath done valiantly.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxvi-p20"></span>**16** The right hand of Jehovah is
exalted, The right hand of Jehovah hath done valiantly.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxvi-p21"></span>**17** I shall not die, yea, I shall
live, And recount the works of God.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxvi-p22"></span>**18** Chastised me sorely hath
 <span id="fr_387"></span>[388](#fn_387) God; But he hath not delivered
me up unto death.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxvi-p24"></span>**19** Open to me the gates of
righteousness; *And* having entered into them, I will celebrate God.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxvi-p25"></span>**20** This is the gate of Jehovah,
The just ones shall enter into it.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxvi-p26"></span>**21** I will celebrate thee because
thou hast heard me, And hast been my salvation.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxvi-p27"></span>**22** The stone which the builders
rejected Is become the head \[*stone*\] of the corner.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxvi-p28"></span>**23** By Jehovah hath this been
done: It is marvelous in our eyes.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxvi-p29"></span>**24** This *is* the day which
Jehovah hath made; Let us exult and rejoice in it.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxvi-p30"></span>**25** I beseech thee, O Jehovah!
save me; I beseech thee, I beseech thee, O Jehovah! give prosperity I
beseech thee.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxvi-p31"></span>**26** Blessed is he who cometh in
the name of Jehovah: We bless you from the house of Jehovah.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxvi-p32"></span>**27** God *is* Jehovah, and he hath
given light to us: Bind ye the lamb with cords, even to the horns of the
altar.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxvi-p33"></span>**28** My God art thou, and I will
celebrate thee: My God, I will exalt thee.

<span id="xxxv.iv.xxvi-p34"></span>**29** Celebrate ye Jehovah; for *he*
*is* good: For to everlasting *is* his mercy.

<span id="xxxv.v"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v-p1"></span>PSALMS 119—150

<span id="xxxv.v.i"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p2"></span>PSALM 119

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p3"></span><span id="xxxv.v.i-p3.1"></span>א
\[**Aleph**.\]

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p4"></span>**1** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p4.1"></span>א
Blessed *are* those who are upright in *their* way, Walking in the law
of Jehovah.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p5"></span>**2** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p5.1"></span>א
Blessed *are* those who keep his testimonies, *Who* with *their* whole
heart seek him.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p6"></span>**3** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p6.1"></span>א,
Surely they do not work iniquity, *Who* in his ways do walk.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p7"></span>**4** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p7.1"></span>א
Thou hast commanded That thy statutes be kept carefully.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p8"></span>**5** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p8.1"></span>א O
that my ways may be directed To the keeping of thy statutes!

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p9"></span>**6** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p9.1"></span>א
Then shall I not be ashamed, When I shall have been attentive to all thy
commandments.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p10"></span>**7** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p10.1"></span>א
I will celebrate thee with uprightness of heart, When I shall have
learned the judgments of thy righteousness.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p11"></span>**8** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p11.1"></span>א,
Thy statutes I will keep: Do not thou forsake me very far.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p12"></span><span id="xxxv.v.i-p12.1"></span>ב
\[**Beth**.\]

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p13"></span>**9** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p13.1"></span>ב
By what \[*means*\] shall a young man cleanse his way? By taking heed
according to thy word.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p14"></span>**10** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p14.1"></span>ב
With my whole heart have I sought thee; Let me not go astray from thy
commandments.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p15"></span>**11** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p15.1"></span>ב
In my heart I have hidden thy word, That I might not sin against thee.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p16"></span>**12** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p16.1"></span>ב
Blessed *art* thou, O Jehovah! Teach me thy statutes.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p17"></span>**13** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p17.1"></span>ב
With my lips have I declared All the judgments of thy mouth.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p18"></span>**14** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p18.1"></span>ב
In the way of thy testimonies I have taken delight, As much as in all
riches.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p19"></span>**15** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p19.1"></span>ב
Upon thy statutes will I meditate, And I will consider thy paths.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p20"></span>**16** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p20.1"></span>ב
In thy commandments will I delight myself; I will not forget thy words.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p21"></span><span id="xxxv.v.i-p21.1"></span>ג
\[**Gimel**.\]

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p22"></span>**17** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p22.1"></span>ג
Do good to thy servant, And I shall live and keep thy word.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p23"></span>**18** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p23.1"></span>ג
Open mine eyes, And I shall behold the wonders of thy law.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p24"></span>**19** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p24.1"></span>ג
I am a stranger on the earth: Hide not from me thy commandments.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p25"></span>**20** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p25.1"></span>ג
Broken is my soul with the desire *it hath* To thy judgments at all
times.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p26"></span>**21** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p26.1"></span>ג
Thou hast destroyed the proud ones; Cursed are those who decline from
thy commandments.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p27"></span>**22** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p27.1"></span>ג
Remove from me reproach and contempt; For thy testimonies I have kept.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p28"></span>**23** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p28.1"></span>ג
Princes also have sat, against me they have spoken: Thy servant
meditated upon thy statutes.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p29"></span>**24** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p29.1"></span>ג
Also thy testimonies *are* my delights, The men of my counsel.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p30"></span><span id="xxxv.v.i-p30.1"></span>ד
\[**Daleth**.\]

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p31"></span>**25** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p31.1"></span>ד
Cleave to the dust doth my soul: Quicken me according to thy word.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p32"></span>**26** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p32.1"></span>ד
I have declared my ways, and thou hast answered me: Teach me thy
statutes.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p33"></span>**27** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p33.1"></span>ד
The way of thy commandments make me to understand, And I will meditate
upon thy wonders.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p34"></span>**28** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p34.1"></span>ד
Drop away doth my soul for grief: Raise me up according to thy word.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p35"></span>**29** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p35.1"></span>ד
The way of falsehood remove from me, And thy law grant me graciously.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p36"></span>**30** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p36.1"></span>ד
The way of truth I have chosen; Thy judgments I have set before me.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p37"></span>**31** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p37.1"></span>ד
I have cleaved to thy testimonies, O Jehovah Let me not be put to shame.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p38"></span>**32** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p38.1"></span>ד
The way of thy statutes I will run, When thou shalt have enlarged my
heart.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p39"></span><span id="xxxv.v.i-p39.1"></span>ה
\[**He**.\]

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p40"></span>**33** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p40.1"></span>ה
Teach me, O Jehovah! the way of thy statutes, And I will keep it unto
the end.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p41"></span>**34** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p41.1"></span>ה
Make me to understand, and I will observe thy law, And keep it with my
whole heart.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p42"></span>**35** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p42.1"></span>ה
Direct me in the way of thy statutes; For in it is my delight.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p43"></span>**36** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p43.1"></span>ה
Incline my heart to thy testimonies, And not to covetousness.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p44"></span>**37** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p44.1"></span>ה
Turn away my eyes from seeing vanity; In thy way quicken me.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p45"></span>**38** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p45.1"></span>ה
Confirm to thy servant thy word, Who to thy fear *is devoted*

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p46"></span>**39** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p46.1"></span>ה
Remove my reproach which I have dreaded, For thy judgments are good.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p47"></span>**40** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p47.1"></span>ה
Behold! I have longed after thy commandments: In thy righteousness
quicken me.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p48"></span><span id="xxxv.v.i-p48.1"></span>ו
\[**Vau**.\]

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p49"></span>**41** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p49.1"></span>ו
And let come to me thy mercies, O Jehovah! Thy salvation according to
thy word.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p50"></span>**42** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p50.1"></span>ו
And I will answer a word to him who reproacheth me; For I have trusted
in thy word.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p51"></span>**43** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p51.1"></span>ו
And take not from my mouth the word of truth utterly: Because for thy
judgments I wait.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p52"></span>**44** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p52.1"></span>ו
And I will keep thy law continually, For ever and ever.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p53"></span>**45** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p53.1"></span>ו
And I will walk at large; For thy statutes I have sought.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p54"></span>**46** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p54.1"></span>ו
And I will speak of thy testimonies before kings, And will not be
ashamed.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p55"></span>**47** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p55.1"></span>ו
And I will delight myself in thy commandments Which I have loved.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p56"></span>**48** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p56.1"></span>ו
And I will lift up my hands to thy commandments Which I have loved; And
I will meditate upon thy statutes.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p57"></span><span id="xxxv.v.i-p57.1"></span>ז
\[**Zain**.\]

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p58"></span>**49** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p58.1"></span>ז
Remember thy word to thy servant, Upon which thou hast caused me to
hope.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p59"></span>**50** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p59.1"></span>ז
This is my consolation in my affliction; For thy word revives me.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p60"></span>**51** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p60.1"></span>ז
The proud ones have derided me exceedingly: From thy law I have not
declined.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p61"></span>**52** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p61.1"></span>ז
I remembered thy judgments of old, O Jehovah! And comforted myself.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p62"></span>**53** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p62.1"></span>ז
Terror hath seized upon me, Because of the ungodly who forsake thy law.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p63"></span>**54** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p63.1"></span>ז
Thy statutes have been songs to me In the house of my pilgrimage.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p64"></span>**55** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p64.1"></span>ז
I remembered in the night thy name, O Jehovah! And I will keep thy law.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p65"></span>**56** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p65.1"></span>ז
This is done to me, Because thy statutes I have observed.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p66"></span><span id="xxxv.v.i-p66.1"></span>ח
\[**Cheth**.\]

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p67"></span>**57** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p67.1"></span>ח
*Thou art* my portion, O Jehovah! I have said that I will keep thy
words.  <span id="fr_388"></span>[389](#fn_388)

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p69"></span>**58** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p69.1"></span>ח
I have sought thy face with my whole heart; Have mercy upon me according
to thy word.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p70"></span>**59** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p70.1"></span>ח
I thought upon my ways, And turned my feet to thy testimonies.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p71"></span>**60** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p71.1"></span>ח
I made haste and delayed not To keep thy commandments.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p72"></span>**61** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p72.1"></span>ח
The cords of the ungodly have caught hold of me; Thy law I have not
forgotten.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p73"></span>**62** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p73.1"></span>ח
At midnight I will rise to praise thee, Because of the judgments of thy
righteousness.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p74"></span>**63** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p74.1"></span>ח
A companion am I to all who fear thee, And who keep thy statutes.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p75"></span>**64** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p75.1"></span>ח
Of thy mercy, O Jehovah! the earth is full: Thy statutes teach thou me.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p76"></span><span id="xxxv.v.i-p76.1"></span>ת
\[**Teth**.\]

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p77"></span>**65** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p77.1"></span>ת
Kindly hast thou dealt with thy servant, O Jehovah! According to thy
word.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p78"></span>**66** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p78.1"></span>ת
Goodness of taste and knowledge teach me; For thy commandments I have
believed.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p79"></span>**67** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p79.1"></span>ת
Before I was brought low I went astray; But now thy word I keep.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p80"></span>**68** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p80.1"></span>ת
Good *art* thou, and beneficent: Teach me thy statutes.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p81"></span>**69** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p81.1"></span>ת
Weaved a lie  <span id="fr_389"></span>[390](#fn_389) against me have
the proud ones; *But as for me* I with my whole heart will keep
statutes.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p83"></span>**70** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p83.1"></span>ת
Fat as grease is their heart; *But as for me* I in thy law do delight.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p84"></span>**71** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p84.1"></span>ת
*It hath been* good for me that I have been afflicted, That I might
learn thy statutes.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p85"></span>**72** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p85.1"></span>ת
Better to me is the law of thy mouth Than thousands of gold and silver.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p86"></span><span id="xxxv.v.i-p86.1"></span>י
\[**Yod**.\]

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p87"></span>**73** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p87.1"></span>י
Thy hands have made and formed me; Make me to understand, and I shall
learn thy commandments.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p88"></span>**74** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p88.1"></span>י
Those who fear thee shall see me and rejoice; Because for thy word I
have waited.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p89"></span>**75** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p89.1"></span>י
I have known, O Jehovah! that righteousness are thy judgments; And in
truth thou hast humbled me.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p90"></span>**76** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p90.1"></span>י
To thy word to thy servant.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p91"></span>**77** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p91.1"></span>י
Let come to me thy compassions, and I shall live; For thy law is my
delight.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p92"></span>**78** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p92.1"></span>י
Ashamed let be the proud, for they have falsely wronged me: As for me I
will meditate upon thy precepts.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p93"></span>**79** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p93.1"></span>י
Let those turn unto me who fear thee, And have known thy testimonies.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p94"></span>**80** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p94.1"></span>י
Let my heart be sound in thy statutes, That I may not be put to shame.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p95"></span><span id="xxxv.v.i-p95.1"></span>כ
\[**Caph**.\]

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p96"></span>**81** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p96.1"></span>כ
Fainted for thy salvation hath my soul: For thy word I wait.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p97"></span>**82** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p97.1"></span>כ
Failed have my eyes \[*in looking*\] for thy word, While I say, “When
wilt thou comfort me?”

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p98"></span>**83** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p98.1"></span>כ
For I have been as a bottle in the smoke; *And yet* thy statutes I have
not forgotten.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p99"></span>**84** <span id="xxxv.v.i-p99.1"></span>כ
How many are the days of thy servant? When wilt thou execute judgment on
my persecutors?

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p100"></span>**85** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p100.1"></span>כ The proud have digged pits for me, Which
is not according to thy law.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p101"></span>**86** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p101.1"></span>כ All thy commandments are truth:
Deceitfully do they persecute me; *therefore* help thou me.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p102"></span>**87** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p102.1"></span>כ Almost have they consumed me upon the
earth; Yet I have not forsaken thy statutes.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p103"></span>**88** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p103.1"></span>כ According to thy goodness quicken me; And
I will keep the testimony of thy mouth.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p104"></span><span id="xxxv.v.i-p104.1"></span>ל
\[**Lamed**.\]

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p105"></span>**89** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p105.1"></span>ל For ever, O Jehovah! Thy word endureth in
the heavens.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p106"></span>**90** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p106.1"></span>ל From generation to generation *is* thy
truth: Thou hast established the earth, and it abideth.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p107"></span>**91** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p107.1"></span>ל By thy judgments they continue to this
day; For all are thy servants.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p108"></span>**92** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p108.1"></span>ל Unless thy law *had been* my delight, Then
should I have perished in my affliction.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p109"></span>**93** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p109.1"></span>ל Never will I forget thy statutes, For in
them thou hast quickened me.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p110"></span>**94** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p110.1"></span>ל Thine I am; O save me! For thy statutes I
have sought.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p111"></span>**95** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p111.1"></span>ל For me wait do the ungodly to destroy me:
*But* I consider thy testimonies.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p112"></span>**96** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p112.1"></span>ל In all perfection I have seen an end:
Broad is thy commandment exceedingly.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p113"></span><span id="xxxv.v.i-p113.1"></span>מ
\[**Mem**.\]

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p114"></span>**97** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p114.1"></span>מ O how have I loved thy law! All the day it
is my meditation.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p115"></span>**98** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p115.1"></span>מ Than my adversaries thou hast made me
wiser by thy commandments; Because for ever they are with me.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p116"></span>**99** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p116.1"></span>מ Than all my teachers thou hast made me
wiser; Because thy testimonies are my meditation.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p117"></span>**100** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p117.1"></span>מ Than the aged I have more understanding;
Because thy statutes I have observed.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p118"></span>**101** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p118.1"></span>מ From every evil path I have restrained my
feet, That I may keep thy word.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p119"></span>**102** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p119.1"></span>מ From thy judgments I have not declined;
For thou thyself hast taught me.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p120"></span>**103** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p120.1"></span>מ How sweet to my palate have been thy
words! More \[*sweet*\] than honey to my mouth!

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p121"></span>**104** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p121.1"></span>מ By thy statutes I have gotten
understanding; Therefore I have hated every path of falsehood.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p122"></span><span id="xxxv.v.i-p122.1"></span>נ
\[**Nun**.\]

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p123"></span>**105** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p123.1"></span>נ A lamp to my feet is thy word, And a light
to my path.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p124"></span>**106** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p124.1"></span>נ I have sworn and will make sure, To
observe the judgments of thy righteousness.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p125"></span>**107** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p125.1"></span>נ I am afflicted exceedingly, O Jehovah!
Quicken me according to thy word.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p126"></span>**108** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p126.1"></span>נ I Let the freewill *offerings* of my
mouth, I pray thee, be pleasing to thee, O Jehovah! And thy judgments
teach me.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p127"></span>**109** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p127.1"></span>נ My soul *is* in my hand continually; And
thy law I have not forgotten.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p128"></span>**110** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p128.1"></span>נ Laid have the ungodly a snare for me: Yet
from thy statutes I have not erred.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p129"></span>**111** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p129.1"></span>נ I have as \[*my*\] inheritance thy
testimonies for ever; For the joy of my heart are they.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p130"></span>**112** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p130.1"></span>נ I have inclined my heart to perform thy
statutes For ever, and even to the end.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p131"></span><span id="xxxv.v.i-p131.1"></span>ס
\[**Samech**.\]

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p132"></span>**113** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p132.1"></span>ס *Crooked* thoughts I have hated; But thy
law I have loved.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p133"></span>**114** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p133.1"></span>ס My hiding-place and my shield art thou: In
thy word I have trusted.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p134"></span>**115** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p134.1"></span>ס Depart from me, ye wicked men! And I will
keep the commandments of my God.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p135"></span>**116** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p135.1"></span>ס Sustain me by thy word, and I shall live:
And make me not ashamed of my expectation.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p136"></span>**117** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p136.1"></span>ס Establish me, and I shall be safe, And I
will consider thy statutes continually.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p137"></span>**118** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p137.1"></span>ס Thou hast trodden down all who go astray
from thy statutes; For falsehood is their deceit.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p138"></span>**119** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p138.1"></span>ס *As* dross thou hast made to cease all the
ungodly of the earth; Therefore I have loved thy testimonies.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p139"></span>**120** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p139.1"></span>ס Tremble  <span
id="fr_390"></span>[391](#fn_390) for fear of thee did my flesh, And of
thy judgments I was afraid.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p141"></span><span id="xxxv.v.i-p141.1"></span>ע
\[**Ain**.\]

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p142"></span>**121** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p142.1"></span>ע I have done judgment and righteousness:
Give me not up to my oppressors.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p143"></span>**122** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p143.1"></span>ע Become surety for thy servant for good,
That the proud may not oppress me.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p144"></span>**123** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p144.1"></span>ע My eyes have failed for thy salvation, And
for the word of thy righteousness.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p145"></span>**124** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p145.1"></span>ע Deal with thy servant according to thy
goodness, And thy statutes teach thou me.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p146"></span>**125** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p146.1"></span>ע Thy servant am I, give me understanding,
That I may learn thy testimonies.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p147"></span>**126** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p147.1"></span>ע *It is* time \[*for thee*\] to work, O
Jehovah! *For they* have destroyed thy law.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p148"></span>**127** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p148.1"></span>ע Therefore I have loved thy statutes Mere
than gold and fine gold.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p149"></span>**128** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p149.1"></span>ע Therefore all *thy* commandments I have
esteemed *to be* altogether right: Every way of falsehood I have hated:

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p150"></span><span id="xxxv.v.i-p150.1"></span>פ
\[**Phe**.\]

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p151"></span>**129** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p151.1"></span>פ Marvelous things *are* thy testimonies;
Therefore observed them hath my soul.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p152"></span>**130** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p152.1"></span>פ The entrance of thy words is light, Giving
understanding to the little ones.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p153"></span>**131** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p153.1"></span>פ My mouth I opened and panted, Because thy
commandments I loved.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p154"></span>**132** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p154.1"></span>פ Look upon me and have pity upon me,
According to *thy* judgment towards those who love thy name.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p155"></span>**133** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p155.1"></span>פ My steps direct thou according to thy
word, And let not any iniquity have dominion in me.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p156"></span>**134** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p156.1"></span>פ Redeem me from the oppression of men, And
I will keep thy precepts.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p157"></span>**135** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p157.1"></span>פ Thy face cause thou to shine upon thy
servant, And teach me thy statutes.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p158"></span>**136** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p158.1"></span>פ Rivers of waters run from my eyes, Because
they have not kept thy law.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p159"></span><span id="xxxv.v.i-p159.1"></span>ץ
\[**Tsadde**.\]

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p160"></span>**137** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p160.1"></span>ץ Righteous art thou, O Jehovah! And right
*are* thy judgments.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p161"></span>**138** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p161.1"></span>ץ Thou hast commanded righteousness *in* thy
testimonies, And truth exceedingly.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p162"></span>**139** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p162.1"></span>ץ Consumed me hath my zeal, Because
forgotten thy words have my adversaries.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p163"></span>**140** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p163.1"></span>ץ Refined *is* thy word exceedingly: And thy
servant hath loved it.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p164"></span>**141** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p164.1"></span>ץ Small *am* I, and despised; \[*Yet*\] thy
precepts I have not forgotten.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p165"></span>**142** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p165.1"></span>ץ Thy righteousness *is* righteousness for
ever, And thy law is truth.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p166"></span>**143** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p166.1"></span>ץ Trouble and anguish have come upon me;
*But* thy commandments *have been* my delights.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p167"></span>**144** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p167.1"></span>ץ The righteousness of thy testimonies
*endureth* for ever; Make me to understand, and I shall live.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p168"></span><span id="xxxv.v.i-p168.1"></span>ק
\[**Koph**.\]

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p169"></span>**145** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p169.1"></span>ק I have cried with my whole heart; Answer
me, O Jehovah! *And* thy statutes I will keep.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p170"></span>**146** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p170.1"></span>ק I have called upon thee, save me, And I
will keep thy testimonies.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p171"></span>**147** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p171.1"></span>ק I have prevented the dawn of the morning,
 <span id="fr_391"></span>[392](#fn_391) and have cried: To thy word I
have looked up.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p173"></span>**148** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p173.1"></span>ק Prevented have my eyes the watches *of the
night*, To meditate upon thy word.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p174"></span>**149** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p174.1"></span>ק My voice hear thou, according to thy
mercy, O Jehovah According to thy judgment quicken me.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p175"></span>**150** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p175.1"></span>ק Drawn near have the pursuers of malice;
From thy law they have departed.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p176"></span>**151** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p176.1"></span>ק Near art thou, O Jehovah! And all thy
commandments *are* truth.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p177"></span>**152** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p177.1"></span>ק From the beginning I have known from thy
testimonies, That for ever thou hast founded them.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p178"></span><span id="xxxv.v.i-p178.1"></span>ר
\[**Resh**.\]

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p179"></span>**153** <span
