id="xxxv.v.i-p179.1"></span>ר Behold my affliction, and rescue me; For
thy law I have not forgotten.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p180"></span>**154** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p180.1"></span>ר Debate my cause, and redeem me; According
to thy word quicken me.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p181"></span>**155** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p181.1"></span>ר Far from the ungodly is safety; Because
thy statutes they have not sought.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p182"></span>**156** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p182.1"></span>ר Thy compassions *are* great, O Jehovah!
According to thy judgments quicken me.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p183"></span>**157** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p183.1"></span>ר Many *are* my persecutors and my
oppressors: From thy testimonies I have not declined.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p184"></span>**158** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p184.1"></span>ר I saw the perfidious, and chid them;
Because thy word they have not kept.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p185"></span>**159** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p185.1"></span>ר Behold how thy commandments I have loved:
According to thy clemency quicken me.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p186"></span>**160** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p186.1"></span>ר The beginning of thy word *is* truth; And
to everlasting *is* all the judgment of thy righteousness.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p187"></span><span id="xxxv.v.i-p187.1"></span>ש
\[**Shin**.\]

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p188"></span>**161** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p188.1"></span>ש Princes have persecuted me without a cause
Yet at thy word afraid hath been my heart.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p189"></span>**162** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p189.1"></span>ש Joyful am I over thy word, As he who hath
found much spoil.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p190"></span>**163** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p190.1"></span>ש Deceit I *have* hated and abhorred; Thy
law I *have* loved.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p191"></span>**164** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p191.1"></span>ש Seven times a day have I praised thee,
Because of the judgments of thy righteousness.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p192"></span>**165** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p192.1"></span>ש Much peace have those who love thy law,
And they have no stumbling-block.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p193"></span>**166** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p193.1"></span>ש I have waited for thy salvation, O
Jehovah! And thy commandments I have done.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p194"></span>**167** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p194.1"></span>ש Kept hath my soul thy testimonies, And I
have loved them exceedingly.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p195"></span>**168** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p195.1"></span>ש I have kept thy commandments and thy
testimonies; For all my ways *are* before thee.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p196"></span><span id="xxxv.v.i-p196.1"></span>ת
\[**Thau**.\]

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p197"></span>**169** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p197.1"></span>ת Come let my cry into thy presence, O
Jehovah! According to thy word give me understanding.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p198"></span>**170** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p198.1"></span>ת Come let my prayer into thy presence:
According to thy word deliver me.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p199"></span>**171** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p199.1"></span>ת Speak shall my lips praise, When thou
shalt have taught me thy statutes.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p200"></span>**172** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p200.1"></span>ת Speak shall my tongue of thy word; For all
thy precepts are righteousness.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p201"></span>**173** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p201.1"></span>ת Let thy hand be to succor me; For thy
commandments I have chosen.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p202"></span>**174** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p202.1"></span>ת I have longed for thy salvation, O
Jehovah! And thy law *hath been* my delights.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p203"></span>**175** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p203.1"></span>ת Live let my soul, and let it praise thee;
And let thy judgments succor me.

<span id="xxxv.v.i-p204"></span>**176** <span
id="xxxv.v.i-p204.1"></span>ת I have wandered like a lost sheep; Seek
thy servant, for thy statutes I have not forgotten.

<span id="xxxv.v.ii"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.ii-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.ii-p2"></span>PSALM 120

<span id="xxxv.v.ii-p3"></span>A Song of Degrees

<span id="xxxv.v.ii-p4"></span>**1** To Jehovah in my distress I cried,
And he answered me.

<span id="xxxv.v.ii-p5"></span>**2** O Jehovah! deliver my soul from the
lip of falsehood, From the tongue of deceit.

<span id="xxxv.v.ii-p6"></span>**3** What give thee, and what avail thee
Shall the tongue of deceit?

<span id="xxxv.v.ii-p7"></span>**4** The arrows of a strong *man*
sharpened, With coals of junipers.

<span id="xxxv.v.ii-p8"></span>**5** Alas for me! that I have been a
sojourner in Meseeh, *And* have dwelt among the tents of Kedar.

<span id="xxxv.v.ii-p9"></span>**6** Long dwelt hath my soul with him
who hateth peace.

<span id="xxxv.v.ii-p10"></span>**7** I \[*am for*\] peace; But when I
speak, they \[*are*\] for war.

<span id="xxxv.v.iii"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.iii-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.iii-p2"></span>PSALM 121

<span id="xxxv.v.iii-p3"></span>A Song of Degrees

<span id="xxxv.v.iii-p4"></span>**1** I will lift up my eyes to the
mountains, Whence come shall my help.

<span id="xxxv.v.iii-p5"></span>**2** My help *cometh* from Jehovah, Who
made heaven and earth.

<span id="xxxv.v.iii-p6"></span>**3** He will not suffer thy foot to
stumble; Slumber not shall thy guardian.

<span id="xxxv.v.iii-p7"></span>**4** Behold! slumber not nor sleep
Shall the guardian of Israel.

<span id="xxxv.v.iii-p8"></span>**5** Jehovah *is* thy guardian; Jehovah
*is* *thy* defense on thy right hand.

<span id="xxxv.v.iii-p9"></span>**6** By day the sun shall not smite
thee, Nor the moon by night.

<span id="xxxv.v.iii-p10"></span>**7** Jehovah shall keep thee from all
evil; He shall keep thy soul.

<span id="xxxv.v.iii-p11"></span>**8** Jehovah shall keep thy going out
and thy coming in, From this time, and for ever.

<span id="xxxv.v.iv"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.iv-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.iv-p2"></span>PSALM 122

<span id="xxxv.v.iv-p3"></span>A Song of Degrees Of David

<span id="xxxv.v.iv-p4"></span>**1** I was glad when they said to me,
“Into the house of Jehovah we will go.

<span id="xxxv.v.iv-p5"></span>**2** “Our feet shall be standing in thy
gates, O Jerusalem!”

<span id="xxxv.v.iv-p6"></span>**3** Jerusalem built as a city, compact
in itself together.

<span id="xxxv.v.iv-p7"></span>**4** Thither ascended the tribes, the
tribes of God, For a testimony to Israel, To celebrate the name of
Jehovah.

<span id="xxxv.v.iv-p8"></span>**5** For there have sat  <span
id="fr_392"></span>[393](#fn_392) thrones for judgment, The thrones of
the house of David.

<span id="xxxv.v.iv-p10"></span>**6** Pray ye for the peace of
Jerusalem: Prosper may those who love thee!

<span id="xxxv.v.iv-p11"></span>**7** Peace be within thy bulwark!
Prosperity within thy towers!

<span id="xxxv.v.iv-p12"></span>**8** For the sake of my brethren and my
neighbors, I will say now, “Peace \[*be*\] within thee!“

<span id="xxxv.v.iv-p13"></span>**9** For the sake of the house of
Jehovah our God, I will seek good for thee.

<span id="xxxv.v.v"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.v-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.v-p2"></span>PSALM 123

<span id="xxxv.v.v-p3"></span>A Song of Degrees

<span id="xxxv.v.v-p4"></span>**1** To thee will I lift up mine eyes,
\[*O thou*\] who dwellest in the heavens!

<span id="xxxv.v.v-p5"></span>**2** Behold! as the eyes of servants look
to the hand of their masters; As the eyes of a handmaid *look* to the
hand of her mistress, So our eyes \[*look*\] to Jehovah our God, Until
he have mercy upon us.

<span id="xxxv.v.v-p6"></span>**3** Have mercy upon us, O Jehovah! have
mercy upon us; For we are exceedingly filled with reproach.

<span id="xxxv.v.v-p7"></span>**4** Exceedingly filled in itself is our
soul With the mockery of the rich, With the contempt of the proud.

<span id="xxxv.v.vi"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.vi-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.vi-p2"></span>PSALM 124

<span id="xxxv.v.vi-p3"></span>A Song of Degrees. Of David

<span id="xxxv.v.vi-p4"></span>**1** “But for Jehovah who was on our
side” — Say now may Israel:

<span id="xxxv.v.vi-p5"></span>**2** “But for Jehovah who was on our
side, “When men rose up against us;

<span id="xxxv.v.vi-p6"></span>**3** “Then alive had they swallowed us
up, “When kindled was their wrath against us;

<span id="xxxv.v.vi-p7"></span>**4** “Then the waters had overwhelmed
us, “The torrent had gone over our soul:

<span id="xxxv.v.vi-p8"></span>**5** “Then had gone over our soul the
proud waters.”

<span id="xxxv.v.vi-p9"></span>**6** Blessed *be* Jehovah, Who gave us
not for a prey to their teeth.

<span id="xxxv.v.vi-p10"></span>**7** Our soul as a bird, hath been
rescued  <span id="fr_393"></span>[394](#fn_393) from the snare of the
fowlers; The snare hath been broken, and we have been delivered.

<span id="xxxv.v.vi-p12"></span>**8** Our help *is* in the name of
Jehovah, Who made heaven and earth.

<span id="xxxv.v.vii"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.vii-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.vii-p2"></span>PSALM 125

<span id="xxxv.v.vii-p3"></span>A Song of Degrees

<span id="xxxv.v.vii-p4"></span>**1** They who confide in Jehovah *are
as* mount Zion, *Which* shall not be removed, *but* shall abide for
ever.

<span id="xxxv.v.vii-p5"></span>**2** As the mountains *are* about
Jerusalem, So Jehovah *is* round about his people, From henceforth, and
for ever.

<span id="xxxv.v.vii-p6"></span>**3** For rest not shall the scepter of
the ungodly ones upon the lot of the just, Lest the just ones should put
forth to iniquity their hands.

<span id="xxxv.v.vii-p7"></span>**4** Do good, O Jehovah! to the good,
And to *those who* are upright in their hearts.

<span id="xxxv.v.vii-p8"></span>**5** But those who turn aside into
their crooked paths, Jehovah shall make them walk with the workers of
iniquity: *But there shall be* peace upon Israel.

<span id="xxxv.v.viii"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.viii-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.viii-p2"></span>PSALM 126

<span id="xxxv.v.viii-p3"></span>A Song of Degrees

<span id="xxxv.v.viii-p4"></span>**1** When bring back did Jehovah the
captivity of Zion, We were like those that dream.

<span id="xxxv.v.viii-p5"></span>**2** Now filled with laughter *shall*
be our mouth, And our tongue with exultation: Now shall they say among
the heathen, “Great things Jehovah hath done for them.”

<span id="xxxv.v.viii-p6"></span>**3** Great things Jehovah hath done
for us, *Whereof* we have been made glad.

<span id="xxxv.v.viii-p7"></span>**4** Bring back, O Jehovah! our
captivity, As rivers in the South.

<span id="xxxv.v.viii-p8"></span>**5** They who sow in tears In
exultation shall reap.

<span id="xxxv.v.viii-p9"></span>**6** Going forth, he shall go and
weep, Carrying the price of the seed: Returning he shall return with
exultation, Bearing his sheaves.

<span id="xxxv.v.ix"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.ix-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.ix-p2"></span>PSALM 127

<span id="xxxv.v.ix-p3"></span>A Song of Degrees. Of Solomon

<span id="xxxv.v.ix-p4"></span>**1** Except Jehovah build the house, In
vain they labor that build it; Except Jehovah keep the city, In vain
watcheth the watchman.

<span id="xxxv.v.ix-p5"></span>**2** Vain *is it* for you early to
hasten to rise, To go late to rest, To eat the bread of sorrows: *For*
thus will he give to his beloved one sleep.

<span id="xxxv.v.ix-p6"></span>**3** Lo! the heritage of Jehovah are
children: The reward *which he bestows* is the fruit of the womb.

<span id="xxxv.v.ix-p7"></span>**4** As arrows in the hand of a strong
man, So *are* the sons of youth.

<span id="xxxv.v.ix-p8"></span>**5** Blessed is the man who shall have
filled his quiver with them; *For* they shall not be ashamed when they
speak with their enemies in the gate.

<span id="xxxv.v.x"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.x-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.x-p2"></span>PSALM 128

<span id="xxxv.v.x-p3"></span>A Song of Degrees

<span id="xxxv.v.x-p4"></span>**1** Blessed *is* the man who feareth
Jehovah, Who walketh in his ways.

<span id="xxxv.v.x-p5"></span>**2** The labor of thy hands when thou
shalt eat thou shalt be blessed, And it *shall be* well with thee.

<span id="xxxv.v.x-p6"></span>**3** Thy wife *shall be* as a vine
fruitful on the sides of thy house: Thy children as plants of olives
around thy table.

<span id="xxxv.v.x-p7"></span>**4** Lo! surely, thus blessed shall be
the man who feareth Jehovah.

<span id="xxxv.v.x-p8"></span>**5** Bless thee shall Jehovah from Zion;
And thou shalt see the good of Jerusalem all the days of thy life.

<span id="xxxv.v.x-p9"></span>**6** And thou shalt see thy children’s
children, *And* peace upon Israel.

<span id="xxxv.v.xi"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.xi-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.xi-p2"></span>PSALM 129

<span id="xxxv.v.xi-p3"></span>A Song of Degrees

<span id="xxxv.v.xi-p4"></span>**1** “Often have they afflicted me from
my youths” Say now let Israel:

<span id="xxxv.v.xi-p5"></span>**2** “Often have they afflicted me from
my youth; “Yet they have not prevailed against me.

<span id="xxxv.v.xi-p6"></span>**3** “Upon my back ploughed have the
ploughers; “They have made long their furrows.

<span id="xxxv.v.xi-p7"></span>**4** “Jehovah, who is righteous, hath
cut asunder the cords of the wicked.”

<span id="xxxv.v.xi-p8"></span>**5** Confounded and turned backward
shall be all who hate Zion.

<span id="xxxv.v.xi-p9"></span>**6** They shall be as the grass of the
housetops, Which before it cometh forth is withered:

<span id="xxxv.v.xi-p10"></span>**7** With which the mower hath not
filled his hand, Nor his bosom he who gathereth handfuls.

<span id="xxxv.v.xi-p11"></span>**8** Nor have they said who pass by,
“The blessing of Jehovah *be* upon you, “We bless you in the name of
Jehovah.”

<span id="xxxv.v.xii"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.xii-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.xii-p2"></span>PSALM 130

<span id="xxxv.v.xii-p3"></span>A Song of Degrees

<span id="xxxv.v.xii-p4"></span>**1** Out of the depths have I cried to
thee, O Jehovah!

<span id="xxxv.v.xii-p5"></span>**2** O Lord! hear my voice; Let thy
ears be attentive to the voice of my prayers.

<span id="xxxv.v.xii-p6"></span>**3** If iniquities thou shouldest mark,
O God! O Lord! who shall stand?

<span id="xxxv.v.xii-p7"></span>**4** For with thee is forgiveness that
thou mayest be feared.

<span id="xxxv.v.xii-p8"></span>**5** I have waited for Jehovah, waited
hath my soul; And in his word have I hoped.

<span id="xxxv.v.xii-p9"></span>**6** My soul \[*hath waited*\] for the
Lord Before the watchers of the morning, the watchers of the morning.

<span id="xxxv.v.xii-p10"></span>**7** But  <span
id="fr_394"></span>[395](#fn_394) hope let Israel in Jehovah; For with
Jehovah *there is* mercy, And with him there is plenteous redemption.

<span id="xxxv.v.xii-p12"></span>**8** And he shall redeem Israel from
all his iniquities.

<span id="xxxv.v.xiii"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.xiii-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.xiii-p2"></span>PSALM 131

<span id="xxxv.v.xiii-p3"></span>A Song of Degrees. Of David

<span id="xxxv.v.xiii-p4"></span>**1** O Jehovah! my heart hath not been
elated, Nor lifted up have been my eyes, Nor have I exercised myself in
great matters, Or in things hidden from me.

<span id="xxxv.v.xiii-p5"></span>**2** If I have not framed \[*or set*\]
and quieted my soul, Like one that is weaned from his mother, —  <span
id="fr_395"></span>[396](#fn_395) Like a child that is weaned is my soul
upon me.

<span id="xxxv.v.xiii-p7"></span>**3** Hope shall Israel in Jehovah From
henceforth, and for ever.

<span id="xxxv.v.xiv"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.xiv-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.xiv-p2"></span>PSALM 132

<span id="xxxv.v.xiv-p3"></span>A Song of Degrees

<span id="xxxv.v.xiv-p4"></span>**1** Remember, O Jehovah! David With
all his affliction:

<span id="xxxv.v.xiv-p5"></span>**2** Who sware to Jehovah, \[*Who*\]
vowed to the Mighty One of Jacob:

<span id="xxxv.v.xiv-p6"></span>**3** “If I shall enter into the
tabernacle of my house, “If I shall go up upon the covering of my bed,

<span id="xxxv.v.xiv-p7"></span>**4** “If I give sleep to my eyes, “To
my eyelids slumber,

<span id="xxxv.v.xiv-p8"></span>**5** “Until I find a place for Jehovah,
“Habitations for the mighty God of Jacob,” —  <span
id="fr_396"></span>[397](#fn_396)

<span id="xxxv.v.xiv-p10"></span>**6** Lo! we heard of it at Ephratha;
We found it in the fields of the wood.

<span id="xxxv.v.xiv-p11"></span>**7** We will enter into his
habitations, We will worship at his footstool.

<span id="xxxv.v.xiv-p12"></span>**8** Arise, O Jehovah! into thy rest,
Thou and the ark of thy strength.

<span id="xxxv.v.xiv-p13"></span>**9** Let thy priests be clothed with
righteousness, And let thy meek ones exult.

<span id="xxxv.v.xiv-p14"></span>**10** For the sake of David thy
servant Turn not away the face of thy Christ.

<span id="xxxv.v.xiv-p15"></span>**11** Sworn hath Jehovah to David in
truth, Nor will he turn from it: “Of the fruit of thy belly will I set
upon thy throne.

<span id="xxxv.v.xiv-p16"></span>**12** “If thy children shall keep my
covenant, “And my testimonies, which I will teach them; “Also their
children for ever shall sit upon thy throne.”

<span id="xxxv.v.xiv-p17"></span>**13** For chosen hath Jehovah Zion; He
hath desired her for a habitation to himself.

<span id="xxxv.v.xiv-p18"></span>**14** “This is my rest for ever; “Here
will I dwell, because I have loved her.

<span id="xxxv.v.xiv-p19"></span>**15** “Her provision blessing I will
bless;” Her poor I will satisfy with bread.

<span id="xxxv.v.xiv-p20"></span>**16** “And her priests I will clothe
with salvation; “And her merciful ones with exultation shall exult.

<span id="xxxv.v.xiv-p21"></span>**17** “There will I make to bud the
horn of David: “I have prepared a lamp for my Christ.

<span id="xxxv.v.xiv-p22"></span>**18** “His enemies will I clothe with
shame, “And upon him flourish shall his crown.”

<span id="xxxv.v.xv"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.xv-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.xv-p2"></span>PSALM 133

<span id="xxxv.v.xv-p3"></span>A Song of Degrees. Of David

<span id="xxxv.v.xv-p4"></span>**1** Behold! how good, and how becoming,
That brethren should even dwell together!

<span id="xxxv.v.xv-p5"></span>**2** Like the precious oil upon the
head, Which descendeth  <span id="fr_397"></span>[398](#fn_397) upon the
beard, the beard of Aaron, Which descendeth upon the skirt of his
garments.

<span id="xxxv.v.xv-p7"></span>**3** Like the dew of Hermon, Which
descendeth upon the mountains of Zion: For there commanded hath Jehovah
the blessing, Life for evermore.

<span id="xxxv.v.xvi"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.xvi-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.xvi-p2"></span>PSALM 134

<span id="xxxv.v.xvi-p3"></span>A Song of Degrees

<span id="xxxv.v.xvi-p4"></span>**1** Behold! bless ye Jehovah, All ye
servants of Jehovah! Who stand in the house of Jehovah nightly.

<span id="xxxv.v.xvi-p5"></span>**2** Lift up your hands to the
sanctuary, And bless ye Jehovah.

<span id="xxxv.v.xvi-p6"></span>**3** May Jehovah bless thee out of
Zion, \[*Even he*\] who hath made heaven and earth.

<span id="xxxv.v.xvii"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.xvii-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.xvii-p2"></span>PSALM 135

<span id="xxxv.v.xvii-p3"></span>Hallelujah

<span id="xxxv.v.xvii-p4"></span>**1** Praise ye the name of Jehovah;
Praise \[*it*\] O ye servants of Jehovah!

<span id="xxxv.v.xvii-p5"></span>**2** Who stand in the house of
Jehovah, \[*And ye who stand*\] in the courts of the house of our God.

<span id="xxxv.v.xvii-p6"></span>**3** Praise God; for good *is*
Jehovah: Sing to his name; for it is pleasant:

<span id="xxxv.v.xvii-p7"></span>**4** For God hath chosen Jacob to
himself, Israel for his own possession.

<span id="xxxv.v.xvii-p8"></span>**5** For I know that great is Jehovah,
And *that* our God is above all gods.

<span id="xxxv.v.xvii-p9"></span>**6** All things which Jehovah
pleaseth, lie doeth in the heavens and on the earth, In the sea and in
all the deeps.

<span id="xxxv.v.xvii-p10"></span>**7** Causing the clouds to ascend
from the end of the earth: The lightnings for the rain he maketh,
Bringing forth the wind out of his secret places.

<span id="xxxv.v.xvii-p11"></span>**8** He smote the first born of
Egypt, From man even unto beast.

<span id="xxxv.v.xvii-p12"></span>**9** He sent signs and wonders in the
midst of thee, O Egypt! On Pharaoh and on all his servants.

<span id="xxxv.v.xvii-p13"></span>**10** He smote great nations, And
slew mighty kings.

<span id="xxxv.v.xvii-p14"></span>**11** Sihon, king of the Amorites,
And Og the king of Basham, And all the kingdoms of Canaan.

<span id="xxxv.v.xvii-p15"></span>**12** And gave their land for an
heritage, An heritage to Israel, his people.

<span id="xxxv.v.xvii-p16"></span>**13** O Jehovah! thy name *is* for
ever; O Jehovah! thy memorial *is* from generation to generation.

<span id="xxxv.v.xvii-p17"></span>**14** For judge will Jehovah his
people, And concerning his servants he will repent himself.

<span id="xxxv.v.xvii-p18"></span>**15** The images of the nations *are*
silver and gold, The work of the hands of man.

<span id="xxxv.v.xvii-p19"></span>**16** A mouth have they, and they
will not speak;  <span id="fr_398"></span>[399](#fn_398) Eyes have they,
and they will not see.

<span id="xxxv.v.xvii-p21"></span>**17** Ears have they, and they will
not hear: Also, there is no breath in their mouth.

<span id="xxxv.v.xvii-p22"></span>**18** Like unto them are those who
make them, *And* every one who trusteth in them.

<span id="xxxv.v.xvii-p23"></span>**19** O house of Israel! bless ye
Jehovah; O house of Aaron! bless ye Jehovah;

<span id="xxxv.v.xvii-p24"></span>**20** O house of Levi! bless ye
Jehovah; O ye who fear Jehovah! bless ye Jehovah.

<span id="xxxv.v.xvii-p25"></span>**21** Blessed *be* Jehovah out of
Zion, Who dwelleth at Jerusalem. Hallelujah.

<span id="xxxv.v.xviii"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.xviii-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.xviii-p2"></span>PSALM 136

<span id="xxxv.v.xviii-p3"></span>**1** Praise Jehovah, for *he is*
good, For to everlasting *endureth* his mercy.

<span id="xxxv.v.xviii-p4"></span>**2** Praise the God of gods, For to
everlasting *endureth* his mercy.

<span id="xxxv.v.xviii-p5"></span>**3** Praise the Lord of lords, For to
everlasting *endureth* his mercy.

<span id="xxxv.v.xviii-p6"></span>**4** Who hath done wonders great
alone, For to everlasting *endureth* his mercy.

<span id="xxxv.v.xviii-p7"></span>**5** Who hath made the heavens in
wisdom, For to everlasting *endureth* his mercy.

<span id="xxxv.v.xviii-p8"></span>**6** Who hath stretched out the earth
above the waters, For to everlasting *endureth* his mercy.

<span id="xxxv.v.xviii-p9"></span>**7** Who hath made the great lights,
For to everlasting *endureth* his mercy.

<span id="xxxv.v.xviii-p10"></span>**8** The sun for rule by day, For to
everlasting *endureth* his mercy.

<span id="xxxv.v.xviii-p11"></span>**9** The moon and stars for rule by
night, For to everlasting *endureth* his mercy.

<span id="xxxv.v.xviii-p12"></span>**10** Who smote the Egyptians in
their first born, For to everlasting *endureth* his mercy.

<span id="xxxv.v.xviii-p13"></span>**11** And brought out Israel from
the midst of them, For to everlasting *endureth* his mercy.

<span id="xxxv.v.xviii-p14"></span>**12** With a hand of strength and an
arm stretched out, For to everlasting *endureth* his mercy.

<span id="xxxv.v.xviii-p15"></span>**13** Who divided the Red Sea into
divisions, For to everlasting *endureth* his mercy.

<span id="xxxv.v.xviii-p16"></span>**14** And made Israel to pass
through the midst of it, For to everlasting *endureth* his mercy.

<span id="xxxv.v.xviii-p17"></span>**15** And cast Pharaoh and his host
headlong into the Red Sea, For to everlasting *endureth* his mercy.

<span id="xxxv.v.xviii-p18"></span>**16** And led his people through the
wilderness, For to everlasting *endureth* his mercy.

<span id="xxxv.v.xviii-p19"></span>**17** Who smote great kings, For to
everlasting *endureth* his mercy.

<span id="xxxv.v.xviii-p20"></span>**18** And slew renowned kings, For
to everlasting *endureth* his mercy.

<span id="xxxv.v.xviii-p21"></span>**19** Sihon, king of the Arnorites,
For to everlasting *endureth* his mercy.

<span id="xxxv.v.xviii-p22"></span>**20** And Og, the king of Bashan,
For to everlasting *endureth* his mercy.

<span id="xxxv.v.xviii-p23"></span>**21** And gave their land for an
heritage, For to everlasting *endureth* his mercy.

<span id="xxxv.v.xviii-p24"></span>**22** An heritage to Israel his
servant, For to everlasting *endureth* his mercy.

<span id="xxxv.v.xviii-p25"></span>**23** Who in our humiliation
remembered us, For to everlasting *endureth* his mercy.

<span id="xxxv.v.xviii-p26"></span>**24** And rescued us from our
oppressors, For to everlasting *endureth* his mercy.

<span id="xxxv.v.xviii-p27"></span>**25** Who giveth food to all flesh,
For to everlasting *endureth* his mercy.

<span id="xxxv.v.xviii-p28"></span>**26** Make acknowledgments to the
God of heavens, For to everlasting *endureth* his mercy.

<span id="xxxv.v.xix"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.xix-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.xix-p2"></span>PSALM 137

<span id="xxxv.v.xix-p3"></span>**1** By the rivers of Babylon, there we
sat down, Yea we wept when we remembered thee, O Zion!

<span id="xxxv.v.xix-p4"></span>**2** Upon the willows, in the midst
thereof, We hanged our harps.

<span id="xxxv.v.xix-p5"></span>**3** Then they required of us, they who
carried us away captive, the words of a song, And, when we were in
suspense, mirth, \[*Saying*\] Sing us one of the songs of Zion.”

<span id="xxxv.v.xix-p6"></span>**4** How shall we sing the song of
Jehovah, In a strange land?

<span id="xxxv.v.xix-p7"></span>**5** If I shall forget thee, O
Jerusalem! Forget let my right hand \[*its cunning*.\]

<span id="xxxv.v.xix-p8"></span>**6** Cleave let my tongue to my palate,
If I do not remember thee, If I do not raise Jerusalem above my highest
joy.  <span id="fr_399"></span>[400](#fn_399)

<span id="xxxv.v.xix-p10"></span>**7** Remember, O Jehovah! the children
of Edom in the day of Jerusalem: ‘Who said, “Lay it bare — “Lay it bare,
even to the foundations thereof.”

<span id="xxxv.v.xix-p11"></span>**8** O daughter of Babylon laid waste!
Happy he who shall repay thee The retribution with which thou hast
retributed us!

<span id="xxxv.v.xix-p12"></span>**9** Happy he who shall take And dash
thy little ones against the stones.

<span id="xxxv.v.xx"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.xx-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.xx-p2"></span>PSALM 138

<span id="xxxv.v.xx-p3"></span>Of David

<span id="xxxv.v.xx-p4"></span>**1** I will celebrate thee with my whole
heart; Before the gods! will sing psalms to thee.

<span id="xxxv.v.xx-p5"></span>**2** I will worship *thee* towards the
temple of thy holiness, And sing to thy name for thy mercy and for thy
truth; For thou hast magnified above all *things* thy name by thy word.

<span id="xxxv.v.xx-p6"></span>**3** In the day *when*, I cried *to
thee*, then thou heardest me, Thou didst abundantly minister to me
strength in my soul.

<span id="xxxv.v.xx-p7"></span>**4** Celebrate thee, O Jehovah! let all
the kings of the earth; For they have heard the words of thy mouth.

<span id="xxxv.v.xx-p8"></span>**5** And let them sing in the ways of
Jehovah, For great is the glory of Jehovah.

<span id="xxxv.v.xx-p9"></span>**6** For high *is* Jehovah; yet the
lowly he will regard; And being high will know afar off:

<span id="xxxv.v.xx-p10"></span>**7** If I shall walk in the midst of
trouble, thou wilt revive me; Against the wrath of my enemies thou wilt
put forth thy hand, And save me shall thy right hand.

<span id="xxxv.v.xx-p11"></span>**8** Jehovah will perform in me *his
work*, O Jehovah! thy mercy is from everlasting; The works of thy hands
thou wilt not forsake.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxi"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.xxi-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.xxi-p2"></span>PSALM 139

<span id="xxxv.v.xxi-p3"></span>To the Chief Musician. A Psalm of David

<span id="xxxv.v.xxi-p4"></span>**1** O Jehovah! thou hast searched me
and known *me*

<span id="xxxv.v.xxi-p5"></span>**2** Thou hast known my down sitting
and my uprising, Thou understandest my thought afar off.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxi-p6"></span>**3** My path and my lying down thou
besiegest, And with all my ways thou art acquainted.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxi-p7"></span>**4** For there is not a word in my
tongue \[*But*\] lo! O God! thou knowest it altogether.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxi-p8"></span>**5** Behind and before thou hast shut
me up, And hast laid upon me thy hand.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxi-p9"></span>**6** Wonderful is *thy* knowledge above
me; It is high, I cannot *attain* to it.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxi-p10"></span>**7** Whither shall I go from thy
Spirit? And whither from thy time shall I flee?

<span id="xxxv.v.xxi-p11"></span>**8** If I ascend up into the heavens,
there thou art; If I lie down  <span id="fr_400"></span>[401](#fn_400)
in the sepulcher, behold! thou \[*art there*.\]

<span id="xxxv.v.xxi-p13"></span>**9** Should I take the wings of the
morning, That I may dwell in the uttermost parts of the sea,

<span id="xxxv.v.xxi-p14"></span>**10** Even there thy hand shall lead
me, And hold me shall thy right hand.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxi-p15"></span>**11** If I should say: “At least the
darkness shall cover me; ” “And the night shall be light for me;“

<span id="xxxv.v.xxi-p16"></span>**12** Even the darkness shall not hide
from the And the night as the day shall shine, And the darkness as the
light.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxi-p17"></span>**13** For thou hast possessed my
reins; Thou hast covered me in the womb of my mother.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxi-p18"></span>**14** I will celebrate thee; for I
have been fearfully and wonderfully made:  <span
id="fr_401"></span>[402](#fn_401) Marvelous are thy works, And my soul
shall know them full well.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxi-p20"></span>**15** Not hidden is my strength from
thee, Which thou hast made in secret: I was woven together in the lowest
parts of the earth.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxi-p21"></span>**16** My shapelessness see did thine
eyes;  <span id="fr_402"></span>[403](#fn_402) In thy book all shall be
written; They were formed *in many* days, And *there was* not one of
them.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxi-p23"></span>**17** And towards me how precious are
thy thoughts, O God! How great *are* the sums of them!

<span id="xxxv.v.xxi-p24"></span>**18** If I should count them; above
the sand they shall be multiplied: I am awakened, and still I am with
thee.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxi-p25"></span>**19** If thou shalt slay, O God! the
wicked, Then ye men of bloods depart from me.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxi-p26"></span>**20** Who have spoken of thee
wickedly: Taken thy name falsely have thy adversaries.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxi-p27"></span>**21** Thy haters, O Jehovah! shall not
I hate? And with those that rise up against thee shall I not strive?

<span id="xxxv.v.xxi-p28"></span>**22** With perfect hatred I have hated
them, As my enemies I have held them.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxi-p29"></span>**23** Search me, O God! and know my
heart: Examine me and know my thoughts.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxi-p30"></span>**24** And know whether the way of
wickedness be in me, And lead me in the way of this life.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxii"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.xxii-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.xxii-p2"></span>PSALM 140

<span id="xxxv.v.xxii-p3"></span>To the Chief Musician. A Psalm of David

<span id="xxxv.v.xxii-p4"></span>**1** Deliver me, O Jehovah! from the
evil man: From the man of injuries do thou preserve me.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxii-p5"></span>**2** Who devise mischiefs in *their*
heart; Daily do they congregate for wars.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxii-p6"></span>**3** Sharpened have they their tongue
like a serpent: The poison of an asp is under their lips. Selah.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxii-p7"></span>**4** Keep me, O Jehovah! from the
hands of the ungodly: From the man of injuries preserve me; Who plot to
overthrow my goings.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxii-p8"></span>**5** Laid have the proud a snare for
me: And with cords they have spread a net: By the wayside traps have
they set for me. Selah.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxii-p9"></span>**6** I said, O Jehovah! my God are
thou: Listen, O Jehovah! to the voice of my supplication.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxii-p10"></span>**7** O Jehovah, my Lord! the strength
of my salvation, Thou hast put a covering on my head in the day of arms.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxii-p11"></span>**8** Grant not, O Jehovah! the
desires of the ungodly man: They have devised, consummate thou not, they
shall be exalted. Selah.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxii-p12"></span>**9** \[*As for*\] the head of those
who encompass me, Let the mischief of his lips cover him.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxii-p13"></span>**10** Fall upon them let coals with
fire: He shall cast them into deep pits, They shall not rise again.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxii-p14"></span>**11** The man of tongue shall not be
established in the earth: The man of violence, evil shall hunt him to
banishments.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxii-p15"></span>**12** I have known that accomplish
will Jehovah the judgment of the poor one, The judgment of the afflicted
one.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxii-p16"></span>**13** Surely the righteous ones will
celebrate thy name, Dwell shall the upright ones before thy face.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxiii"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.xxiii-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.xxiii-p2"></span>PSALM 141

<span id="xxxv.v.xxiii-p3"></span>A Psalm of David

<span id="xxxv.v.xxiii-p4"></span>**1** O Jehovah! I have cried to thee:
Haste thou to me: Listen to my voice when I cry to thee.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxiii-p5"></span>**2** Directed let my prayer be as
incense before thy face: \[*Let*\] the lifting up of my hands \[*be*\]
as the sacrifice of the evening.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxiii-p6"></span>**3** Set, O Jehovah! a watch to my
mouth; Keep a guard upon the door of my lips.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxiii-p7"></span>**4** Incline not my heart to an evil
thing, To commit works of ungodliness with the men who work iniquity;
And let me not eat of their dainties.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxiii-p8"></span>**5** Smite me let the righteous man,
\[*it shall be*\] a kindness; And let him chastise me, \[*it shall be*\]
an oil that is precious, It shall not break my head: For yet also my
prayer *shall be* in their calamities.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxiii-p9"></span>**6** Cast down on stony places have
been their judges: And they shall hear my words, for they are sweet.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxiii-p10"></span>**7** As he who breaketh and cutteth
on the earth, Scattered have been our bones at the mouth of the grave.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxiii-p11"></span>**8** Because to thee, O Jehovah! my
Lord! *are* my eyes, In thee I have hoped: do not leave destitute my
soul.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxiii-p12"></span>**9** Keep me from the hands of the
snare which they have spread for me. From the nets of those who work
iniquity.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxiii-p13"></span>**10** Fall into his nets let the
ungodly ones together, Until I escape.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxiv"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.xxiv-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.xxiv-p2"></span>PSALM 142

<span id="xxxv.v.xxiv-p3"></span>Maschil of David, when he was in the
cave. A Prayer

<span id="xxxv.v.xxiv-p4"></span>**1** With my voice to, Jehovah I
cried; With my voice to. Jehovah I made supplication.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxiv-p5"></span>**2** I poured out before his face my
meditation; My affliction before his face I declare.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxiv-p6"></span>**3** When perplexed within me was my
spirit, And thou knewest my path: In the way wherein I walked, they laid
a snare for me.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxiv-p7"></span>**4** On looking to the right hand, and
beholding, None there was who would know me, Perish did refuge from me,
\[*There was*\] no man seeking after my soul.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxiv-p8"></span>**5** I cried to thee, O Jehovah! I
said, Thou *art* my hope, My portion in the land of the living.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxiv-p9"></span>**6** Attend to my cry, For under
affliction I labor exceedingly: Deliver me from my persecutors, For they
are too strong for me.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxiv-p10"></span>**7** Rescue from prison my soul, That
I may celebrate thy name: Crown me shall the righteous ones, For thou
shalt recompense me.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxv"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.xxv-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.xxv-p2"></span>PSALM 143

<span id="xxxv.v.xxv-p3"></span>A Psalm of David

<span id="xxxv.v.xxv-p4"></span>**1** O Jehovah! hear my prayer; Give
ear to my supplication; In thy truth answer me, in thy righteousness.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxv-p5"></span>**2** And enter not into judgment with
thy servant, For there shall not be justified in thy sight any living
man.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxv-p6"></span>**3** For persecuted hath the enemy my
soul; He hath prostrated on the earth my life; He hath set me in dark
*places*, as the dead of an age.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxv-p7"></span>**4** And perplexed within me is my
spirit Within me astonished is my heart.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxv-p8"></span>**5** I remembered the days of old, I
meditated on all thy doings; Upon the work of thy hands I meditated.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxv-p9"></span>**6** I spread out my hearts to thee; My
soul, as the earth without water, *is* to thee. Selah.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxv-p10"></span>**7** Hasten, answer me, O Jehovah!
Fail doth my spirit: Hide not thy face from me, Because I shall be like
to those who descend into the pit.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxv-p11"></span>**8** Cause me to hear in the morning
thy mercy, For in thee have I hoped: Show me the way in which I may
walk, For to thee have I lifted up my soul.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxv-p12"></span>**9** Deliver me from my enemies, O
Jehovah! With thee have I hidden \[*myself*.\]

<span id="xxxv.v.xxv-p13"></span>**10** Teach me to do thy will, For
thou *art* my God: Let thy good Spirit lead me into the right land.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxv-p14"></span>**11** Because of thy name, O Jehovah I
thou wilt quicken me: In thy righteousness bring out of trouble my soul.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxv-p15"></span>**12** And in thy mercy thou wilt
scatter my enemies, And wilt destroy all those who afflict my soul;
Because I *am* thy servant.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxvi"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.xxvi-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.xxvi-p2"></span>PSALM 144

<span id="xxxv.v.xxvi-p3"></span>Of David

<span id="xxxv.v.xxvi-p4"></span>**1** Blessed *be* Jehovah, my
strength, Who teacheth my hands for the fight, My fingers for the
battle.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxvi-p5"></span>**2** My goodness, and my fortress, My
citadel, my deliverer for me, My shield, and in him I have hoped, Who
subdueth my people under me.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxvi-p6"></span>**3** O Jehovah! what is man that thou
acknowledgest him? The son of man that thou thinkest of him?

<span id="xxxv.v.xxvi-p7"></span>**4** Man to vanity is like, His days
\[*are*\] as a shadow that is passing.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxvi-p8"></span>**5** O Jehovah! bow thy heavens and
descend: Touch the mountains and they shall smoke.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxvi-p9"></span>**6** Thunder forth thunderings and
scatter them; Shoot out thy arrows, and destroy them.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxvi-p10"></span>**7** Send thy hand from on high;
Rescue me and deliver me from waters great, From the hand of the sons of
the alien.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxvi-p11"></span>**8** For their mouth hath spoken
falsehood, And their right hand is a right hand of deceit.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxvi-p12"></span>**9** O God! a song that is new I will
sing to thee: Upon the nablum, upon the psaltery I will sing psalms to
thee

<span id="xxxv.v.xxvi-p13"></span>**10** Who givest salvation to kings,
Who redeemest David his servant from the hurtful sword.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxvi-p14"></span>**11** Redeem me, and rescue me, From
the hand of the sons of the alien, Whose mouth hath spoken falsehood,
And their right hand *is* a right hand of deceit.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxvi-p15"></span>**12** Because our sons *are* as
plants Which have grown up in their youth; Our daughters as corners
polished After the similitude of a palace.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxvi-p16"></span>**13** Our recesses full, Supplying
all kinds of good things. Our sheep bringing forth thousands, \[*Yea*\]
ten thousands in our streets.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxvi-p17"></span>**14** Our oxen to the burden
accustomed; No breach, nor going out, Nor cry in our streets.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxvi-p18"></span>**15** Happy the people to whom it is
so, To whom Jehovah is their God.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxvii"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.xxvii-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.xxvii-p2"></span>PSALM 145

<span id="xxxv.v.xxvii-p3"></span>Praise of David

<span id="xxxv.v.xxvii-p4"></span>**1** I will exalt thee, my God, *my*
King! And will bless thy name for ever and ever.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxvii-p5"></span>**2** Every day will I bless thee, And
praise thy name for ever and ever.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxvii-p6"></span>**3** Great *is* Jehovah, and to be
praised greatly, And his greatness is incomprehensible.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxvii-p7"></span>**4** Generation to generation shall
praise thy works, And thy power they shall declare.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxvii-p8"></span>**5** Upon the majesty of the glory of
thy excellence, And upon the words of thy wonders, I will meditate.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxvii-p9"></span>**6** And the might of thy terrible
*works* shall they recount; And thy greatness I will declare.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxvii-p10"></span>**7** The memory of the greatness of
thy goodness they shall speak forth; And of thy righteousness they shall
sing.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxvii-p11"></span>**8** Gracious and compassionate *is*
Jehovah, Slow to anger and great in clemency.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxvii-p12"></span>**9** Good *is* Jehovah to all, And
his compassions *are* over all his works.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxvii-p13"></span>**10** Celebrate thee, O Jehovah!
shall all thy works, And thy meek ones shall bless thee.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxvii-p14"></span>**11** Of the glory of thy kingdom
they shall tell, And of thy power they shall speak:

<span id="xxxv.v.xxvii-p15"></span>**12** To make known to the sons of
men his mighty acts, And the glory of the beauty of his kingdom.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxvii-p16"></span>**13** Thy kingdom *is* a kingdom of
all ages, And thy dominion is throughout generations of generations.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxvii-p17"></span>**14** Uphold doth Jehovah all the
falling, He raiseth up all who are bowed down.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxvii-p18"></span>**15** The eyes of all in thee do
hope, And thou givest them their food in its season.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxvii-p19"></span>**16** Thou openest thy hand And
satisfiest every living *creature* by thy good pleasure.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxvii-p20"></span>**17** Righteous *is* Jehovah in all
his ways, And merciful in all his works.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxvii-p21"></span>**18** Near *is* Jehovah to all who
call upon him, To all who call upon him in truth.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxvii-p22"></span>**19** The desire of those who fear
him he will perform, And their cry he will hear, told he will save
then,.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxvii-p23"></span>**20** Keep doth Jehovah all who love
him, And all the wicked he will destroy.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxvii-p24"></span>**21** The praise of Jehovah speak
shall my mouth: And bless shall all flesh his holy name for ever and
ever.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxviii"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.xxviii-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.xxviii-p2"></span>PSALM 146

<span id="xxxv.v.xxviii-p3"></span>Hallelujah

<span id="xxxv.v.xxviii-p4"></span>**1** Praise, O my soul! Jehovah.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxviii-p5"></span>**2** I will praise Jehovah in my
life; I will sing psalms to my God, while I have being.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxviii-p6"></span>**3** Confide not in princes, *Nor*
in the son of man, in whom there is not help.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxviii-p7"></span>**4** Go forth shall his breath, He
shall return to his earth, In that day perish shall his thoughts.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxviii-p8"></span>**5** Blessed *is* he who hath for
his help the God of Jacob; Whose hope is in Jehovah, his God:

<span id="xxxv.v.xxviii-p9"></span>**6** Who made heaven and earth, The
sea, and all that is in them: Who keepeth truth for ever:

<span id="xxxv.v.xxviii-p10"></span>**7** Who doeth judgment for those
who are unrighteously oppressed: Who giveth bread to the hungry: Jehovah
looseth the prisoners;

<span id="xxxv.v.xxviii-p11"></span>**8** Jehovah enlighteneth the
blind; Jehovah raiseth up those who are bowed down; Jehovah loveth the
righteous;

<span id="xxxv.v.xxviii-p12"></span>**9** Jehovah keepeth the strangers;
The orphan and the widow he succoureth; And the way of the ungodly he
will destroy.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxviii-p13"></span>**10** Reign shall Jehovah for ever:
Thy God, O Zion, *is* from generation to generation. Hallelujah.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxix"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.xxix-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.xxix-p2"></span>PSALM 147

<span id="xxxv.v.xxix-p3"></span>**1** Praise ye God; For it is a good
*thing* to sing psalms to our God, For *it is* pleasant, comely *is*
praise.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxix-p4"></span>**2** Build up Jerusalem doth Jehovah,
The dispersed of Israel he will gather.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxix-p5"></span>**3** He healeth the contrite in heart;
He bindeth their sorrows.  <span id="fr_403"></span>[404](#fn_403)

<span id="xxxv.v.xxix-p7"></span>**4** He counteth the multitude of the
stars: To each of them names doth he give.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxix-p8"></span>**5** Great is our Lord, and abundant
in power, His understanding is infinite.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxix-p9"></span>**6** Raise up the afflicted ones doth
Jehovah, He casteth down the ungodly ones to the ground.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxix-p10"></span>**7** Sing to Jehovah in praise, Sing
psalms to our God upon the harp.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxix-p11"></span>**8** Who covereth the heavens with
clouds, Who prepareth for the earth rain, Who maketh to spring up grass
upon the mountains,

<span id="xxxv.v.xxix-p12"></span>**9** Who giveth to the cattle their
food, To the young ones  <span id="fr_404"></span>[405](#fn_404) of the
ravens which cry to him.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxix-p15"></span>**10** Nor in the strength of the
horse will he take pleasure, Nor in the legs of man will he delight.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxix-p16"></span>**11** Delight doth Jehovah in those
who fear him, \[*In those*\] who hope in his mercy.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxix-p17"></span>**12** Celebrate, O Jerusalem!
Jehovah; Praise thy God, O Zion!

<span id="xxxv.v.xxix-p18"></span>**13** For he strengtheneth the bars
of thy gates; He blesseth thy children in the midst of thee.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxix-p19"></span>**14** Who maketh in thy borders
peace; With the fatness of wheat he satisfieth thee.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxix-p20"></span>**15** When he sendeth forth his word
upon the earth, Very swiftly run doth his word.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxix-p21"></span>**16** Who giveth snow *white* as
wool; The hoarfrost as ashes he scattereth.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxix-p22"></span>**17** He casteth forth his ice as
morsels: Before his cold who shall stand?

<span id="xxxv.v.xxix-p23"></span>**18** He shall send his word: red
shall melt them: Blow shall his breath, *and* flow shall the waters.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxix-p24"></span>**19** He announceth his words to
Jacob, his statutes and his judgments to Israel.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxix-p25"></span>**20** He hath not done so to every
nation, And his judgments he hath not made known to them. Hallelujah.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxx"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.xxx-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.xxx-p2"></span>PSALM 148

<span id="xxxv.v.xxx-p3"></span>Hallelujah

<span id="xxxv.v.xxx-p4"></span>**1** Praise ye Jehovah from the
heavens; Praise him in the heights.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxx-p5"></span>**2** Praise him, all ye his angels!
Praise him, all ye his armies!

<span id="xxxv.v.xxx-p6"></span>**3** Praise him, ye Sun and Moon!
Praise him, all ye shining stars!

<span id="xxxv.v.xxx-p7"></span>**4** Praise him, ye heavens of heavens!
And ye waters above the heavens!

<span id="xxxv.v.xxx-p8"></span>**5** Let them praise the name of
Jehovah; For he commanded and they were created:

<span id="xxxv.v.xxx-p9"></span>**6** And he established them for ever:
For ever he hath set for them a decree, and it shall not pass beyond.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxx-p10"></span>**7** Praise Jehovah, ye *creatures*
from the earth! Dragons, and all deeps!

<span id="xxxv.v.xxx-p11"></span>**8** Fire and hail, snow and ice! Wind
of storm, executing his word!

<span id="xxxv.v.xxx-p12"></span>**9** Mountains, and all hills! The
tree bearing fruit, and all cedars!

<span id="xxxv.v.xxx-p13"></span>**10** Wild beasts, and all cattle!
Reptile, and winged birds!

<span id="xxxv.v.xxx-p14"></span>**11** Kings of the earth, and all
peoples! Princes, and all judges of the earth!

<span id="xxxv.v.xxx-p15"></span>**12** Young men, and also maidens! Old
men with children!

<span id="xxxv.v.xxx-p16"></span>**13** Let them praise the name of
Jehovah; For high is his name alone; His praise is above the earth and
heavens.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxx-p17"></span>**14** And he hath exalted the horn of
his people: Praise *is* to all his merciful ones, To the children of
Israel, A people which is near to him. Hallelujah.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxxi"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.xxxi-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.xxxi-p2"></span>PSALM 149

<span id="xxxv.v.xxxi-p3"></span>Hallelujah

<span id="xxxv.v.xxxi-p4"></span>**1** Sing ye to Jehovah a song that is
new: His praise *is* in the assembly of the merciful ones.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxxi-p5"></span>**2** Rejoice let Israel in his Maker;
Let the children of Zion exult in their king:

<span id="xxxv.v.xxxi-p6"></span>**3** Let them praise his name on the
pipe: On the timbrel and the harp let them sing psalms to him.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxxi-p7"></span>**4** For taken pleasure hath Jehovah
in his people: He will glorify the poor ones unto salvation.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxxi-p8"></span>**5** Exult let the merciful ones in
glory; Let them shout with joy on their couches.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxxi-p9"></span>**6** The exaltations of God are in
their mouth, And a sword of two edges in their hand;

<span id="xxxv.v.xxxi-p10"></span>**7** To execute vengeance on the
heathen, Chastisements on the nations:

<span id="xxxv.v.xxxi-p11"></span>**8** To bind their kings with chains,
And their nobles with fetters of iron:

<span id="xxxv.v.xxxi-p12"></span>**9** To execute upon them the
judgment written. This honor is to all his merciful ones. Hallelujah.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxxii"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.xxxii-p1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.xxxii-p2"></span>PSALM 150

<span id="xxxv.v.xxxii-p3"></span>Hallelujah

<span id="xxxv.v.xxxii-p4"></span>**1** Praise God in his sanctuary;
Praise him in the firmament of his power.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxxii-p5"></span>**2** Praise him in his might; Praise
him for the multitude of his greatness:

<span id="xxxv.v.xxxii-p6"></span>**3** Praise him with sound of
trumpet; Praise him with nablum and harp.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxxii-p7"></span>**4** Praise him with timbrel and
pipe; Praise him with strings and organ.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxxii-p8"></span>**5** Praise him with cymbals of
sound; Praise him with cymbals of shouting.

<span id="xxxv.v.xxxii-p9"></span>6 Let every thing that breatheth
praise God. Hallelujah.

are set.”

<span id="fn_393"></span>[394](cc12034.htm#fr_393) <span
id="xxxv.v.vi-p10.1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.vi-p11"></span> “Is escaped.” — *Fr.*

<span id="fn_394"></span>[395](cc12034.htm#fr_394) <span
id="xxxv.v.xii-p10.1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.xii-p11"></span> This supplement is in the Latin
version but not in the French.

<span id="fn_395"></span>[396](cc12034.htm#fr_395) <span
id="xxxv.v.xiii-p5.1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.xiii-p6"></span> These two lines which are David’s oath
are in the abrupt form in which the Jews were accustomed to swear.

<span id="fn_396"></span>[397](cc12034.htm#fr_396) <span
id="xxxv.v.xiv-p8.1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.xiv-p9"></span> These two verses have also the abrupt
termination characteristic of the Jewish form of swearing.

<span id="fn_397"></span>[398](cc12034.htm#fr_397) <span
id="xxxv.v.xv-p5.1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.xv-p6"></span> “<span
id="xxxv.v.xv-p6.1"></span>Descendit.” — *Lat.* “<span
id="xxxv.v.xv-p6.2"></span>Descend.” — *Fr.*

<span id="fn_398"></span>[399](cc12034.htm#fr_398) <span
id="xxxv.v.xvii-p19.1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.xvii-p20"></span> In the French version the verb for
“speak” in this line; and the verbs for “see” and “hear” in the two next
lines, are in the present tense.

<span id="fn_399"></span>[400](cc12034.htm#fr_399) <span
id="xxxv.v.xix-p8.1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.xix-p9"></span> Literally, “above the head of my joy.”

<span id="fn_400"></span>[401](cc12034.htm#fr_400) <span
id="xxxv.v.xxi-p11.1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.xxi-p12"></span> “If I make my bed” — *Fr.*

<span id="fn_401"></span>[402](cc12034.htm#fr_401) <span
id="xxxv.v.xxi-p18.1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.xxi-p19"></span> Literally, “for terribly I have been
made wonderful.”

<span id="fn_402"></span>[403](cc12034.htm#fr_402) <span
id="xxxv.v.xxi-p21.1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.xxi-p22"></span> “Thine eyes did see me when I was yet
without form.” — *Fr.*

<span id="fn_403"></span>[404](cc12034.htm#fr_403) <span
id="xxxv.v.xxix-p5.1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.xxix-p6"></span> “Their wounds.” — *Fr.*

<span id="fn_404"></span>[405](cc12034.htm#fr_404) <span
id="xxxv.v.xxix-p12.1"></span>

<span id="xxxv.v.xxix-p13"></span> Literally, “to the sons.”
